## QOL-040.3 ŌĆö Deep-link node pre-activation via Stage 6.4 entry-hint extension (Epic Interaction)

**Status:** Build complete (awaiting Review). Issue #271, branch
`feat/QOL-040.3-deep-link-node-pre-activation-via-stage-6.4`.

**Doctrine highlights:**

- Pure routing refinement. The hint mechanism does not produce a verdict
  and does not consult heat, popularity, or engagement signals. Doctrine
  ┬¦1ŌĆō┬¦3 satisfied by construction.
- No AI moderator call. The new code paths in `App.tsx`,
  `ArgumentGameSurface.tsx`, and the two new pure-TS helpers
  (`buildDeepLinkEntryHint`, `deriveInitialActiveMessageId`) import no
  AI client. Doctrine ┬¦4 + ┬¦7 satisfied.
- The rules engine is untouched. Doctrine ┬¦5 satisfied.
- No new secret, no new env var. Doctrine ┬¦6 satisfied.
- No migration, no Edge Function, no RLS change. Soft-delete invariant
  honoured (the loader's `status === 'posted'` filter is the gate; the
  hint extension respects it). Doctrine ┬¦8 satisfied.
- No new user-facing copy. The notification-path hint sets
  `verbPhrase: ''`, which the room shell uses to suppress the
  micro-moment banner. Doctrine ┬¦9 satisfied.
- v1 scope guards: no voting, no realtime editing, no OAuth, no public
  API, no push notifications, no search. The card refines routing
  inside QOL-040's already-shipped notification list. Doctrine ┬¦10
  satisfied.

**Three-layer visibility composition (confirmed natural ŌĆö no new check):**

1. `room_notifications` SELECT RLS restricts to `recipient_id =
   auth.uid()`. The user only sees notifications addressed to them.
2. `useDebates()` loads only RLS-visible debates. `debates.find((d) =>
   d.id === link.debateId)` returns `undefined` for any room the user
   cannot see ŌåÆ `if (!target) return;` no-ops the callback.
3. `useArgumentRoomMessages` pulls only `status === 'posted'` rows for
   the debate. Soft-deleted / wrong-room / RLS-hidden arguments never
   reach `sorted`. One `sorted.find(...)` returning `undefined` covers
   every inaccessible case ŌåÆ fallback to `latestId`.

**Files added:**

- `src/features/debates/deepLinkEntryHint.ts` (~60 lines): pure-TS
  helper `buildDeepLinkEntryHint(link)` that builds the optional
  `GalleryEntryHint` from a `NotificationDeepLink`. Returns null when
  the link has no `activeArgumentId` (so the App.tsx caller passes null
  to `setEntryHint` and the room shell picks `latestId` as today). Zero
  React / Supabase / network / AI imports.
- `__tests__/notificationDeepLinkPreActivation.test.ts` (~250 lines,
  18 tests): room-consumer behaviour ŌĆö hint present + valid id, hint
  absent, hint references missing id (soft-deleted / wrong-room /
  RLS-hidden), empty slice, all existing GAL-002 fallback paths (root /
  first_open_challenge / latest), source-file safety, doctrine
  ban-list scan.
- `__tests__/notificationDeepLinkRouting.test.ts` (~120 lines, 7 tests):
  App.tsx hand-off ŌĆö `buildDeepLinkEntryHint` with id / null /
  empty-string, source-file safety, doctrine ban-list scan.

**Files modified:**

- `src/features/debates/conversationGalleryModel.ts`: appended optional
  `entryHintForArgumentId?: string` to the `GalleryEntryHint` interface
  with a JSDoc comment naming QOL-040.3 as the source. No change to
  `deriveGalleryEntryHint` ŌĆö the gallery deriver never sets this field.
- `App.tsx`: extended `handleOpenNotificationDeepLink` to call
  `buildDeepLinkEntryHint(link)` + `setEntryHint(...)` BEFORE
  `selectDebate(target, side)`. The reserved-field comment block is
  replaced by a ┬¦17-resolved comment naming QOL-040.3. Imports the new
  helper. Notifications module untouched.
- `src/features/arguments/argumentGameSurfaceModel.ts`: appended pure
  deriver `deriveInitialActiveMessageId(sorted, latestId, entryHint)`
  inside a bracketed `// ŌöĆŌöĆ QOL-040.3 ŌĆö Deep-link node pre-activation
  deriver` / `// ŌöĆŌöĆ End QOL-040.3 region` block. Type-only import of
  `GalleryEntryHint` (erased at compile time ŌåÆ no runtime cycle).
- `src/features/arguments/ArgumentGameSurface.tsx`: `initialActiveId`
  useMemo now delegates to the pure deriver. The dev-only
  `console.warn` for the rare fallback case (no PII; opaque ids only)
  lives in the React consumer; the pure deriver remains silent.
- `__tests__/galleryEntryHintModel.test.ts`: appended 2 tests covering
  the new optional field's type acceptance and the gallery deriver's
  no-set invariant.

**No changes to:**
- `src/features/notifications/*` (QOL-040 surface ŌĆö frozen).
- `src/features/invites/*` (QOL-038 surface ŌĆö frozen).
- `src/features/debates/roomVisibilityModel.ts` (QOL-039 ŌĆö frozen).
- `supabase/functions/room-notifications/*` (QOL-040 Edge Function ŌĆö
  frozen).
- `supabase/functions/submit-argument/*` (frozen).
- Any `.tsx` notification component, any other test, any migration, any
  Edge Function, any RLS, any `.env*`, any storage.

**Test delta:** 10452 ŌåÆ 10479 (+27 tests, +2 suites). Typecheck + lint
clean. No regressions.

**Operator follow-up:** none. Pure code change. No migration, no Edge
Function deploy, no Supabase write, no env change.

**Not in scope for this card** (see design ┬¦12):

- Realtime notification delivery (still polls on focus).
- Notification preferences (QOL-040.1, deferred).
- Native deep-link path (Expo Linking integration is a follow-up).
- Self-notification on the same-room case (the room does not re-focus
  on the hinted move when the user is already inside it; documented
  gap, deferred per design ┬¦8 case 8).
- `selectionStatus` enrichment (the existing `'entry_hint'` value
  covers the unmet-hint case adequately; no new union value).

## QOL-036.1 ŌĆö Composition-layer integration for payment-evidence pill state (Epic Evidence)

**Status:** Build complete (awaiting Review). Issue #270, branch
`feat/QOL-036.1-composition-layer-integration-for-paymen`.

**Doctrine highlights:**

- A pill chip flip is a STRUCTURAL indicator, never a standing reward.
  The deriver imports nothing from `pointStanding/`; emits no
  `PointStandingDelta`. Anti-amplification preserved.
- The deriver authors zero user-facing strings. All copy passes through
  unchanged from QOL-037's `summarizeApplicabilityChip` and EV-003's
  chip-rendering surface. No new chip, no new enum value.
- Pill visibility = artifact visibility. The deriver runs on the client
  over data the client already fetched via existing RLS; no new
  visibility surface, no new RLS rule.
- Observer-mode is backward-compatible by construction: empty mutation
  arrays ŌåÆ layer-1-only derivation, byte-identical to pre-QOL-036.1.
- Cross-layer conflict resolution: last-wins by `sourceMoveId.createdAt`;
  ties go to layer-1 (user-action signal is more deliberate); when
  chronology is unknown, layer-1 wins as a safe default. A more-advanced
  layer-1 obligation lifecycle (`accepted_by_both`) is NEVER regressed by
  a layer-2 `evidence_debt_resolved` mutation that would downgrade it.
- The four mutations map to TWO orthogonal axes (applicability +
  obligation). Cross-axis stacking is additive ŌĆö both chips can render
  together on a single payment artifact.

**Files added:**

- `src/features/evidence/paymentEvidencePillState.ts` (~530 lines):
  pure-TS deriver `derivePaymentEvidencePillState`, the
  `PaymentEvidencePillState` + `PaymentEvidencePillProvenance` types,
  the frozen `MUTATION_TO_PILL_STATE` four-row mapping, and the frozen
  `PILL_STATE_CONFLICT_RULE` constant. Zero React / Supabase / network
  / `pointStanding/` / AI imports.
- `__tests__/paymentEvidencePillState.test.ts` (~830 lines, 59 tests):
  mapping-table coverage, conflict-rule constant, four happy paths
  (the ┬¦5 mappings), layer-1-only regression, layer-1+layer-2
  corroboration, within-axis last-wins (debt resolved-later / earlier /
  tie-break, applicability disputed-later), cross-layer conflict
  (layer-2 newer / no map / exact tie), cross-axis orthogonality
  (dispute + debt-opened, corroboration + debt-resolved), observer-mode
  degradation, ┬¦8 edge cases 1ŌĆō15, doctrine ban-list (word-boundary
  match, non-comment source scan, enum-value scan, provenance scan),
  purity (no React / Supabase / Edge / pointStanding / AI / Date.now /
  console / service-role / Authorization), determinism (same input ŌåÆ
  deeply-equal output; argument-order independence).

**Files modified:**

- `src/features/evidence/index.ts`: appended QOL-036.1 type + value
  re-exports for the new module under a clearly commented block.
- `src/features/semanticReferee/compositionLayer.ts`: JSDoc-only
  annotations above each of the four COMP-001 rule branches (R-EV-01,
  R-EV-02, R-EV-APP-01, R-CAT-Corroborating) pointing back to QOL-036.1
  as the consumer. **No logic change.** 112/112 composition tests still
  passing.

**No changes to:**
- `src/features/evidence/evidenceModel.ts` (QOL-036 surface ŌĆö frozen).
- `src/features/evidence/evidenceApplicabilityModel.ts` (QOL-037 ŌĆö frozen).
- `src/features/evidence/evidenceDebtModel.ts` (EV-003 ŌĆö frozen).
- `src/features/semanticReferee/compositionTypes.ts` (COMP-001 ŌĆö frozen).
- `src/features/arguments/useSemanticReferee.ts` (COMP-001 hook ŌĆö frozen).
- Any `.tsx` component, any other test, any migration, any Edge Function,
  any RLS, any `.env*`, any storage.

**Test delta:** 10393 ŌåÆ 10452 (+59 tests, +1 suite). Typecheck + lint
clean. No regressions.

**Operator follow-up:** none. Pure code change. No migration, no Edge
Function deploy, no Supabase write, no env change.

**Not in scope for this card:** the room render layer's wiring of
`derivePaymentEvidencePillState` into `ArgumentGameSurface.tsx` is a
separate small card (or organic follow-up) once the deriver lands.
QOL-036.1 ships the pure model; consumers wire later (same pattern as
QOL-036 + the QOL-030 box wiring).

## QOL-039 ŌĆö Public Ōåö Private Room Visibility Transition Rules (Epic Interaction)

**Status:** Shipped ŌĆö PR #268 merged 2026-05-24 (squash `9e60310`). Adds the room visibility
field, the one-way `public ŌåÆ private` transition, the creator-only UI
gate (OD-1), the counts-only audit table (OD-2), and the
`record-visibility-transition` Edge Function (OD-3) that atomically
flips visibility, writes the audit row, and dispatches the QOL-040
notifications.

**Doctrine highlights:**

- Visibility is an access property of the room, NEVER a verdict. Making
  a room private is a structural transition, never a punishment.
- One-way: `public ŌåÆ private` only. The `BEFORE UPDATE OF visibility`
  trigger rejects any reverse attempt ŌĆö mods/admins are not exempted.
- The transition mutates ONE column on ONE `debates` row and ZERO
  `arguments` rows. "Retained (muted), never deleted" is met by
  definition; only the read audience shrinks.
- The audit table records COUNTS + chime-in ARGUMENT IDs only ŌĆö never
  individual dropped-observer user IDs (OD-2 privacy guard).
- The Edge Function is creator-only at the server layer to match
  QOL-040's `room_made_private` handler. The DB+RLS layer keeps the
  creator-or-mod permission as defense-in-depth.
- All copy is plain English, ban-list-clean (no winner/loser/true/false/
  correct/liar/booted/kicked/rejected (person)/unwanted (person)/shame/
  viral/trending). User-facing strings say "argument", not "debate"
  (QOL-035).
- Notification dispatch failures NEVER roll back the transition
  (mirrors the `submit-argument` side-effect pattern).

**Files added:**
- `supabase/migrations/20260524000015_qol_039_room_visibility.sql`
  (~280 lines): visibility column + one-way trigger + 2 SECURITY
  DEFINER helpers + 4 RLS policy replacements + audit table + 3
  SELECT policies + OPS-001 four-class compliance.
- `supabase/functions/record-visibility-transition/index.ts`
  (~350 lines): JWT-verified, creator-only, atomic UPDATE + audit
  INSERT + cross-function `room_made_private` + per-chime-in
  `chime_in_rejected` notification dispatch via `room-notifications`.
- `src/features/debates/roomVisibilityModel.ts` (~250 lines): pure-TS
  model with `canTransitionToPrivate`, `buildTransitionConsequences`,
  `summarizeRejectedChimeInBranches`, `RoomVisibilityChangeEvent`.
  Zero React / Supabase / network / AI imports.
- `src/features/debates/MakePrivateConfirmation.tsx` (~190 lines):
  neutral confirmation modal with the six effect bullets,
  count-aware chime-in copy variant, 44px targets, accessibilityRole +
  busy state.

**Files modified:**
- `src/features/debates/types.ts`: `visibility: RoomVisibility` on
  `Debate`; `visibility?: RoomVisibility` on `CreateDebateInput`.
- `src/features/debates/debatesApi.ts`: visibility threaded through
  list/create; `transitionRoomToPrivate` wrapper calls the Edge
  Function (NOT a direct UPDATE per OD-3).
- `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts`: frozen `ROOM_VISIBILITY_COPY`
  block + four plain-language reason codes. No verdict / shaming /
  popularity tokens.
- `src/features/debates/conversationGalleryModel.ts`: `visibility` on
  `ConversationGalleryCard`; `classifyCardToSection` routes private
  cards to `my_rooms` only.
- `src/features/debates/CreateDebateForm.tsx`: 2-option visibility
  segmented control (radiogroup, default 'public'); shape (check
  mark) + label weight carry selection beyond color.
- `src/features/debates/DebateDetailHeader.tsx`: creator-only
  make-private action + private-room badge + neutral inline error
  display.
- `src/features/debates/index.ts`: barrel re-exports for the new
  model symbols + `transitionRoomToPrivate`.
- `supabase/config.toml`: registers
  `[functions.record-visibility-transition] verify_jwt = true`.
- `docs/rls.md`: policy table rows updated for `debates`,
  `debate_participants`, `arguments`; new "Room visibility" section;
  `room_visibility_changes` policy row added.

**Test count:** 10163 ŌåÆ 10393 (+230 new tests). Suites: 400 ŌåÆ 414
(+14). Typecheck + lint clean.

**Operator follow-up to ship live:**
1. `npx supabase db push --linked` ŌĆö apply migration
   `20260524000015_qol_039_room_visibility.sql`. Adds the visibility
   column (backfilled to 'public' for every existing row), the
   one-way trigger, the two SECURITY DEFINER helpers, the four RLS
   policy replacements, and the audit table.
2. `npx supabase db lint` ŌĆö confirm the new policies + trigger +
   audit table lint clean.
3. `npx supabase functions deploy record-visibility-transition --linked` ŌĆö
   deploy the new Edge Function. QOL-040's `room-notifications` is
   unchanged; the cross-function call uses its existing contract.

No env var changes (the function reuses the service-role key
already in Supabase secrets). No dependency installs. No
modifications to any QOL-038 or QOL-040 file (per the design's E4
authority boundary).

See `docs/designs/QOL-039.md` (original + ┬¦E1-┬¦E4 operator decisions
enrichment) and `docs/designs/QOL-039-verification.md`.

## QOL-040 ŌĆö Invite & response notification lifecycle (Epic Interaction)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö adds the in-app
notification lifecycle for an argument room. Ten triggers cover
invite / new_response / concession_challenged / source_requested /
evidence_supplied / chime_in_posted / room_made_private /
chime_in_rejected / argument_settled / invite_accepted_by_invitee.
The eleventh trigger (`invite_expired_notice`) is intentionally
deferred per operator decision 2026-05-24 (E7.3).

**Doctrine highlights:**

- No verdict / truth / popularity language in any notification
  string (in-app + email body both pass the ban-list scan).
- The actor display name is gated by `meta.actorNameVisible` ŌĆö
  set false ŌåÆ copy says "Someone" (design ┬¦9 rule 3).
- `chime_in_rejected` copy describes the move's fit to the room,
  NEVER the person. No "rejected you", no rejecter name, no
  count framed as a verdict (design ┬¦9 rule 5 + Scenario 1
  Step 14).
- `argument_settled` says "settled", never "case closed" or any
  outcome verdict.
- No notification carries argument body text ŌĆö only the room
  title snapshot, plus a tiny `meta` JSONB for neutral nouns.
- RLS: SELECT own / UPDATE own (read_at-only via API wrapper) /
  NO INSERT or DELETE policy ŌĆö inserts are service-role-only
  inside `submit-argument` and `room-notifications` Edge
  Functions.
- Email scaffold (E1) is OFF by default in every environment.
  Returns `'not_configured'` until the operator flips
  `INVITE_EMAIL_ENABLED=true` + `RESEND_API_KEY` +
  `INVITE_EMAIL_FROM` as Edge Function secrets. Mirrors
  `request-argument-deletion`'s Resend pattern verbatim. No
  unsubscribe link in v1 (E1.2a ŌĆö deferred along with
  preferences).
- `InviteEmailStatus = 'sent' | 'not_configured' | 'queued'`
  matches QOL-038's existing `CreateRoomInviteResponse.notification`
  union exactly ŌĆö no new value, no QOL-038 client-code change.
- A notification-insert failure in `submit-argument` is
  swallowed (try/catch) ŌĆö a notification can NEVER block the
  argument post.

**Files added:**
- `supabase/migrations/20260524000014_qol_040_room_notifications.sql`
  (~170 lines): table + 2 RLS policies (SELECT own / UPDATE
  own). pgcrypto dependency documented in header per OPS-001
  ┬¦4 Class 4. Fully-qualified column references in policies
  per defensive discipline. Idempotency partial unique index
  on (recipient_id, type, argument_id) for argument-derived
  triggers.
- `supabase/functions/room-notifications/index.ts` (~600 lines):
  JWT-verified Edge Function for the six non-argument-derived
  triggers. Email scaffold (`maybeSendInviteEmail`) gated on
  INVITE_EMAIL_ENABLED.
- `src/features/notifications/notificationModel.ts` (~310 lines):
  pure-TS classifier + recipient resolver + copy builder +
  deep-link resolver. Zero React / Supabase / network imports.
- `src/features/notifications/notificationsApi.ts` (~120 lines):
  SELECT + read_at UPDATE wrappers only (no inserts; insert is
  Edge-Function-only).
- `src/features/notifications/NotificationListScreen.tsx`
  (~210 lines): loading / empty / error / populated states,
  "Mark all read" affordance, non-navigable confirmation card
  for revoked-access rows.
- `src/features/notifications/NotificationRow.tsx` (~180 lines):
  Ōēź44-px tap target, accessibilityRole="button" +
  accessibilityState (unread/read), glyph-driven type icon
  (shape carries meaning before color).
- `src/features/notifications/NotificationBadge.tsx` (~60 lines):
  unread count badge, hides at zero, caps at "9+".
- `src/features/notifications/useNotifications.ts` (~110 lines):
  load + mark-read hook. Always polls (no preference branch ŌĆö
  per E3.2 deferral).
- `src/features/notifications/notificationCopy.ts` (~40 lines):
  screen chrome (header / empty / error / mark-all-read).

**Files modified:**
- `supabase/functions/submit-argument/index.ts`: +~80 lines for
  the notification side-effect insert. Wrapped in try/catch;
  uses service-role only; classifies trigger inline mirroring
  notificationModel.classifyArgumentTrigger precedence
  (evidence > concession > source > new_response).
- `supabase/config.toml`: registers
  `[functions.room-notifications] verify_jwt = true`.
- `src/features/preferences/userPreferencesModel.ts`: JSDoc-only
  addition to `notificationsOptInStub` documenting the
  preferences deferral (E3.2). Field shape, default, copy
  unchanged.
- `App.tsx`: mounts `NotificationBadge` on the Arguments tab
  label; adds a "Notifications" trigger in the gallery toolbar;
  renders `NotificationListScreen` as an in-tab sub-screen when
  open; routes a tapped notification to the target debate via
  `selectDebate` (the active-node deep-link is a ┬¦17 follow-up;
  the existing Stage 6.4 entry-hint mechanism does not yet
  take an explicit argument id).

**Test count:** 9976 ŌåÆ 10163 (+187 new tests). Suites: 383 ŌåÆ
400 (+17). Typecheck + lint clean.

**Operator follow-up to ship live notifications:**
1. `npx supabase db push --linked` ŌĆö apply the new migration.
2. `npx supabase functions deploy room-notifications --linked`
   ŌĆö deploy the new Edge Function.
3. `npx supabase functions deploy submit-argument --linked` ŌĆö
   re-deploy submit-argument (it gained the notification
   side-effect block).
4. Optional (email channel, off by default):
   `npx supabase secrets set INVITE_EMAIL_ENABLED=true --linked`
   `npx supabase secrets set RESEND_API_KEY=<key> --linked`
   `npx supabase secrets set INVITE_EMAIL_FROM='no-reply@<domain>' --linked`
   Only flip after deliverability setup (SPF, DKIM, bounce
   handling) is complete ŌĆö unsubscribe is part of that
   operator-infrastructure work, NOT QOL-040.

See `docs/designs/QOL-040.md` (original + E1-E7 enrichment +
E7 operator decisions) and `docs/designs/QOL-040-verification.md`.

## QOL-038 ŌĆö Invite ŌåÆ signup/auth ŌåÆ argument-room return path (Epic Interaction)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö closes Scenario 1's
"single largest gap": a person invited to a live conflict cannot
actually be brought into the right room. QOL-038 ships the invite data
model (`argument_room_invites` migration + RLS), the write path
(`manage-room-invite` Edge Function with five actions: create / revoke /
list_for_debate / lookup_by_token / accept), the auth deep link
(`/invite/<token>` route surviving signup and email-confirmation
round-trip via a persisted `pendingInviteIntent` session slice), and
seamless return entry (enrolling the invitee as a primary participant
BEFORE the room renders so Stage 6.4 seamless entry shows them the
primary view ŌĆö no observer/side modal). The card includes the ┬¦17
designer-pass enrichment for the soft-deleted-room edge case (a
`409 room_archived` error path in both lookup_by_token and accept, plus
a new `InviteRedeemGate` "Room archived" state).

**Doctrine highlights:**

- Raw invite token NEVER stored ŌĆö only `token_hash` (sha-256 hex) goes
  to the DB. The raw token appears only in the invite email link and in
  the inviter's create-time response (the inviter's own capability, not
  logged anywhere).
- Email-binding check (┬¦5.5 step 4) is the security spine: the
  signed-in user's verified email MUST equal the invited address or
  accept returns `403 invite_email_mismatch`. A forwarded link cannot
  be redeemed by whoever receives the forward.
- `verify_jwt = false` on the function is documented inline; every
  mutating action re-checks the JWT explicitly inside the handler. The
  only unauthenticated action (`lookup_by_token`) treats the token as
  the auth and returns the absolute minimal projection (title +
  display name, no email, no body).
- The invitee enters as a primary participant (affirmative or negative ŌĆö
  opposite of the room creator's side, defaulting to negative). The
  `debate_participants` insert is the only authoritative write of a
  user's seat; the (debate_id, user_id) PK makes accept idempotent for
  re-tap and for an already-member.
- No service-role in the client. No raw token in audit rows or logs
  (the audit payload carries `emailDomain` + `tokenIssued` bool only).
- Stage 6.4 observer-default consistency: the invitee bypass is a
  documented, narrowly-scoped exception ŌĆö not a global default change.
  The bypass is the `debate_participants` row insert that happens
  BEFORE `selectDebate` runs.
- Full doctrine ban-list scan over every exported invite string:
  zero `winner` / `loser` / `challenger` / `opponent` / `debate
  challenge` / `game invite` / verdict tokens. The post-QOL-035
  terminology refresh (verification doc ┬¦5) is closed.

**Files added:**

## OPS-001 ŌĆö Reviewer template strengthening for migration-bearing cards (Operations ┬Ę process)

**Status:** Shipped ŌĆö PR #262 merged 2026-05-24 (squash `2d91b5a`). Documentation-only update to `.claude/agents/roadmap-reviewer.md` adding a "Migration-bearing card verification (mandatory)" section that codifies the four-class verification template surfaced by the QOL-041 migration deploy chain.

**Doctrine highlights:**
- Reviewer template now requires either (a) `npx supabase db reset --linked=false` (when Docker is available) or (b) heightened textual review against four named issue classes.
- The four classes: (1) Ambiguous column references in RLS policy bodies (QOL-041 motivating example), (2) Column type mismatches, (3) Implicit ordering dependencies, (4) Function / trigger / extension dependencies.
- The template is process-only ŌĆö no production code, no migrations, no Edge Function changes.
- Doctrine ban-list applies to the policy text: zero verdict tokens in additions.

**Files added:** none.

**Files modified:**
- `.claude/agents/roadmap-reviewer.md` (~80 lines added): new mandatory section + four-class checklist.
- `CLAUDE.md`: one-line mention of the new template under "Supabase Conventions" + cross-reference.
- `docs/core/agent-charters.md`: cross-reference under "Common preflight".
- `docs/core/agent-workflow.md`: per-cell update to the agents-table reviewer-row Output cell.
- `docs/core/known-blockers.md`: new "QOL-041 Migration Deploy Chain ŌĆö Reviewer Template Strengthened (OPS-001)" entry preserving the QOL-041 lesson (Incident / Recovery / Template update paragraphs).

**Test count:** unchanged (process card; 9757 baseline preserved).

**Operator follow-up:** none ŌĆö process change effective on merge. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration.

See `docs/designs/OPS-001.md` and `docs/reviews/OPS-001.md`.

## QOL-041.2 ŌĆö In-place migration recovery for QOL-041 (doctrine-scoped exception ┬Ę Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Shipped ŌĆö PR #259 merged 2026-05-23 (squash `6fcfdbf`). Doctrine-scoped exception to the "never edit an applied migration" rule: rewrites the QOL-041 migration `20260522000012_qol_041_concession_acceptance.sql` in-place to fix the five `debate_id` column-ambiguity references at source, then deletes the QOL-041.1 fix-forward migration (which is no longer needed).

**Doctrine highlights:**
- Doctrine-scoped exception is explicitly tracked in `docs/core/known-blockers.md` "QOL-041 Migration Deploy Chain" entry. Factual basis at design time: `npx supabase migration list --linked` at 2026-05-23T22:54Z showed the Remote column for `20260522000012` empty (the original migration had never applied to the remote). Reviewer re-verified at review time the Remote column was still empty ŌĆö no race condition.
- The exception is one-time and explicitly does NOT modify the standard doctrine ("future migration-bearing cards continue to follow the standard never-edit-applied doctrine" ŌĆö verbatim in the recovery banner).
- OPS-001 (PR #262) codified the lesson learnt into the roadmap-reviewer template so future migration-bearing cards catch the column-ambiguity issue at review time, not at deploy time.

**Files modified:**
- `supabase/migrations/20260522000012_qol_041_concession_acceptance.sql`: prepended 30-line recovery comment banner (lines 1ŌĆō29) + five qualifier replacements inside policy WITH-CHECK subqueries (bare `debate_id` ŌåÆ `concession_items.debate_id` / `concession_acceptances.debate_id` / `move_reactions.debate_id`). Per-policy authz logic preserved byte-for-byte except qualifier disambiguation.

**Files deleted:**
- `supabase/migrations/20260523000001_qol_041_1_fix_concession_acceptances_policies.sql`: the QOL-041.1 fix-forward (129 lines), no longer needed.

**Test count:** unchanged (migration-only; 9757 baseline preserved).

**Operator follow-up to ship live:** For dev ŌĆö `npx supabase db reset --linked=false` re-applies migrations cleanly. For any environment that already applied QOL-041 + QOL-041.1 ad-hoc, manual drop + recreate of the four policies is the one-time recovery path documented in `docs/designs/QOL-041.2.md`.

See `docs/designs/QOL-041.2.md` and `docs/reviews/QOL-041.2.md`.

## QOL-041 ŌĆö Concession list + acceptance gradient + fist-bump reaction (Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö fills the deliberate hole
QOL-030 left in the `respond` and `respond_to_concession` box types
(QOL-030 ┬¦6.2 / ┬¦12 explicitly named "the concession-gradient internals
(QOL-041)" as a hole for this card to fill). Ships three structured
surfaces a concession exchange needs: (1) the itemized concession list
(the concession section of the `respond` box is now a forced list of
separately-addressable points, each its own row); (2) the per-concession
5-level acceptance gradient (the `respond_to_concession` box mirrors the
incoming concession set row-for-row; each row picks one of `agree` /
`agree_with_caveat` / `disagree_framing` / `disagree_context` /
`disagree_fact` with a clarification required whenever the level is not
`agree`); (3) the no-score fist-bump acknowledgment reaction (the ONE
allowed reaction in v1 because it carries no score, no verdict, no
standing change). Issue #210.

- **What it ships ŌĆö new pure-TS models (`src/features/concessions/`):**
  `acceptanceGradient.ts` (5-level `AcceptanceLevel` enum, the verbatim
  design ┬¦7.2 `ACCEPTANCE_LEVEL_COPY` plain-language map,
  `acceptanceRequiresClarification` predicate, the
  `ACCEPTANCE_TO_CONCESSION_EFFECT` vocabulary bridge to the shipped
  point-standing `ConcessionEffect` families); `concessionListModel.ts`
  (forced-list draft model ŌĆö cap 8 items / 600-char-per-item, validation
  with plain-language `firstReason`, payload builder); `respondToConcessionModel.ts`
  (mirrored forced-list ŌĆö buildRespondToConcessionDraft, setRowLevel /
  setRowClarification, `isPostable()` enforcing every-row-picked +
  every-non-agree-row-has-clarification, payload builder);
  `activeDisagreement.ts` (deterministic derivation ŌĆö `deriveActiveDisagreement`
  with `fact > context > framing` precedence + newest-argument-wins
  rule; `agree_with_caveat` is a rider, not a dispute); `moveReactionModel.ts`
  (`MoveReactionKind` with EXACTLY ONE value `fist_bump`; `summarizeReactions`
  returns `{ fistBumpCount, viewerHasReacted }` for rendering only);
  `index.ts` (public surface re-export).

- **What it ships ŌĆö new UI components:**
  `src/features/arguments/oneBox/schemas/AcceptanceGradientControl.tsx`
  (5-segment radio group ŌĆö color-independent "Ō£ō" selection marker, 44dp,
  radio + radiogroup roles, NO LayoutAnimation, NO Animated);
  `src/features/arguments/oneBox/schemas/ConcessionListSection.tsx`
  (forced-list section that plugs into the `respond` box; collapsible
  default-collapsed when empty; per-item TextInput; validation
  `firstReason` rendered as a visible single-line `accessibilityLiveRegion`);
  `src/features/arguments/oneBox/schemas/RespondToConcessionSchema.tsx`
  (the `respond_to_concession` box body ŌĆö mirrors every incoming item;
  Post disabled with a VISIBLE reason via the `firstDisabledReason`,
  NEVER silent; the Post's `accessibilityLabel` includes the reason
  when disabled); `src/features/concessions/FistBumpReaction.tsx`
  (the acknowledgment affordance ŌĆö renders NOTHING on own-move; "Ō£ō"
  indicator is color-independent; optional "┬ĘN" count from row count
  only, NEVER stored, NEVER feeds standing).

- **What it ships ŌĆö new DB + Edge:**
  `supabase/migrations/20260522000012_qol_041_concession_acceptance.sql`
  (three tables ŌĆö `concession_items` (1..600-char text via CHECK; unique
  (argument_id, ordinal); soft-delete only), `concession_acceptances`
  (5-value `acceptance_level` CHECK; `clarification_required_unless_agree`
  CHECK as defense-in-depth; immutable ŌĆö no UPDATE/DELETE policy;
  receiver-only INSERT via RLS), `move_reactions` (kind CHECK contains
  EXACTLY ONE value `fist_bump`; partial unique index allows toggle on/off
  via soft-delete; no score column anywhere)). NEVER stores LEVEL +
  CLARIFICATION delta ŌĆö QOL-041 consumes (does NOT re-derive) the
  point-standing economy.
  `supabase/functions/react-to-move/index.ts` (~225 lines ŌĆö the SOLE
  write path for `move_reactions`; JWT-verified, caller-scoped to reactor;
  own-bubble rejection; idempotent re-add via soft-delete reactivation;
  NEVER touches `public.arguments`; NEVER imports point-standing; NEVER
  makes an AI call; service-role used ONLY for the best-effort audit row;
  returns the render-only summary `{ fistBumpCount, viewerHasReacted }`).
  `supabase/config.toml` registers `verify_jwt = true` for the function.

- **What it ships ŌĆö modified files:**
  `supabase/functions/submit-argument/index.ts` (accepts optional
  `concession_items[]` on a `respond` move + optional `concession_acceptances[]`
  on a `respond_to_concession` move; inserts child rows after the parent
  argument insert; on any child-insert failure, soft-rolls-back the
  parent argument via `status='deleted'` so the move stays atomic from
  the user's perspective; authoritative defense-in-depth check that only
  the conceded-to author may grade; clarification-required-unless-agree
  re-asserted server-side; NEVER imports any point-standing module).
  `supabase/functions/_shared/validationSchemas.ts` (`AcceptanceLevelSchema`,
  `ConcessionItemPayloadSchema` with 1..600-char text + ordinal >= 0,
  `ConcessionAcceptancePayloadSchema` with a `.refine` enforcing
  clarification-required-unless-agree; `SubmitArgumentSchema` extended
  with optional `concession_items[]` (max 8 ŌĆö mirrors `MAX_CONCESSION_ITEMS`)
  + `concession_acceptances[]`). `src/lib/edgeFunctions.ts` (extends
  `SubmitArgumentInput` with optional `concession_items` +
  `concession_acceptances`; adds `reactToMove()` wrapper for the new
  Edge Function ŌĆö returns the `ReactToMoveSummary` shape with NO score
  field structurally). `src/lib/types.ts` (re-exports `AcceptanceLevel`,
  `MoveReactionKind` via `export type` declarations; adds
  `ConcessionItem`, `ConcessionAcceptance`, `MoveReaction` row interfaces
  as cross-feature domain types).

- **Doctrine encoded (cdiscourse-doctrine ┬¦1 / ┬¦4 / ┬¦6 / ┬¦9 ┬Ę
  point-standing-economy):** a concession is a scoring REPAIR, not a
  defeat ŌĆö no QOL-041 surface labels a concession a loss or the
  receiver a winner. The gradient is the receiver's STATED STANCE,
  mapped to `ConcessionEffect` VOCABULARY only; no delta, no score is
  stored or shown by this card. "Disagree based on fact" describes the
  RECEIVER'S STANCE toward a point, never a verdict that the point is
  false. `fact > context > framing` is a UI-FOCUS materiality ordering,
  not a truth rank ŌĆö the source comment documents this. Score never
  blocks posting; the conditional clarification is a VALIDATION block
  in the same family as the existing length check (cdiscourse-doctrine
  ┬¦1: "Validation can block, score cannot."). The fist-bump carries NO
  score, NO standing change, NO weight; the single-value `kind` enum
  makes the `move_reactions` table structurally incapable of becoming a
  voting system in v1 (anti-amplification respected by construction).
  No AI calls anywhere (deterministic + pure for the model layer; the
  Edge Function makes no provider call). No service-role in client code.
  All `arguments` writes still go through `submit-argument`; the new
  `react-to-move` function never touches `arguments`. RLS enabled on all
  three new tables; no DELETE policy anywhere ŌĆö soft-delete only. Edge
  Functions never log Authorization. Plain language only ŌĆö no internal
  codes leak; `argument` preferred over `debate` in every new copy
  string.

- **Hard constraints honored:** `src/lib/constitution/engine.ts` NOT
  modified. No new `arguments.argument_type` value. `concession` is
  already a valid argument type; QOL-041 ships the structured INPUT
  surface that the existing engine consumes. `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PACKET_VERSION`,
  `SEED_PROMPT_VERSION`, every classifier id, the MCP adapter, and the
  `process-language-draft` function are ALL untouched. No client file
  inserts into `public.arguments` / `concession_items` / `concession_acceptances`
  / `move_reactions` directly (a doctrine test asserts this for all 9
  QOL-041 client files). The migration carries NO standing / score /
  weight / delta column (a doctrine test asserts this against the
  migration source). The Edge Function NEVER imports `pointStanding` /
  `PointStandingDelta` / `gradeRepair` / `gradeChallenge` (a doctrine
  test asserts this with comment-stripping).

- **Tests (5 pure-model + 4 UI + 2 Edge-contract + 1 doctrine = 12 new
  suites / 218 new tests):** `acceptanceGradient.test.ts` (5-level enum
  vocab; `acceptanceRequiresClarification`; `ACCEPTANCE_TO_CONCESSION_EFFECT`
  maps to known ConcessionEffect families; ban-list); `concessionListModel.test.ts`
  (add/remove/reorder/update; empty list is VALID; 8-item cap; 600-char
  cap; over-cap / empty-item / over-length validation; payload builder
  trims + contiguous ordinals); `respondToConcessionModel.test.ts`
  (mirror; setRowLevel preserves clarification across re-pick (D3);
  isPostable enforces every-row-picked + every-non-agree-has-clarification;
  storyboard cases); `activeDisagreement.test.ts` (storyboard Step 8
  agree+disagree_fact ŌåÆ fact; precedence; newest-argument-wins; rider
  rule); `moveReactionModel.test.ts` (ONE value vocab; counts active
  rows only; viewer flag; shape has no score field structurally);
  `ConcessionListSection.test.tsx` (source-scan: exactly ONE TextInput
  in the section; forced-list shape; validation surface; 44dp; ban-list);
  `AcceptanceGradientControl.test.tsx` (radio + radiogroup roles; "Ō£ō"
  selection marker; iterates ALL_ACCEPTANCE_LEVELS; SEGMENT_MIN_HEIGHT
  = 44; NO LayoutAnimation); `RespondToConcessionSchema.test.tsx`
  (mirrors every incoming item; conditional clarification render;
  Post disabled with visible reason; buildConcessionAcceptancesPayload
  integration); `FistBumpReaction.test.tsx` (renders null on own move;
  toggle role; "Ō£ō" indicator; NO score/vote/standing field; never uses
  agree/like/upvote/approve); `submit-argument-concessions.test.ts`
  (source-scan: inserts items + acceptances; soft-rollback on failure;
  conceded-to-only authorization; clarification-required server check;
  migration Ōåö Zod vocabulary parity; migration carries NO standing/
  score column); `react-to-move.test.ts` (source-scan: JWT gate;
  caller-scoped client; own-bubble rejection; idempotent re-add;
  soft-delete only; NO score path; NO AI call; NO standing import);
  `qol041-doctrine.test.ts` (ban-list scan over EVERY 38 user-facing
  QOL-041 strings; pure-model source-purity scan over 6 files;
  client-side direct-write guard over 9 files; 5-level vocabulary
  parity across migration + Edge + client model).

- **Implementer decisions documented:**
  - **Migration sequential numbering:** the design named the migration
    `20260521000010_qol_041_concession_acceptance.sql`, but that prefix
    is taken by the shipped `20260521000010_qol042_argument_room_links.sql`.
    Bumped to `20260522000012_qol_041_concession_acceptance.sql` to land
    after the most recent `20260522000011_admin_ai_001_ŌĆ”` migration.
    Migrations are monotonic; the design's collision was a typo, not a
    constraint.
  - **Vocabulary bridge mapping:** the design ┬¦4 mandates a deterministic
    mapping from each `AcceptanceLevel` to a `ConcessionEffect` family,
    but does NOT specify which family each level maps to. Chose:
    `agree` + `agree_with_caveat` ŌåÆ `explicit_narrow_concession_preserves_broad_point`
    (the most common / charitable interpretation ŌĆö the offered
    concession was accepted); every `disagree_*` ŌåÆ
    `performative_concession_no_repair` (the offered concession did NOT
    function as a repair from the receiver's perspective). The future
    wiring stage may refine this; the bridge here is a LABEL
    correspondence, not a scoreboard.
  - **`react-to-move` audit row:** mirrored the `apply-manual-tag`
    pattern ŌĆö best-effort audit insert via service role, swallow errors,
    don't block the user response. Service role is used exactly ONCE
    (for the audit), satisfying the doctrine "service-role used ONLY for
    the best-effort audit row" pattern.
  - **`renderSchema` (`boxModel.ts`) untouched:** `boxModel.renderSchema()`
    already returns the right `SchemaKind` + sections for `respond`
    (`composite` / `[concession_list, body]`) and `respond_to_concession`
    (`forced_list` / `[concession_list]`). The QOL-041 UI components are
    READY for the consumer / host to mount; wiring them into
    `OneBox.tsx` is composition logic the consumer owns (the QOL-037
    `RespondToEvidenceForm` follows the same precedent ŌĆö built as a
    standalone surface, host wires it). No `boxModel.ts` change needed.
  - **Atomic move via soft-rollback:** `supabase-js` cannot wrap
    multi-statement transactions across separate `.insert()` calls. On a
    child-insert failure (`concession_items` or `concession_acceptances`)
    the Edge Function sets the parent argument's `status='deleted'` ŌĆö
    the closest atomic approximation available. From the user's
    perspective the move is atomic: either everything posts or nothing
    is visible.
  - **Q1-Q5 design defaults shipped:** Q1 cap = 8 items; Q2
    `agree_with_caveat` requires clarification (the caveat is a rider,
    not a `framing`/`context`/`fact` axis); Q3 any room reader may
    fist-bump (but NEVER own-move ŌĆö enforced in the Edge Function); Q4
    `react-to-move` ships in the same card (operator decides whether to
    deploy together or stage); Q5 the tiny "┬ĘN" count is shown
    (controllable via `showCount=false` prop for a future
    conservative-reading rollout).

  all passing** (from the 9542 / 360 QOL-035 baseline). Typecheck + lint

     `20260522000012_qol_041_concession_acceptance.sql` (the three

  `debate_id` references in three INSERT-policy WITH-CHECK subqueries

- **Implementer decisions documented:**
  - **"argument" vs "conversation":** per the rules doc both are approved. Used "argument" for the STRUCTURAL framing (form labels, error messages, room titles ŌĆö "Create Argument", "Failed to create argument", "Join Argument") and would have used "conversation" for the SOCIAL framing (gallery cards, lobby copy). The current 16 files were all structural; no conversation framing applied this round.
  - **"observer" vs "admin":** per the rules doc both are approved replacements for "moderator". Used "admin" wherever the role is a HARD MODERATION GATE (flag review, civility-heuristic review, validation `needs_moderator_review`, gameStatus.needs_judge_human_review) ŌĆö the function is operator review, not passive observation. Used the existing "observer" canon vocabulary nowhere new (it already covers the read-only role in OBSERVER_COPY).
  - **"Debate club" mode name:** chose "Practice argument club" over plain "Argument club" to retain the cultural "practice / structured-rehearsal" connotation the original implied, while replacing "debate" with "argument" per the canon vocabulary. Other mode names in ARGUMENT_MODE_COPY use varied vocabulary (e.g., "Friendly disagreement", "Workplace decision", "Evidence review") so adding "practice" fits the pattern.
  - **ArgumentTreeScreen empty-state wording:** the audit-flagged string was "This debate has no posted arguments." A literal replacement would yield "This argument has no posted arguments." ŌĆö awkward repetition. Used the established "move" vocabulary ("This argument has no posted moves yet.") because COMPOSER_COPY.yourMove = "Your Move" and the entire MOVE_COPY / TIMELINE_COPY surface already treats "move" as the canonical word for a message inside a room. This keeps the noun for the room ("argument") distinct from the noun for the messages ("moves").
  - **Anthropic prompt labels (buildAnthropicRequest.ts + anthropicProvider.ts):** the prompt labels "Debate resolution:" / "Debate description:" / "User's debate side:" travel to the AI provider (not the user). Strictly speaking they're prompt content, not UI copy ŌĆö but the audit's scope includes them (`src/features/` is in scope, supabase functions are NOT). Changed both the Node-side mirror AND the supabase function side to keep them in sync; the Node-side comment explicitly says "Mirrors the logic in supabase/functions/_shared/languageProcessing/anthropicProvider.ts (buildAnthropicRequestBody). Keep in sync if the prompt changes." The TypeScript field names `input.debateResolution` / `input.debateDescription` / `input.userSide` stay unchanged per the internal-identifier exemption.
  - **"Could not load debates" string in DebateListScreen:** the audit's JSX-text extractor uses `>[^<>{}]+<`, which skipped this string because it sits next to a `{error}` JSX expression. Not flagged in the audit table, but updated for consistency since the whole screen received the scrub.

- **+0 tests / +0 suites.** Full suite **9542 tests / 360 suites ŌĆö all passing** (unchanged from the MCP-CAT-001 baseline of 9542 / 360). No test required updates because no existing test asserted the exact value of a modified user-facing string ŌĆö the cascade tests scan ban-lists, not literal copy. Typecheck + lint clean.

- **Operator follow-up:** NONE. No migration. No Edge Function redeploy (the supabase-side prompt label change is included in this card's commit set, but the deployed `process-language-draft` Edge Function picks up the new prompt only when an operator redeploys it ŌĆö the change is cosmetic-to-the-AI and not user-visible, so the redeploy is OPTIONAL). No secret change. No admin runtime-config change. Rollback: `git revert` the four QOL-035 commits ŌĆö the audit returns to its 32 live + 7 legacy + 1 prohibited baseline. The category floors are minimums (Ōēź), so adding banners to existing categories does NOT break any floor assertion.

Adding ids to the catalog grows the question list but does NOT change the template shape, the instruction text, the worked-example block, or the redacted-input block. Per MCP-MOD-005's design ("Bumped to `-v2` in MCP-MOD-008: `buildInputBlock` now emits an optional `Room thread context:` blockŌĆ” The structural format of the prompt changed"), a version bump is warranted when the prompt's STRUCTURAL format changes ŌĆö not when the catalog grows. ## COMP-001 ŌĆö Deterministic composition layer for connected-node visual state (Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö pure-TS function `composeVisualState` maps the semantic referee's binary classifier signal vectors into typed `NodeVisualMutation` enum values targeting specific connected `moveId`s on the timeline. 22 composition rules + 2 exemption patterns (R-EX-01 root, R-EX-02 first-move-per-author) covering parent-continuity, evidence / source-chain, constructive movement, debate-mode, and branch / friction families. 12 PROPOSED ids from MCP-CAT-001 are referenced behind runtime catalog guards ŌĆö the rules degrade gracefully today and automatically activate when MCP-CAT-001 lands the ids. The composition layer is PURE (no Supabase, no React, no network, no async, no AI SDK), deterministic (snapshot-testable), and produces ZERO natural language (typed enum values only; rendering is downstream via the existing `gameCopy.toPlainLanguage` pattern). Integration is ADDITIVE: `useSemanticReferee` gains `getMutationsForMove(moveId)` + `getCompositionState()` accessors with the existing public surface unchanged; `argumentGameSurfaceModel.ts` gains an optional `crossNodeMutations` field + `getCrossNodeMutations` helper for the bubble-rendering layer to consume in a future UI card. `scripts/bot-fixtures/runMcpSmokeTest.js` optionally logs mutations per move (diagnostic-only, non-gating). Issue #244.

- **What it ships ŌĆö new files:** `src/features/semanticReferee/compositionTypes.ts` (pure-TS type contract ŌĆö `CompositionState` + per-item lifecycle types `EvidenceDebtState` / `ClarificationDebtState` / `SubAxisState` / `ConcessionLinkState` / `SourceChainGapState` / `NarrowingLinkState` / `SynthesisReadinessState`; - **Doctrine encoded (cdiscourse-doctrine ┬¦1 / ┬¦2 / ┬¦3 / ┬¦4):** the layer makes NO truth claims ŌĆö every value is a STRUCTURAL state (debt opened, point conceded, sub-axis resolved); the composition function reads 0/1 values from `SemanticBinarySample.value` and does NOT interpret `reasonCode` strings (the binary contract is preserved); the `popularity_amplification_warning` rule (R-EV-04) emits ONLY on the current move ŌĆö doctrine forbids attaching a verdict to an ancestor; every value in `NodeVisualMutationType` is scanned against the verdict ban-list (`winner` / `loser` / `truth` / `correct` / `wrong` / `right` / `false` / `proven` / `defeated` / `won` / `lost`) and the person-label ban-list (`liar` / `dishonest` / `bad faith` / `manipulative` / `extremist` / `propagandist` / `troll`) ŌĆö zero hits across all 35 enum values + all emitted mutations under the all-ones packet; the layer produces ZERO natural language (rendering is downstream); the layer is PURE TS (same purity rules as `engine.ts` ŌĆö no Supabase / React / network / async / AI SDK imports ŌĆö enforced by `compositionLayerPurity.test.ts`); the layer is DETERMINISTIC (same inputs ŌåÆ same outputs ŌĆö enforced by the determinism test in the purity suite); the layer is INDIFFERENT to deletion state (the design's ┬¦13 Q4 ŌĆö rendering policy lives downstream); the layer does NOT decide what the AI classifies (the catalog is the source of truth for classifier ids ŌĆö adding an id is MCP-CAT-001 territory; adding a rule is COMP-001 territory; the two slates do not collide).

  - **35-id mode tests (band-space-rent):** included as a forward-compatibility parity check that asserts the runtime-guarded PROPOSED-id rules do NOT speculatively fire before MCP-CAT-001 lands the ids in the catalog (the 35-id snapshot equals the 23-id snapshot). ## MCP-MOD-008 ŌĆö Move-position-aware triggering rule + full-thread context (Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX ┬Ę Movement C)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö **FINAL CARD of the modularity slate**. Movement C, Card 2 of 2. **The ONLY card in the entire slate that changes user-observable behavior.** Stage 6.4.x ŌĆö From each participant's SECOND move onward, the semantic referee evaluates the FULL thread context, not just the parent. Each participant's FIRST move in a debate no longer triggers classification (it would mostly fail by definition). Visible effect: users see the referee banner on their second move and onward; the layer-1 fallback is what they see on the opening statement and first rebuttal, exactly as if `{ enabled: false }` came back. The first-move-skip is participant-scoped ŌĆö a chime-in participant's first contribution is exempt too, automatic from the pure helper's counting logic. Issue #237.

- **What it ships ŌĆö new files:** `src/features/semanticReferee/threadContext.ts` (pure-TS helpers `buildAuthorAliasMap` + `assemblePriorMovesPayload` + `aliasForIndex`; spreadsheet-column alias scheme A..Z, AA..AZ, BA..BZ; redacts each prior-move body via the client redactor, drops moves whose author has no alias, enforces the per-batch token budget by dropping OLDEST first, returns [] when even move + parent overflow); `__tests__/triggerGateFirstMoveSkip.test.ts` (15 tests ŌĆö root move / first-by-opponent / first-by-chime-in all refuse with `first_move_by_author`; A's second + later moves allowed; ordering: refusal runs BEFORE per-moment preconditions but AFTER layer / mode / role checks; backward compat when authorId / priorMoves are absent); `__tests__/movePositionThreadBudget.test.ts` (11 tests ŌĆö under / just-over / way-over budget regimes; oldest-first drop preserving newest; budget accounting for prior-move bytes; defensive paths); `__tests__/seedPromptThreadContextBlock.test.ts` (10 tests ŌĆö block presence / absence / ordering above parent + move blocks; chronological preservation; byte-for-byte `- Move N by <alias>: <body>` 1-indexed format; AA wrap-around alias support; v2 prompt-version assertion); `__tests__/classifyMoveRequestPriorMovesParity.test.ts` (15 tests ŌĆö source-scan parity across Node `edgeFunctions.ts`, Deno `types.ts`, Deno `schema.ts`, Deno `redaction.ts` for the new optional field shape; alias bound `MAX_ALIAS_LEN`; field-name agreement; PII-field absence on `PriorMoveContext`); `__tests__/movePositionRoomHookIntegration.test.ts` (8 tests ŌĆö synthetic 5-move room; A1 / B1 / C-chime-in first moves all skip; A's second + B's second fire WITH the redacted prior-moves payload; alias stability across calls; no raw user id / display name / email leaks; backward-compat path when priorMoves is absent).

## MCP-MOD-007 ŌĆö Move-position tracking helper (Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX ┬Ę Movement C)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö Movement C, Card 1 of 2. **No behavior change in this card.** Adds a small, PURE helper `getMovePositionForAuthor` that derives whether a just-posted (or about-to-be-posted) move is the FIRST, SECOND, or LATER move by its author in the debate. Pure-TS, no Supabase, no React, no async, no network ŌĆö same purity rules as `engine.ts`. The classification is participant-scoped: it counts how many entries in `priorMoves` share the input's `authorId` (0 ŌåÆ `'first'`, 1 ŌåÆ `'second'`, Ōēź2 ŌåÆ `'later'`). Chime-in handling is automatic: a chime-in participant's first contribution returns `'first'` regardless of how many moves the primary participants have made before them. The helper does NOT talk to Supabase ŌĆö the caller (MCP-MOD-008) is responsible for assembling `priorMoves` from the room state, and for NOT including the move under classification inside `priorMoves`. **No file outside `src/features/semanticReferee/movePosition.ts` and its test file imports the helper yet** ŌĆö MCP-MOD-008 wires it into `evaluateTrigger`. **No change to `triggerGates.ts`, `seedPrompt.ts`, the banner library, the ledger, the content-safety scan, the catalog file, any Edge Function, `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PACKET_VERSION`, or any schema.** Issue #236.

- **What it ships ŌĆö new files:** `src/features/semanticReferee/movePosition.ts` (pure-TS helper; exports `MovePosition` type, `MovePositionInput` interface, and `getMovePositionForAuthor` function with early short-circuit at count Ōēź 2); `__tests__/movePositionHelper.test.ts` (12 tests ŌĆö 7 core counting-contract tests covering first / second / later transitions, ignoring other authors, empty `priorMoves`, the moveId-in-priorMoves edge case; plus 5 scenario tests covering first-move-by-initiator with empty `priorMoves`, first-move-by-opponent after initiator's root, second-move-by-initiator after a reply, first-move-by-chime-in after 5 primary-participant moves, and an author with zero prior moves in a 20-move thread by others).
- **What it ships ŌĆö modified files:** `docs/core/current-status.md` ŌĆö this entry.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the helper performs counting only ŌĆö it never produces a verdict, a truth value, a winner / loser label, or any person-label of any kind. Pure TypeScript with same purity rules as `engine.ts` (no Supabase / React / network imports, side-effect-free, JSON-serializable inputs / outputs). No file outside the helper itself and its test file imports it yet ŌĆö MCP-MOD-008's diff is the wire-in.
- **+12 tests / +1 suite.** Full suite **9212 tests / 344 suites ŌĆö all passing** (from the 9200 / 343 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **Operator follow-up:** none. The helper is pure-TS and unused; no Edge Function redeploy, no migration, no secret change, no admin runtime-config change. MCP-MOD-008 wires the helper into `evaluateTrigger`. Rollback is `git revert` of the merge commit ŌĆö the helper file disappears and no caller depended on it.

## MCP-MOD-006 ŌĆö Banner + ledger refactor: `CLASSIFIER_TO_BANNERS` and `classifierFor` consume `SEMANTIC_CLASSIFIER_CATALOG` (Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX ┬Ę Movement B)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö the **final card of Movement B** in the semantic-referee modularity slate. Closes the two documented departures MCP-MOD-004 reviewer-approved (PASS 21/21): the banner library's `CLASSIFIER_TO_BANNERS` and the ledger's inverted `classifierFor` table are now DERIVED VIEWS over the catalog. Extends `SemanticClassifierCatalogEntry` (Node + Deno mirrors stay byte-identical) with two new fields: `bannerCodePriorityList: readonly string[]` (the full ordered candidate list per id ŌĆö `selectBanner` consumes this; the primary `bannerCode` is its first entry) and `ledgerCategories: readonly string[]` (the list of `RefereePointCategory` values the id surfaces under in the ledger's `l2SignalForCategory` lookup ŌĆö inverted to build the `category ŌåÆ id` table at module load; `responds_to_parent` is the only id that surfaces under two categories: `continuity` AND `direct_response`). `toPlainLanguage` (in `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts`) now consults `CATALOG_BY_ID.get(id).plainLanguageLabel` first and falls back to the existing `PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY` table ŌĆö catalog v0 has no label set on any of the 23 entries so behavior is byte-identical. **Behavior is byte-identical** ŌĆö the MCP-MOD-004 golden snapshot test still passes byte-for-byte, three new fuzz-parity tests confirm the post-refactor and pre-refactor reference implementations agree across 50 random packets (banner), 50 random packets ├Ś 10 categories (ledger), and every classifier id (plain-language). **No new classifier ids, no banner codes, no ledger codes, no `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PACKET_VERSION` bump, no `SEED_PROMPT_VERSION` bump, no `seedPrompt.ts` change, no `process-language-draft` change, no admin Edge Function change, no MCP adapter change, no migration, no env var.** Issue #235.

- **What it ships ŌĆö new files:** `__tests__/semanticBannerFuzzParity.test.ts` (6 tests ŌĆö 50 deterministically-random `BannerSelectionInput` packets seeded with `COMMITTED_SEED = 0x6dcb5106`; for each fixture asserts the live `selectBanner` and a local-only reference impl that reads a frozen pre-MCP-MOD-006 `CLASSIFIER_TO_BANNERS` literal produce byte-identical `BannerSelectionResult`s; plus corpus shape, determinism, and a sanity assertion that the reference is a distinct function object); `__tests__/semanticLedgerFuzzParity.test.ts` (10 tests ŌĆö asserts the catalog-derived `classifierFor` view equals the frozen pre-MCP-MOD-006 literal entry-for-entry; for 50 random packets ├Ś 10 categories asserts the live l2-signal helper and a local-only reference impl that reads the frozen literal produce identical `(present, sign, confidence)` tuples; plus inversion-collision-freedom and the 14-without-lookup catalog v0 baseline; seeded with `COMMITTED_SEED = 0x4f6d8c12`); `__tests__/semanticPlainLanguageParity.test.ts` (8 tests ŌĆö for every classifier id in `ALL_SEMANTIC_CLASSIFIER_IDS` asserts `toPlainLanguage(id)` returns the captured pre-MCP-MOD-006 value; plus the catalog-v0 baseline that no entry sets `plainLanguageLabel`, the override-precedence shape, and the non-classifier fallback path).
- **What it ships ŌĆö modified files:** `src/lib/constitution/semanticClassifierCatalog.ts` (Node-side catalog) and `supabase/functions/_shared/semanticReferee/semanticClassifierCatalog.ts` (Deno-side mirror) ŌĆö `SemanticClassifierCatalogEntry` gains two new fields `bannerCodePriorityList` + `ledgerCategories`; every existing entry is populated (the per-id priority list lifted verbatim from the pre-refactor `CLASSIFIER_TO_BANNERS` block in `classifierBannerMap.ts`; the per-id category list lifted verbatim from the pre-refactor inline `classifierFor` block in `reconcileMove.l2SignalForCategory`); header docstrings updated. `src/features/refereeBanners/classifierBannerMap.ts` ŌĆö `CLASSIFIER_TO_BANNERS` becomes a single `Object.fromEntries(SEMANTIC_CLASSIFIER_CATALOG.map(...))` derivation; the 23 hand-written per-id list entries are gone; header docstring updated to name the new authority chain. `src/features/refereeLedger/reconcileMove.ts` ŌĆö the inline `classifierFor` `const` inside `l2SignalForCategory` is replaced with a module-level `CLASSIFIER_FOR_CATEGORY` table built at module load by inverting the catalog's `ledgerCategories` field (defensively guards against same-category-twice collisions ŌĆö the build throws if catalog v0 ever introduces a collision); `l2SignalForCategory`'s body reads the derived table. `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` ŌĆö `toPlainLanguage` now consults the catalog's `plainLanguageLabel` first; a new private `catalogPlainLanguageLabelFor` helper handles the lookup; the existing fallback to `PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY` is preserved. `__tests__/semanticClassifierCatalogParity.test.ts` ŌĆö the now-tautological "bannerCode matches CLASSIFIER_TO_BANNERS[id][0]" assertion is rewritten as the catalog-internal invariant `bannerCode === bannerCodePriorityList[0]`; new `ledger-categories parity` block adds 4 assertions covering the type, inversion-collision-freedom, the 9-vs-14 catalog v0 split, and `responds_to_parent`'s two-category surface; new "every code in any bannerCodePriorityList is a valid banner code" + "derived view equals catalog" + "intentionally-silent classifiers have empty lists" assertions. `__tests__/semanticClassifierCatalogDenoNodeParity.test.ts` ŌĆö two new extractors (`extractBannerPriorityLists`, `extractLedgerCategoriesLists`) and two new tests assert per-id parity between Node and Deno mirrors for the new fields. `__tests__/refereeBannerForbiddenImports.test.ts` ŌĆö the allowlist for cross-feature imports adds `../../lib/constitution/semanticClassifierCatalog` (the new runtime import required for the derived view); the "type-only imports" sub-test docstring is updated to note the catalog is a runtime import and is correctly skipped. `docs/core/current-status.md` ŌĆö this entry.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the catalog stays pure TypeScript ŌĆö same `engine.ts` purity rules (no Supabase / React / network imports, frozen at module load, JSON-serializable values). `ledgerCategories` is typed as `readonly string[]` (the same posture `bannerCodePriorityList` already takes) so the catalog stays standalone-pure (no `import type { RefereePointCategory }` from the features tree) ŌĆö the parity test enforces every value is a member of `ALL_REFEREE_POINT_CATEGORIES`. The Deno mirror's type matches the Node side byte-for-byte on the catalog span (no `import type`-shaped drift). `selectBanner` and `l2SignalForCategory` keep their pre-existing pure-TS character ŌĆö the only changes are the table source (catalog-derived) and not the iteration / confidence / priority logic. `toPlainLanguage` keeps its plain-language contract: no internal codes ever reach a user surface; unknown codes are suppressed, not echoed. The MCP-013 anti-amplification doctrine is unchanged ŌĆö engagement credit and factual-standing eligibility stay on separate axes.
- **Behavior preservation evidence:** (1) The MCP-MOD-004 golden snapshot test (`semanticClassifierCatalogSnapshotPrompt.test.ts`) still passes byte-for-byte ŌĆö this card doesn't touch the prompt. (2) The banner fuzz-parity test compares the live `selectBanner` (consuming the catalog-derived `CLASSIFIER_TO_BANNERS`) against a local-only reference impl that reads a frozen pre-refactor literal table; 50/50 fixtures produce byte-identical `BannerSelectionResult`s. (3) The ledger fuzz-parity test asserts the catalog-derived `classifierFor` view equals the frozen pre-refactor literal entry-for-entry, AND for 50 random packets ├Ś 10 categories the live and reference l2-signal helpers produce identical `(present, sign, confidence)` tuples. (4) The plain-language parity test pins `toPlainLanguage(id)` to its pre-refactor return value for every classifier id (22 `null`s + the single `'Ready for synthesis'` for `ready_for_synthesis` that came from the pre-existing `PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY` table). All reference implementations live ONLY inside their respective test files as `localOnly*` functions; they never leak into the public API.
- **Catalog extension decisions (documented):** the design's ┬¦9 explicitly authorized extending `SemanticClassifierCatalogEntry` if the existing shape couldn't hold the per-id structure. Two fields were added: (i) `bannerCodePriorityList: readonly string[]` because `selectBanner` needs the FULL ordered list per id (not just the primary code) to pool candidates inside a category; (ii) `ledgerCategories: readonly string[]` because the ledger's lookup goes `RefereePointCategory ŌåÆ SemanticClassifierId` (the inverse direction of the catalog's `id ŌåÆ ledgerFeedbackCode`), AND a single id may surface under multiple categories (`responds_to_parent` for `continuity` + `direct_response`). Both fields are typed `readonly string[]` (matching the existing posture of `bannerCode: string | null`) so the catalog stays standalone-pure ŌĆö the per-id parity tests enforce the value sets. Alternative B (keep the library tables, cross-reference the catalog) was rejected because it leaves two sources of truth and undermines the modularity goal; alternative C (drop `bannerCode` / `ledgerFeedbackCode` entirely) was rejected because the primary fields are still useful for downstream UI surfaces that want just the one canonical code per id.
- **+29 tests / +3 suites.** Full suite **9200 tests / 343 suites ŌĆö all passing** (from the 9171 / 340 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **Operator follow-up:** the diff is entirely client-side (`src/` + the Deno-side catalog mirror only); the Deno-side `semanticClassifierCatalog.ts` change is consumed by `seedPrompt.ts` and the MCP / Anthropic providers via the existing catalog import path, so `npx supabase functions deploy semantic-referee --linked` after merge is still useful to ship the Deno mirror change. **The smoke test (`node scripts/bot-fixtures/runMcpSmokeTest.js`) is the structural regression check** ŌĆö re-run it post-deploy and confirm results match the pre-MCP-MOD-006 baseline (the unit + fuzz-parity tests are the behavioural check; the smoke test is the contract-end-to-end check). No migration, no secret change, no admin runtime-config change. Rollback is `git revert` of the merge commit ŌĆö the pre-refactor inline tables in `classifierBannerMap.ts` and `reconcileMove.ts` were not preserved verbatim, but every datum needed to reconstruct them lives in the catalog (and the local-only reference impls in the new fuzz-parity tests hold a frozen copy of each).

(2) the catalog's `ledgerFeedbackCode` field is the PRIMARY code per id; the ledger's `classifierFor` table is kept intact because it is structurally `category ŌåÆ classifier` (the INVERSE direction; a single classifier can surface on multiple categories ŌĆö e.g. `responds_to_parent` on both `continuity` and `direct_response`). Parity tests in `semanticClassifierCatalogParity.test.ts` assert the catalog's primary values agree with the banner library's FIRST entry per id and with the existing ledger feedback code enumeration.

## MCP-MOD-002 ŌĆö Classifier catalog inventory (Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX ┬Ę Movement A)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö ships a single new architecture doc, `docs/architecture/semantic-referee-classifier-catalog.md`, that walks through every one of the 23 classifier ids in catalog v0 and names, per id: the binary signal it detects (one-sentence plain-language reconstruction), the structural AI question asked of the live provider (copied byte-for-byte from `CLASSIFIER_QUESTION_TEXT` in `supabase/functions/_shared/semanticReferee/seedPrompt.ts`), the first banner-library code listed in `CLASSIFIER_TO_BANNERS[id]` (or `ŌĆö` with "intentionally silent" for `contains_unplayable_insult_only`), the `RefereeFeedbackCode` the ledger emits when the binary fires `1` for the category this id maps to in `reconcileMove.l2SignalForCategory`'s `classifierFor` table (or `ŌĆö` with "not yet mapped" when no row exists), and the source-of-truth file (`supabase/functions/_shared/semanticReferee/types.ts` / `ALL_SEMANTIC_CLASSIFIER_IDS`). ## MCP-018 ŌĆö Operator-hosted MCP-server adapter (un-stub the `mcp` provider slot) (Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö un-stubs MCP-009's reserved `mcp` provider slot with a real, working **operator-hosted MCP-server adapter** for the `semantic-referee` Edge Function. It is the exact analog of the MCP-017 `anthropic` provider: when `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER=mcp`, a new `mcpAdapter.ts` reaches an operator-hosted MCP server over HTTPS (`SEMANTIC_REFEREE_MCP_URL`, authenticated with `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_MCP_TOKEN`, both read via `Deno.env.get()` inside the Edge Function only) and asks it to classify one argument move's structure. The `mcp` provider is **opt-in**; `mock` stays the default via the unchanged `?? 'mock'` fallback. **No migration, no `supabase/config.toml` change, no `index.ts` change, no type-file widening** (the `McpUnavailableReason` ŌåÆ `ClassifyMoveDisabledReason` map sends `url_missing`/`token_missing` onto the existing `not_configured`). **No live MCP-server call was made by the implementer** ŌĆö every test mocks the HTTP; the first real call is the operator's after deploy + secret set + flag flip. No service-role, no direct insert into `public.arguments`, no new dependency, no `.env` touched. Builds on MCP-016 (boundary) + MCP-017 (live-provider pattern) + ADMIN-AI-001 (DB-resolution layer). Issue #224.

- **What it ships ŌĆö new provider files** (`supabase/functions/_shared/semanticReferee/`): `mcpAdapterCore.ts` (zod-free, Jest-importable core ŌĆö `buildMcpToolRequestBody`, `extractMcpPacket` (tolerates `result` / `output` / `content[]` envelopes), `parseJsonFromContent` (a documented local copy of the `anthropicClassifierCore.ts` sibling helper ŌĆö AC5 forbids editing that file), `sanitizeMcpRawPayload`, the `MCP_CLASSIFY_TOOL_NAME = 'classify_semantic_move'` constant, `MCP_REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS`, `DEFAULT_MCP_MODEL_VERSION`, and the `McpUnavailableReason` / `McpProviderResult` boundary-internal types); `mcpAdapter.ts` (the Deno-only orchestrator and the **only** file that reads `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_MCP_URL` / `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_MCP_TOKEN` via `Deno.env.get()` and `fetch`es the operator-hosted MCP server ŌĆö https-only URL guard, one `POST` with a Bearer-token Authorization header + `AbortSignal.timeout`, every failure path returns a typed `unavailable` result, and even a successful response is re-validated through `SemanticRefereePacketSchema` + `scanPacketContent`; `provider` is hard-stamped `'mcp'`, `authoritative` hard-pinned `false`).
- **What it ships ŌĆö modified files:** `providerRoutingCore.ts` un-stubs the `mcp` branch (was a literal `not_implemented`) ŌĆö wired through a new injected async `runMcp` dep, plus the pure `mcpReasonToOutcomeReason` map. `providerRouting.ts` wires `runMcp: runMcpAdapter` into `DEFAULT_PROVIDER_DEPS`. `__tests__/_helpers/semanticRefereeDeno.ts` bridges the new zod-free `mcpAdapterCore.ts` and extends `SemanticRefereeProviderDeps` with `runMcp`. `semantic-referee/index.ts`, `anthropicProvider.ts`, `anthropicClassifierCore.ts`, `process-language-draft/` ŌĆö **not touched** (acceptance criterion 5).
- **Doctrine encoded:** the `mcp` provider is **opt-in, never default** ŌĆö the `?? 'mock'` fallback is byte-identical and the `semanticProviderRegistry.test.ts` "default is mock" assertion still passes. The adapter **never throws to the client** ŌĆö `url_missing` / `token_missing` / `api_error` / `rate_limited` / `network_error` / `parse_failure` / `validation_failed` all return a typed `unavailable` `McpProviderResult` translated to an `{ enabled: false, reason }` outcome with HTTP 200; the caller falls back to the deterministic layer-1 result. `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_MCP_URL` / `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_MCP_TOKEN` are read via `Deno.env.get()` in **exactly one file** (`mcpAdapter.ts`); they appear nowhere in `src/` / `app/` / `.env*` and are never logged; the token rides the Authorization header only over TLS (a non-`https` URL is rejected as `url_missing` before any `fetch`). Every MCP-server response is re-validated through the outbound `.strict()` `SemanticRefereePacketSchema` **and** the Deno content-safety scanner ŌĆö a smuggled `block` field, `authoritative: true`, or a verdict token forces the deterministic fallback. The MCP-tool request asks for **structure** only ŌĆö `buildMcpToolRequestBody` carries no verdict / truth / winner / popularity / `block` field. `mcp` stays **non-admin-selectable** ŌĆö `adminSemanticConfigSchemas.ts` and `AdminSemanticRefereeTab` are untouched (the write-path `z.enum` stays three-mode; the UI control stays disabled ŌĆö making `mcp` admin-selectable is a separate one-line follow-up card).
- **+89 tests / +3 suites.** Full suite **9056 tests / 328 suites ŌĆö 9055 passing**. The one red suite (`diagnosticInspectPackage.test.ts`) is a **pre-existing failure unrelated to this card** ŌĆö its safety scanner flags an `x_handle`-shaped string inside a gitignored diagnostics artifact; MCP-018 touches no diagnostic script, and the same suite was already red on the untouched baseline. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean. New suites: `semanticMcpAdapterCore.test.ts`, `semanticMcpSourceScan.test.ts`, `semanticEdgeMcpAdapter.test.ts`. Extended: `semanticProviderRegistry.test.ts` (the "mcp stub ŌåÆ not_implemented" test is rewritten as "mcp routes to runMcp"; +reason-map + routing cases), `semanticProviderRegistryDbResolution.test.ts` (the stale "DB mcp ŌåÆ not_implemented stub" test rewritten for the un-stubbed routing), `semanticNoLiveCallInRouter.test.ts` (the `mcpAdapter.ts`-absence assertion inverted), `semanticBoundaryBanList.test.ts`, `semanticBoundaryRedaction.test.ts`, `semanticForbiddenSecrets.test.ts`, `semanticEdgeBoundary.test.ts`.
- **Operator follow-up (deploy is a separate operator action ŌĆö full procedure in `docs/deployment/mcp-018-mcp-adapter-runbook.md`):** `npx supabase functions deploy semantic-referee --linked` ships the `mcpAdapter.ts` code (still mock-behaving until the flag flips); `npx supabase secrets set SEMANTIC_REFEREE_MCP_URL=https://<host>/<path>` + `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_MCP_TOKEN=<token>` wire the operator-hosted MCP server; `npx supabase secrets set SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER=mcp` flips to the MCP provider (or set the ADMIN-AI-001 DB `provider_mode` row to `'mcp'` by hand). Rollback is one line: `npx supabase secrets set SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER=mock`. No migration, no dependency install, no `.env` change.

## ADMIN-AI-001 ŌĆö Admin runtime provider-mode switch for the semantic referee (Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö turns the `semantic-referee` provider mode into an **admin-controlled runtime setting**. Today switching `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER` from `mock` to `anthropic` (or back) needs `npx supabase secrets set` + a cold start ŌĆö an operator-only, terminal-only action. ADMIN-AI-001 moves the *runtime source of truth* to a persisted admin DB setting so an authenticated admin switches the effective provider mode (`anthropic` / `mock` / `fixture`; a reserved-but-disabled `mcp` slot) from the Admin UI with **no env-var edit, no redeploy, no code change**. Resolution hierarchy: **DB config > `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER` env var > code fallback `mock`**. **One new append-only migration + two Edge Function updates** ŌĆö the operator applies them post-merge; the implementer ran no `npx supabase` command and made no live AI call. No service-role in client code, no direct insert into `public.arguments`, no `submit-argument` change, no new dependency, no `.env` touched. Builds on MCP-016 (boundary) + MCP-017 (live `anthropic` provider). Issue #225.

- **What it ships ŌĆö migration (write-only):** `supabase/migrations/20260522000011_admin_ai_001_semantic_referee_runtime_config.sql` ŌĆö `public.semantic_referee_runtime_config` (the strongly-typed singleton: `id boolean PK CHECK (id = true)`, `provider_mode` CHECK-constrained to the four registry slots, `enabled` runtime off-switch; RLS: admin SELECT + admin UPDATE, **no INSERT/DELETE policy** ŌĆö seed-only, permanent row); `public.semantic_referee_config_audit` (append-only provider-mode change history; RLS: admin SELECT + admin INSERT, **no UPDATE/DELETE policy**); `public.get_semantic_referee_runtime_config()` (`SECURITY DEFINER`, locked `search_path`, `RETURNS` the three safe fields only ŌĆö never `updated_by`, never audit history, never a secret); seeds the singleton `{ provider_mode: 'anthropic', enabled: true }`.
- **What it ships ŌĆö Deno resolver + registry:** `supabase/functions/_shared/semanticReferee/runtimeConfig.ts` ŌĆö `resolveSemanticRefereeConfig` reads the persisted config via the `SECURITY DEFINER` RPC; on **any** failure (rpc error / empty / thrown / corrupt row / unknown `provider_mode`) returns `{ source: 'db_unavailable' }` so the caller falls through to env. **NEVER throws.** Zod-free; reads no env key. `providers.ts` ŌĆö `classifyWithConfiguredProvider` now takes the caller-scoped client, resolves the DB layer first, and on `db_unavailable` falls through to the **existing `Deno.env` path verbatim** ŌĆö `providerRoutingCore.ts`'s `?? 'mock'` code fallback is byte-identical (doctrine constraint #1). `semantic-referee/index.ts` passes the caller-scoped client; it still builds no service-role client and performs no write.
- **What it ships ŌĆö admin Edge Function + Admin UI:** `_shared/adminSemanticConfigSchemas.ts` ŌĆö `GetSemanticConfigSchema` + `SetSemanticConfigSchema`; the write enum is `anthropic|mock|fixture` (`mcp` is **not settable** ŌĆö reserved for MCP-018), and a `.refine()` enforces `confirmAnthropic=true` when switching to `anthropic` server-side (the dialog is the UX, the refine is the wall). `admin-users/index.ts` gains `get_semantic_config` (returns mode, enabled, last-changed-by display name, and a SAFE `anthropicKeyPresent` **boolean only**) + `set_semantic_config` (updates the singleton, appends the config-audit row, writes the generic admin-traffic audit row). `src/features/admin/AdminSemanticRefereeTab.tsx` ŌĆö the new **Semantic Referee** Admin tab: status card, provider selector (`anthropic`/`mock`/`fixture` enabled; `mcp` disabled + "Coming later (MCP-018)"), enabled toggle, an Anthropic-switch confirmation panel ("Anthropic mode may use provider credits. Continue?"), one-click Mock rollback. `src/features/admin/semanticRefereeConfigApi.ts` ŌĆö the typed client wrapper + the shared `requiresProviderConfirmation` rule. Tab registered in `types.ts` / `AdminScreen.tsx` / `index.ts`.
- **Doctrine encoded:** provider resolution **never throws to the client** ŌĆö DB read fails ŌåÆ env; env invalid ŌåÆ code fallback `mock`; `anthropic` mode with no key ŌåÆ MCP-017's typed `unavailable` outcome, HTTP 200. The code fallback stays `mock` ŌĆö only the *seed row* is `anthropic`; `providerRoutingCore.ts` is unchanged (a regression test diffs the `?? 'mock'` literal). `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is **never displayed** ŌĆö the UI sees only an "Anthropic key present: Yes/No" boolean; the key is read as `Boolean(Deno.env.get(...))` inside `admin-users` only, never under `src/`. No service-role in client code; the admin write goes through `admin-users` with `requireAdmin`; JWT verification unchanged. The `SECURITY DEFINER` function has a locked `search_path`. Switching to Anthropic needs `confirmAnthropic=true` (server-enforced); switching to Mock is one-click. The card only chooses *which provider answers* ŌĆö every provider's output still flows through MCP-016's `.strict()` schema + MCP-017's content scan; no truth verdict, no scoring path, `submit-argument` untouched.
- **+131 tests / +8 suites.** Full suite **8967 tests / 325 suites ŌĆö 8966 passing**. The one red suite (`diagnosticInspectPackage.test.ts`) is a **pre-existing failure unrelated to this card** ŌĆö its safety scanner flags an `x_handle`-shaped string inside the pre-existing `docs/decision-ledger.md`; ADMIN-AI-001 touches no diagnostic script and no `decision-ledger.md`, and the same suite was already red on the untouched baseline. Creating QOL-001ŌĆ”014 would have been 14 duplicate cards, so they were correctly skipped per the dedupe rule.
