## MCP-019 ŌĆö Wire the semantic referee into a live room surface (Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö threads ONE `SemanticRefereePacket` from a live argument room in **mock mode**. The room hook calls the existing `classifyMove` Edge wrapper only when MCP-012's `evaluateTrigger` allows a `post_submit` moment and the client packet cache misses; the returned packet renders through MCP-014's `selectBanner` as one non-verdict banner and MCP-015's `evaluateSemanticOverridePrompt` as a small reversible lane-choice sheet. The semantic referee stays **OFF by default** ŌĆö `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_ENABLED` / `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER` are operator server secrets MCP-019 never touches; when they are unset (the v1 default) the Edge Function returns `{ enabled: false }` and the surface falls back to the deterministic layer-1 result with **no user-visible error**. **No migration, no Edge Function, no `supabase/` change, no live AI call, no new dependency** ŌĆö MCP-019 is pure client-side wiring. No service-role, no direct insert into `public.arguments`, no `.env` touched. Issue #223.

- **What it ships ŌĆö new files:** `src/features/semanticReferee/clientRedaction.ts` (pure-TS conservative first-pass body redactor ŌĆö strips `@handle` / URL / email / long-digit / provider-key shapes before a body leaves the device; the Edge boundary runs the authoritative second pass ŌĆö Defect 2). `src/features/semanticReferee/semanticTriggerInput.ts` (pure-TS ŌĆö `buildPostSubmitTriggerInput`, the frozen 9-id `POST_SUBMIT_CLASSIFIER_SET` spanning MCP-012 batch groups A+C, `mapParticipantSideToActorRole`, the client-intent-flag + classification-mode defaults). `src/features/arguments/useSemanticReferee.ts` (the room hook ŌĆö owns the room-scoped MCP-012 `SemanticPacketCache`, the in-memory `RepeatedOverrideSignal`, `refereeStateByMoveId`, the in-memory override records; the ONLY file that calls `classifyMove`). `src/features/refereeBanners/bannerSelectionInputFromPacket.ts` (pure-TS packet ŌåÆ `BannerSelectionInput` adapter, forward-compatible with a future `LedgerResult` ŌĆö Defect 1). `src/features/refereeBanners/RefereeBannerView.tsx` (the deferred MCP-014 render component ŌĆö a thin non-blocking strip). `src/features/arguments/SemanticOverrideChoiceSheet.tsx` (the deferred MCP-015 inline choice sheet ŌĆö three lane radios + an answers-parent checkbox + a confirm button, all copy from `gameCopy`).
- **What it ships ŌĆö modified files:** `src/features/semanticReferee/index.ts` + `src/features/refereeBanners/index.ts` re-export only the new pure modules (not the RN/edge-touching ones ŌĆö see the deviation note). `src/features/arguments/ArgumentGameSurface.tsx` gains 3 optional props (`refereeBanner` / `overridePrompt` / `onConfirmOverride`) and renders the banner strip + override sheet inline; absent props ŌåÆ byte-identical to the pre-MCP-019 render. `src/features/arguments/ArgumentTreeScreen.tsx` calls `useSemanticReferee` once at the room-shell level and fires `onMovePosted` only for a newly-arrived move authored by the current user (never on a first load, a draft edit, a node tap, or another participant's message).
- **Doctrine encoded:** the live `anthropic` provider is reached only after an operator flips a server secret ŌĆö never by this card. `{ enabled: false }` for any of the 9 reasons, an `ok:false` wrapper error, and a thrown rejection are ALL collapsed into one inert `'fallback'` state ŌĆö no toast, no error text, no `console.*`; the hook's public surface has **no error field**. `classifyMove` runs strictly *after* `submit-argument` posted the move ŌĆö the hook never gates the composer and score never blocks posting. A `classifyMove` call fires only behind MCP-012's cache + trigger gates; the per-`post_submit` set is Ōēż 2 calls of Ōēż 5 classifiers each. No banner shows a verdict / winner / truth / person-label string ŌĆö all copy is MCP-014's `REFEREE_BANNER_LIBRARY` / MCP-015's `PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY`, both already ban-list-tested. The override choice writes only an in-memory `SemanticOverrideRecord` (no `delta` / `score` / `penalty` / `block` / `flag` field) ŌĆö no scoring path, no `flags` row. No AI runs on the client ŌĆö the only outbound call is `classifyMove ŌåÆ invoke('semantic-referee')`; a source-scan asserts no new file imports a provider SDK. An observer is never offered the override sheet and never originates a classification.
- **Scope honesty:** MCP-019 wires the **packet ŌåÆ banner ŌåÆ override** path only. It does **not** wire the economy-driven `reconcileMove` ledger (Defect 1) ŌĆö `categoryReadings` is `[]` and the override sheet triggers via the `low_confidence` path only; the `l1_l2_conflict` path lights up automatically when the future economy-ledger card passes a real `LedgerResult` (the hook already threads `ledgerResult` through as `undefined`). The `SemanticOverrideRecord` is in-memory (META-001 in-memory-v1); persisting it is a later card.
- **One implementer deviation from the design's ┬¦5:** the room hook ships at `src/features/arguments/useSemanticReferee.ts`, NOT `src/features/semanticReferee/` ŌĆö the latter is a foundation layer and the existing `__tests__/refereeBannerForbiddenImports.test.ts` invariant forbids any `semanticReferee/` file from importing `refereeBanners/`. The hook is a room-layer module by nature (it consumes `refereeBanners` + `semanticOverride` + `edgeFunctions`), so it lives in `arguments/` ŌĆö the same directory the design itself chose for `SemanticOverrideChoiceSheet`. No behavior change. Full rationale in the "Implementer note" addendum at the bottom of `docs/designs/MCP-019.md`.
- **+179 tests / +8 suites.** Full suite **8836 tests / 317 suites passing** (from the 8657 / 309 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean. New suites: `clientRedaction.test.ts`, `semanticTriggerInput.test.ts`, `bannerSelectionInputFromPacket.test.ts`, `useSemanticReferee.test.ts`, `RefereeBannerView.test.tsx`, `SemanticOverrideChoiceSheet.test.tsx`, `semanticRoomForbiddenImports.test.ts`, `argumentGameSurfaceSemanticWiring.test.tsx`.
- **No operator step for MCP-019 itself** ŌĆö pure client code, no `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no dependency install. To *see* the mock referee banner in a real room the operator runs MCP-017's existing steps (`functions deploy semantic-referee` + `secrets set SEMANTIC_REFEREE_ENABLED=true`, provider stays `mock`); the live Anthropic provider needs the additional `secrets set SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER=anthropic`. MCP-019 ships dormant-but-wired.

## MCP-017 ŌĆö Anthropic live-provider pilot for the semantic-referee Edge Function (Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö un-stubs MCP-016's `anthropic` provider slot with a real, working **live Anthropic provider** for the `semantic-referee` Edge Function. The live provider is **opt-in** (`SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER=anthropic`); `mock` stays the default via the unchanged `?? 'mock'` fallback. This is the only MCP-001ŌĆ”MCP-017 card that calls a live AI provider; the call lives **only** in the Edge Function. **No migration, no `supabase/config.toml` change** (the `verify_jwt = true` block is already present). **No live Anthropic call was made by the implementer** ŌĆö every test mocks / source-scans; the first real call is the operator's after deploy + flag flip. No service-role, no direct insert into `public.arguments`, no new dependency, no `.env` touched. Issue #221.

- **What it ships ŌĆö new provider files** (`supabase/functions/_shared/semanticReferee/`): `anthropicClassifierCore.ts` (zod-free, Jest-importable core ŌĆö `buildAnthropicRequestBody`, `extractAnthropicContentText`, `parseJsonFromContent`, `sanitizeRawPayload` (retains exactly `{ model, stop_reason, usage }`), the Haiku-class `DEFAULT_SEMANTIC_REFEREE_MODEL = 'claude-haiku-4-5'`, the structural-only system prompt, and the `ProviderResult` / `ProviderUnavailableReason` types); `seedPrompt.ts` (zod-free ŌĆö `CLASSIFIER_QUESTION_TEXT` keyed by all 23 catalog-v0 ids, each a bounded structural yes/no question; `buildClassifierPrompt`; `SEED_PROMPT_VERSION`); `contentSafetyScan.ts` (zod-free Deno mirror of `semanticRefereeValidator.ts`'s content ban-lists ŌĆö `scanPacketContent` rejects a verdict / person / secret / PII token inside a contract-valid string and a smuggled off-contract key); `anthropicProvider.ts` (the Deno-only orchestrator and the **only** file that reads `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` via `Deno.env.get()` and `fetch`es `api.anthropic.com` ŌĆö every failure path returns a typed `unavailable` result, and even a successful response is re-validated through `SemanticRefereePacketSchema` + `scanPacketContent`); `providerRoutingCore.ts` (the zod-free routing switch extracted out of `providerRouting.ts` so the routing logic stays Jest-testable with injected spy deps).
- **What it ships ŌĆö modified files:** `providerRouting.ts` / `providers.ts` are now `async`; `DEFAULT_PROVIDER_DEPS` wires `runAnthropicClassifier`. `semantic-referee/index.ts` `await`s the now-async registry. `types.ts` + `src/lib/edgeFunctions.ts` widen `ClassifyMoveDisabledReason` with the six live-provider failure reasons (`key_missing` / `api_error` / `rate_limited` / `network_error` / `parse_failure` / `validation_failed`) ŌĆö Node + Deno twins in lockstep. `__tests__/_helpers/semanticRefereeDeno.ts` bridges the three new zod-free files and loads `classifyWithProvider` from `providerRoutingCore.ts`.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the live provider is **opt-in, never default** ŌĆö the `?? 'mock'` fallback is unchanged and the `semanticProviderRegistry.test.ts` "default is mock" assertion still passes. The provider **never throws to the client** ŌĆö every error path returns `{ enabled: false, reason }` with HTTP 200; the caller falls back to the deterministic layer-1 result. `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is read via `Deno.env.get()` in **exactly one file** (`anthropicProvider.ts`); it appears in no `src/` / `app/` executable code and is never logged. Every Anthropic response is re-validated through the outbound `.strict()` `SemanticRefereePacketSchema` **and** the Deno content-safety scanner ŌĆö a smuggled `block` field, `authoritative: true`, or a verdict token forces the deterministic fallback. The seed prompt asks for **structural** yes/no answers only ŌĆö no question asks the model for a verdict, a truth value, a winner, or a popularity reading; a ban-list test scans every question string. `authoritative` is hard-pinned to `false`. The MCP-016 deterministic mock + `validateOrFallback` registry-level wall are unchanged ŌĆö a misbehaving model cannot reach the user.
- **+136 tests / +6 suites.** Full suite **8657 tests / 309 suites passing** (from the 8521 / 303 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean. New suites: `semanticAnthropicCore.test.ts`, `semanticAnthropicContentScan.test.ts`, `semanticAnthropicContentScanParity.test.ts`, `semanticAnthropicSeedPromptBanList.test.ts`, `semanticAnthropicSourceScan.test.ts`, `semanticEdgeAuthAnthropic.test.ts`. `semanticNoLiveCall.test.ts` was renamed to `semanticNoLiveCallInRouter.test.ts` and re-scoped to the still-pure files (the now-live `anthropicProvider.ts` / router files are covered by the new source-scan suite); `semanticProviderRegistry.test.ts` / `semanticEdgeBoundary.test.ts` / `semanticForbiddenSecrets.test.ts` were retargeted for the async router + the documented key boundary.
- **Operator follow-up (deploy is a separate operator action ŌĆö full procedure in `docs/deployment/mcp-017-live-provider-runbook.md`):** `npx supabase functions deploy semantic-referee --linked` ships the live-provider code (still mock-behaving until the flag flips); confirm `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is present (reused from `process-language-draft`); optionally `npx supabase secrets set SEMANTIC_REFEREE_MODEL=claude-haiku-4-5`; `npx supabase secrets set SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER=anthropic` flips to live. Rollback is one line: `npx supabase secrets set SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER=mock`. No migration, no dependency install, no `.env` change.

## QOL-042 ŌĆö Linked prior argument reference as context (Epic ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö lets a new argument room **reference an earlier settled room** as context. The reference is a one-directional, immutable **link record** between two rooms (`public.argument_room_links`): the new room surfaces a context **chip** carrying the prior room's title; a private prior room's *content* opens only for a user authorized on the original room (an unauthorized viewer sees the **title only** ŌĆö never body, nodes, or evidence); the locked prior room is **never re-opened or mutated** by the link. **One new append-only migration** (write-only ŌĆö the operator applies it post-merge); **no Edge Function** ŌĆö RLS + two BEFORE triggers fully enforce the link rules. No service-role, no direct insert into `public.arguments`, no `submit-argument` change, no new dependency, no Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no `.env` touched. Issue #211.

- **What it ships ŌĆö migration (write-only):** `supabase/migrations/20260521000010_qol042_argument_room_links.sql` ŌĆö the `argument_room_links` table (`source_debate_id` ŌåÆ CASCADE, `target_debate_id` ŌåÆ RESTRICT, `created_by` ŌåÆ `public.profiles`, `target_title_snapshot text Ōēż200` for the title-only state, `note text Ōēż280`, `is_removed` soft-remove, `no_self_link` + `one_link_per_pair` constraints), RLS enabled with **exactly four ┬¦7 policies** (SELECT gated on source-room visibility; INSERT by a source-room participant as `created_by = auth.uid()`; UPDATE soft-remove by the link author or an admin) and **no DELETE policy**, two partial indexes on active rows (source + target), and two BEFORE triggers ŌĆö `link_target_must_be_locked` (the target must be a settled `locked` room the inserting user can read) and `link_columns_immutable` (only `is_removed` may change after insert).
- **What it ships ŌĆö pure models + API + UI:** New `src/features/arguments/crossRoom/` module ŌĆö `linkedPriorArgumentModel.ts` (`ArgumentRoomLink`, `LinkAccessState` `authorized` / `title_only` / `unavailable`, `buildLinkedPriorArgumentChip` producing the chip's three view states, `canCreateLink` true only for a `locked` target, `buildLinkedTangentContext` a pure formatter that keeps `archived_or_resolved` tangent nodes ŌĆö degrading to all tangent nodes when LIFE-001 stage data is absent, design ┬¦14 Q4); `linkedPriorArgumentCopy.ts` (every user-facing string, doctrine-ban-list held); `argumentRoomLinksApi.ts` (caller-scoped wrappers ŌĆö `listLinksForRoom`, `createArgumentRoomLink` with idempotent-duplicate handling, `removeArgumentRoomLink` soft-remove, `loadPriorRoomContext` deriving `LinkAccessState` from the RLS outcome); `LinkedPriorArgumentChipRow.tsx` (the timeline context-chip row ŌĆö a disabled "Open prior argument" action shows a visible reason + `accessibilityState` disabled). `ArgumentTimelineMap.tsx` gains an additive optional `linkedPriorChips` prop rendering the chip row in the timeline header above the rail; `oneBox/boxModel.ts` gains an additive optional `linkedPriorRoomId` on the `Draft` buffer (root_claim setup); `oneBox/inspectPopoutModel.ts` gains the additive `buildInspectLinkedPriorSection` ("From the linked prior argument" ŌĆö visible only when the chip is authorized; the fixed seven-section set is untouched). `src/lib/types.ts` re-exports `ArgumentRoomLink` as a cross-feature domain type.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the link is **context, never a verdict** ŌĆö no truth field, no score, no relationship-type enum; the chip never says the prior argument "won", "proved", or "was correct". The move counts on the chip are **activity** facts, never standing. The access check is **RLS-enforced server-side** ŌĆö a `title_only` viewer's prior-room body / nodes are gated by the existing `debates` / `arguments` RLS; the model only *renders* the `LinkAccessState` the API client derived. **Minimal disclosure** ŌĆö the single denormalized field is the prior room's *title* (Ōēż200 chars); no body, node text, evidence, or participant identity is ever copied onto the link. The locked prior room's immutability is **structurally enforced** ŌĆö QOL-042 has no code path that writes to `debates` or `arguments`; the `link_columns_immutable` trigger proves the link itself is immutable except for `is_removed`. **Soft-remove only** (no DELETE policy). Plain language ŌĆö no internal codes; "argument" not "debate", never "game"; "settled" the only end-state word; no "access denied" as an error. The pure models import no React / Supabase / network / AI and read no `Date.now()`.
- **QOL-039 soft dependency ŌĆö degraded path:** QOL-039 (public/private visibility) is **not built** ŌĆö `public.debates` has no `visibility` column. Per design ┬¦11 the ┬¦7 policies and the `link_target_must_be_locked` trigger use `is_debate_open_or_locked` + `is_debate_participant` + `is_moderator_or_admin` alone (today's behaviour ŌĆö every open/locked room is content-readable, so every link resolves to `authorized`); the `title_only` chip state is dead-but-harmless code, still written and tested. When QOL-039 lands a one-line follow-up migration swaps in the visibility-aware source-readability helper.
- **+137 tests / +7 suites.** Full suite **8521 tests / 303 suites passing** (from the 8384 / 296 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean. New suites: `linkedPriorArgumentModel.test.ts`, `linkedPriorArgumentCopy.test.ts`, `argumentRoomLinksApi.test.ts`, `qol042Migration.test.ts`, `oneBoxRootClaimLink.test.ts`, `inspectPopoutLinkedPrior.test.ts`, `qol042NoForbiddenImports.test.ts`.
- **Operator follow-up (deploy is a separate operator action):** `npx supabase db push --linked` to apply `20260521000010_qol042_argument_room_links.sql`; verify with `npx supabase db lint` + `npx supabase db status`. **No Edge Function deploy** ŌĆö QOL-042 adds none. No env var, no secret, no `.env` change, no dependency install. If QOL-039 ships *after* QOL-042, the operator also applies the one-line follow-up migration swapping the source-readability helper to the visibility-aware variant.

## QOL-032 ŌĆö Inspect popout (node & evidence detail) (Epic 8 ŌĆö Timeline Interaction Mechanics)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö the **Inspect popout**, the strictly read-only node / evidence / branch detail surface ("understand what is here") rendered through the QOL-030 flash-popout chassis. Inspect is the *understand* surface ŌĆö it never authors, posts, or edits anything; its single bridge is the ┬¦5 "Suggested next move" hand-off, which closes Inspect and opens the **Act popout** (QOL-031). QOL-032 converges SC-002 (timeline node popover) and SC-003 (sidecar) directly into the popout. **No migration, no Edge Function, no `supabase/` change** ŌĆö QOL-032 is UI-only client composition. No service-role, no direct insert, no new dependency, no Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no `.env` touched. Issue #201.

- **What it ships:** The production code shipped in the branch build commit (`ce802c4`): `src/features/arguments/oneBox/inspectPopoutModel.ts` ŌĆö the pure-TS content model. `buildInspectPopout(input)` produces the **fixed seven-section set** (design ┬¦3.2 ŌĆö ┬¦1 What this move says ┬Ę ┬¦2 Why it matters ┬Ę ┬¦3 What is unresolved ┬Ę ┬¦4 Where it sits ┬Ę ┬¦5 Suggested next move ┬Ę ┬¦6 Semantic flags ┬Ę ┬¦E Evidence detail) with the LIFE-001 **stage-driven emphasis** applied (design ┬¦3.3): the stage-emphasised section is pulled to slot 0 and expanded by default ŌĆö emphasis only **re-orders**, it never removes a section, so `sections.length` is always 7. Each section's body resolves to plain language; an absent input renders an explicit ┬¦7 "nothing here" fallback (`No evidence attached.` / `No semantic flags.`), never a blank section. The ┬¦5 hand-off carries one `ActEntryId` per stage; in an archived room the hand-off chip is disabled with the reason "This argument is settled." while Inspect itself stays fully functional. `InspectPopout.tsx` ŌĆö the render component on the shipped `Popout` / `PopoutGroup` / `PopoutEntry` chassis; it consumes `buildInspectPopout` unchanged and renders the collapsible section rows, the ┬¦5 hand-off chip, the optional settled banner, and a `ŌĆ╣ prev / next ŌĆ║` traversal row (wrap disabled at root / latest, consistent with IX-003). The QOL-030 chassis files and the sibling popouts (Act / Go) are untouched.
- **What this card finishes:** the design ┬¦8 test suite ŌĆö the build commit shipped the model + component but no tests. Two new suites cover ┬¦8 in full: `inspectPopoutModel.test.ts` (206 ŌĆö the fixed seven-section set always all-present; the ┬¦3.3 stage-emphasis table for every `PointLifecycleState` incl. the doctrine test that emphasis only re-orders and never removes a section; the ┬¦5 narrative-frame table S1 F3/F5/F10 + S2 F3/F5/F9; the ┬¦5 suggested-move `ActEntryId` per stage; the read-only contract ŌĆö the model exposes only sections + one hand-off descriptor + a banner flag; the ┬¦7 edge cases ŌĆö node with no evidence, no semantic flags, archived room; no raw `snake_case` / verdict copy in any rendered string; determinism + purity). `inspectPopoutComponent.test.tsx` (62 ŌĆö chassis use, the fixed section set rendered, the ┬¦3.3 emphasised section first + expanded, the read-only contract asserted at the render boundary, the ┬¦5 hand-off closes Inspect + opens Act, the ┬¦7 edge cases incl. own-node identical role-agnostic render and prev/next wrap-disabled, chassis a11y, the no-write doctrine + ban-list).
- **Doctrine encoded:** Inspect is **strictly read-only** ŌĆö `InspectPopout.tsx` imports no Supabase / network / AI / router primitive, renders no `<TextInput>` / `onChangeText`, takes no compose / submit / `onDirectAction` / `onRoleChange` prop; its single action is the ┬¦5 hand-off, which only **names** an `ActEntryId` for the host and closes Inspect. **Plain language only** ŌĆö every rendered string is plain English; no internal code / `snake_case` reaches a section title or body (RULE-001). **No verdict / winner / loser / true / false copy** ŌĆö ┬¦3 "What is unresolved" describes the *move*, never the person; the settled banner states the argument is "settled", never declares a result. **Read-only is universal** ŌĆö there is no own-node special case (unlike Act); the component carries no viewer-role branch. Deterministic pure projection over already-built models (META-001, LIFE-001, RULE-001/003, EV-001) ŌĆö `inspectPopoutModel.ts` re-derives none of them, holds no React / Supabase / network / AI import, and reads no `Date.now()`.
- **+268 tests / +2 suites.** Full suite **8384 tests / 296 suites passing** (from the 8116 / 294 baseline). Typecheck + lint clean. No production defect was found ŌĆö the build commit's `inspectPopoutModel.ts` / `InspectPopout.tsx` are unmodified by this card.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. QOL-032 is the last of the QOL-030 popout-expansion cards (Act / Inspect / Go) ŌĆö all three now build complete.

## QOL-031 ŌĆö Act popout (the flash menu) (Epic 8 ŌĆö Timeline Interaction Mechanics)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö the **Act popout**, the universal contextual action menu ("what can I do here") rendered through the QOL-030 flash-popout chassis. QOL-031 is the **render layer** for QOL-030's shipped `buildActPopout` 3-gate pure function ŌĆö it does **not** re-derive the model; it renders the model's output. **No migration, no Edge Function, no `supabase/` change** ŌĆö QOL-031 is UI-only client composition. No service-role, no direct insert, no new dependency, no Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no `.env` touched. Issue #200.

- **What it ships:** New `src/features/arguments/oneBox/ActPopout.tsx` ŌĆö the Act popout render component on the shipped `Popout` / `PopoutGroup` / `PopoutEntry` chassis (the sibling of QOL-033's `GoPopout.tsx`). It consumes the 3-gate `buildActPopout` output unchanged and renders it: the group order is fixed (`Respond ┬Ę Evidence ┬Ę Resolve ┬Ę Structure ┬Ę Direct ┬Ę Participation`, exactly as the model emits it); the ┬¦3.4 stage-promoted entry is visually emphasized via the chassis `isPromoted` styling (raised surface + heavier text + Ōśģ marker); a host-supplied `disabledEntries` map renders a model-surviving but contextually-unavailable entry **disabled with a one-line reason** ŌĆö never a silent omission (the ┬¦7 wireframe's "Flag ŌĆö disabled: can't flag your own"). Three entry kinds dispatch to host callbacks ŌĆö `box_opening` re-types the OneBox, `direct` fires an immediate action through existing Edge Functions / RLS, `role_change` changes the seat and re-opens the popout (┬¦3.2). The load-bearing render decision is extracted into the pure `buildActRenderGroups` helper so the repo's `.tsx` UI-test discipline can exercise it without a renderer. `OneBox.tsx` is rewired (minimal registration) to render `<ActPopout>` instead of its prior inline `Popout` + `PopoutGroup` block; the QOL-030 chassis files (`boxModel.ts`, `Popout.tsx`, `PopoutEntry.tsx`, `PopoutGroup.tsx`, `actPopoutModel.ts`) are untouched.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the stage gate **only orders** ŌĆö it never removes a valid entry; that is the model's job, the render layer renders the result and emphasizes the promoted entry, nothing more (a promoted entry that is also host-disabled drops the promotion ŌĆö a disabled row cannot be a suggested move). A **disabled entry always shows why** ŌĆö no silent omission (the engine + role gates inside `buildActPopout` *remove* invalid / forbidden entries; the render layer's `disabledEntries` map handles the narrower role-blocked-with-reason case the design ┬¦3.3 / ┬¦7 / ┬¦8 calls out). The convergence of SC-001 (side action rail) / SC-004 (timeline node dock) / RULE-005 (channel chip row) **reuses the shipped models** ŌĆö `ActPopout` calls `buildActPopout` and forks no gate (no `applyEngineGate` / `applyRoleGate` / `applyStageGate` re-implementation). Deterministic pure render projection ŌĆö `ActPopout.tsx` imports no Supabase / network / AI / router primitive, never writes to `public.arguments`, uses no service-role, reads no `Date.now()`; the direct entries that mutate (Flag, Make-private, governance) route through host callbacks to the existing Edge Functions / RLS. No verdict / winner / loser / true / false copy ŌĆö every entry label comes from `actPopoutModel` (already ban-list scanned); the one literal string `ActPopout` authors (the ┬¦8 zero-entry note) joins the shared `oneBoxCopyBanList` doctrine scan.
- **+75 tests / +1 suite.** Full suite **8116 tests / 294 suites passing** (from the 8041 / 293 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean. New suite: `actPopoutComponent.test.tsx` (69 ŌĆö chassis use, fixed group order, the ┬¦3.4 promoted-entry emphasis, disabled-entries-visible-with-a-reason, the entry-kind ŌåÆ chassis-kind mapping, the ┬¦6 narrative-frame table reproduced as 8 frames + the ┬¦8 edge cases, the ┬¦5 convergence, the no-write doctrine, the kind dispatch + OneBox registration, the doctrine ban-list, render-projection faithfulness). `oneBoxCopyBanList.test.ts` extended (+7) to scan the Act render layer's empty-state copy + an `ActPopout.tsx` import-purity scan.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. QOL-031 is the first of the QOL-030 popout-expansion cards; QOL-033 (Go) already shipped, QOL-032 (Inspect) remains.

## QOL-033 ŌĆö Go popout (navigate & re-view) (Epic 8 ŌĆö Timeline Interaction Mechanics)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö the **Go popout**, the navigate-and-re-view surface that plugs into the QOL-030 flash-popout chassis (the third popout beside Act / Inspect). Go moves the viewport and reconfigures the board's render mode ŌĆö it performs **no write and no content mutation**. **No migration, no Edge Function, no `supabase/` change** ŌĆö QOL-033 is UI-only client composition. No service-role, no direct insert, no new dependency, no Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no `.env` touched. Issue #202.

- **What it ships:** New `src/features/arguments/oneBox/goPopoutModel.ts` ŌĆö the pure-TS Go content model (the navigate-and-re-view twin of `actPopoutModel.ts`). `buildGoPopout(input)` produces the four design ┬¦3.2 control groups ŌĆö **Jump** (Root ┬Ę Latest ┬Ę Hot zone ┬Ę Branch list) ┬Ę **View** (Timeline Ōćä Cards) ┬Ę **Density** (Compact ┬Ę Normal ┬Ę Expanded) ┬Ę **Lens** (Active path ┬Ę Unresolved ┬Ę Evidence) ŌĆö with each entry's `isActive` + `isDisabled` + `disabledReason` resolved against the current view / density / lens and the IX-002 `timelineMiniMapModel`. New `src/features/arguments/oneBox/GoPopout.tsx` ŌĆö the render component on the shipped `Popout` / `PopoutGroup` / `PopoutEntry` chassis; it embeds the IX-002 `TimelineMiniMap` strip **read-only** (passes the already-built model straight through; below IX-002's node threshold the strip is omitted with a one-line note). The QOL-030 chassis files are untouched ŌĆö QOL-033 only *consumes* the chassis.
- **Doctrine encoded:** Go performs **no write, no content mutation** ŌĆö every entry only reconfigures the viewport or the render mode (`GoPopout.tsx` imports no Supabase / network / AI / router; a source-scan test proves it). A focus **lens dims, never hides** ŌĆö the lens entries only select a `GoLens`; the actual dimming is IX-001's `applyTimelineLens`, whose `LensEmphasis` has no `hidden` value, so a lens structurally cannot remove a node (a test verifies the ┬¦3.3 stage tables through `applyTimelineLens`: Unresolved ŌåÆ `needs_response`, Evidence ŌåÆ `evidence_requested`, Active path ŌåÆ IX-001's topology `activePathLens` helper; a zero-match lens leaves the board unfiltered). The **hot zone** is the IX-002 `findHotZone` longest warm/hot run ŌĆö an **activity** signal chosen by run length, never "hottest", never correctness; the Go model never re-derives it. Density / lens are **timeline-only** ŌĆö in Cards view every density + lens entry is disabled with a visible "Available in Timeline view" reason; the Branch-list entry disables with "No side branches yet" when no side branch exists. Deterministic pure projection ŌĆö `goPopoutModel.ts` holds no React / Supabase / network / AI import and no `Date.now()`. No verdict / winner / loser copy in any label ŌĆö the QOL-033 group headings, entry labels, accessibility labels and disabled reasons join the shared `oneBoxCopyBanList` doctrine scan.

## IX-001 ŌĆö Timeline density + focus lenses (Epic 8 ŌĆö Timeline Interaction Mechanics)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö the pure **density + lens core** consumed by the already-shipped Conversation Gallery (Epic 11) and the future QOL-033 in-room Go popout. **IX-001 ships NO screen** ŌĆö per design ┬¦0/┬¦1 it is the pure model plus a tiny session-state hook; the gallery screen and QOL-033 *render* it. No standalone IX-001 React shell was built (deliberate ŌĆö the design explicitly honours "build the pure model, not a standalone IX-001 shell"). **No migration, no `supabase/` change, no Edge Function, no new dependency.** No Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no service-role, no `.env` touched. Issue #20.

- **What it ships:** New pure-TS model `src/features/arguments/timelineDensityLensModel.ts` (no React, no Supabase, no network, no AI, no `Date.now()` ŌĆö recency uses an injected `ctx.nowMs`). Density: `GalleryDensityMode` is a **strict superset** of VG-004's shipped 3-mode `TimelineDensityMode` ŌĆö `expanded` / `normal` / `compact` map 1:1 by the same name, plus a 4th *gallery-only* `scan` tier; `TimelineDensityMode` is **not forked** and gains no 4th value. `toTimelineDensityMode` clamps `scan ŌåÆ compact` so an in-room node never renders tighter than 28px (hit targets stay Ōēź44px). `GALLERY_DENSITY_SPECS` is a descriptive per-mode card spec (excerpt line clamps, which optional regions render); `scan` hides only *optional* regions (mini-timeline, stats row), never data. Lenses: 11 named `FocusLensId` values plus the `none` baseline; `GALLERY_LENS_PREDICATES` (each a deterministic boolean over a built `ConversationGalleryCard`, every lifecycle-driven predicate carrying a pre-LIFE-001 fallback to always-present fields) and `TIMELINE_LENS_PREDICATES` (the 7-lens node subset over `ArgumentTimelineMapNode`, with the gallery-only room-level lenses absent from `TIMELINE_LENS_IDS`); `activePathLens` is the separate topology helper. `applyGalleryLens` / `applyTimelineLens` tag every item `bright | dimmed` and never change list length; a zero-match lens forces every item back to `bright` with `isEmpty: true`. `GallerySortAxis` (the 3 coarse axes) maps to the shipped `ConversationSortMode` via `toConversationSortMode`. `DensityLensViewConfig` + `applyViewConfigChange` encode the page-reset rules (search/sort reset the page; density/lens do not). New `src/features/arguments/useDensityLens.ts` ŌĆö a thin session-state hook holding one `DensityLensViewConfig`; the **only** IX-001 file importing React. Both re-exported additively from `src/features/arguments/index.ts`.
- **Doctrine encoded:** a density mode and a focus lens are **view state only** ŌĆö neither is ever an input to the Constitution engine, `argumentScoreModel`, `antiAmplification`, or any validation gate. A focus lens **dims, never deletes** ŌĆö `LensEmphasis` has no `hidden` value, so a lens structurally cannot remove an item from the data set; a dimmed item stays a full, navigable control. Heat/density are **activity** signals, never verdicts ŌĆö `heating_up` / `hot` read `ConversationGalleryCard.heatLevel` (whose source is already "active friction, not popular") and the lens copy says so out loud ("activity, not a result" / "momentum, not a result"). No authored string contains a verdict or popularity token ŌĆö a ban-list test scans every `FOCUS_LENS_COPY` string against the repo's canonical `_forbiddenLifecycleTokens`; no internal snake_case code reaches user-facing copy. The model file holds no popularity-shaped identifier and the constitution engine is untouched.
- **+129 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite **7690 tests / 286 suites passing** (from the 7561 / 282 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate + terminology-audit clean. New suites: `timelineDensityLensModel.test.ts` (the 4 density modes + spec object, all 11 gallery lens predicates incl. the lifecycle-loaded and lifecycle-absent fallback branch of every lifecycle-driven predicate, the 7 timeline lens predicates, `applyGalleryLens`/`applyTimelineLens` invariants, the sort + density converters, `applyViewConfigChange` reset rules, determinism, the documented one-card-per-conversation dedupe rule), `timelineDensityLensNoVerdict.test.ts` (the doctrine ban-list + heat-is-activity disclaimers + no popularity identifier), `timelineDensityLensForbiddenImports.test.ts` (source scan: model is pure, imports type-only, `TimelineDensityMode` still has exactly 3 members), `useDensityLens.test.ts` (hook contract via its pure delegate logic + a structural source scan).
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. **Blocks QOL-033** (the Go popout renders this model's density modes + `TIMELINE_LENS_IDS`). The Conversation Gallery screen does not yet *consume* the model ŌĆö wiring the Density + Lens controls into `ConversationGalleryScreen` is a follow-up surface task (design ┬¦9.2); IX-001's deliverable is the pure core, which is consumable today.

## QOL-037 ŌĆö Evidence applicability dispute flow (Epic 6 ŌĆö Evidence)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö adds the **evidence applicability axis**: a structured way to dispute *what* a piece of evidence applies to (which month a payment covers, which obligation a receipt settles), separate from disputing that the evidence exists (EV-001 `SourceChainStatus`) or that a source/quote was *asked for* (EV-003 evidence debt). QOL-037 ships the behaviour spec for the QOL-030 `respond_to_evidence` box type ŌĆö it produces **no standalone surface**; it is content plugged into QOL-030's `renderSchema` and read by the QOL-032 Inspect popout. Render-time-derived: **no migration, no `evidence_applicability` table, no new RLS policy**. The one Edge Function touch is a **minimal advisory pass-through** in `submit-argument` (┬¦7.4 of the design). No Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no service-role, no direct `public.arguments` insert, no `.env` touched, no dependency install. Issue #206.

- **What it ships:** New pure-TS model `src/features/evidence/evidenceApplicabilityModel.ts` ŌĆö `EvidenceResponseChoice` (the closed seven-choice set: `accept` / `accept_with_caveat` / `dispute_date` / `dispute_amount` / `dispute_applicability` / `request_source` / `request_clarification`), `ApplicabilityStatus` (the three-rung axis: `applicability_undisputed` / `applicability_disputed` / `applicability_supported`), the `EvidenceResponseRecord` advisory block, the frozen `EVIDENCE_RESPONSE_CHOICES` descriptor table + `ALL_EVIDENCE_RESPONSE_CHOICES` / `ALL_APPLICABILITY_STATUSES`, `MIN_CLARIFICATION_CHARS = 12`. Five public functions: `validateEvidenceResponseDraft` (the non-`accept` ŌåÆ clarification-required validation rule), `deriveApplicabilityStatus` (the render-time status derivation from the chronological response history), `previewApplicabilityTransition` (the box preview line), `summarizeApplicabilityChip` (the plain-language chip contract), `buildRespondToEvidenceViewModel` (the full box view-model incl. the QOL-032 ┬¦E claimed-vs-disputed read fields). New `evidenceApplicabilityCopy.ts` ŌĆö every choice label/helper, both applicability chip labels/helpers, both disabled-Post reasons, the preview-line and read-view strings, all frozen, with `ALL_EVIDENCE_APPLICABILITY_STRINGS` so the ban-list test scans the whole surface. New RN components `RespondToEvidenceForm.tsx` (the seven-choice radio set + conditional required-clarification field + status-preview line + own-evidence / observer role gates; plugs into QOL-030's `renderSchema('respond_to_evidence', ŌĆ”)`) and `ApplicabilityChip.tsx` (the applicability-axis status chip ŌĆö text label + tone token, self-hides when `applicability_undisputed`; renders alongside the EV-002 receipt chip so both axes show at once). Barrel `src/features/evidence/index.ts` additively re-exports the model + copy + components. `MoveDraftPatch` (`src/features/arguments/conversationMoves.ts`) gains an optional `evidenceResponse?: MoveEvidenceResponse` field ŌĆö optional, so all existing callers are unaffected.
- **Doctrine encoded:** an applicability dispute changes a **status, never a verdict** ŌĆö `dispute_applicability` flips `applicability_undisputed ŌåÆ applicability_disputed`; the model has deliberately **no** "applicability proven / disproven / true / false" value (no truth-negative state by design). Copy is "Applicability disputed" / "Applicability supported", never "proof" / "true" / "false" / "winner" / "loser" / "verdict" / "case closed" ŌĆö a ban-list test scans every QOL-037 system-generated string for the verdict + amplification + person-attribution token lists and the `looksLikeInternalCode` snake_case predicate. The three axes never collapse: existence/source-chain (EV-001), obligation/debt (EV-003), and applicability (QOL-037) are computed independently and never read each other ŌĆö a test asserts `dispute_date` / `dispute_amount` / `accept_with_caveat` / `request_source` / `request_clarification` never touch `ApplicabilityStatus`. `applicability_supported` is reachable **only** via corroborating *moves* (an `accept` of the contested point by the disputing party, or an explicit `corroboratedByArgumentIds` move id) ŌĆö never via heat, replies, views, or popularity (anti-amplification). The clarification-required rule is a **validation** gate (it may disable Post, always with a visible plain-language reason ŌĆö no silent no-op); it is not a score gate, and score never blocks. The model is pure TS ŌĆö no React, no Supabase, no network, no AI, no `Date.now()`. The constitution engine is untouched; the seven choices route to existing argument types and QOL-037 adds **no new Constitution transition**.
- **The one Edge Function change ŌĆö minimal and advisory:** `supabase/functions/submit-argument/index.ts` accepts an optional `evidence_response` block on the request body and copies it **verbatim** into the `server_validation` JSONB snapshot it already writes (`supabase/functions/_shared/validationSchemas.ts` gains a permissive optional `EvidenceResponseSchema`). The function does **not** validate it, does **not** hard-block on it, does **not** branch the insert path on it ŌĆö a malformed block can never block a post; the existing body validation is the only gate, unchanged. This keeps the applicability axis render-time-derivable: the client reads `evidenceResponse` blocks off the argument rows it already fetches and runs `deriveApplicabilityStatus`. No new RLS, no migration, no service-role, no new insert path.
- **+174 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite **7561 tests / 282 suites passing** (from the 7387 / 278 baseline). Typecheck + lint + skills:validate + terminology-audit clean (audit: 0 live prohibited). New suites: `evidenceApplicabilityModel.test.ts` (full line + branch coverage ŌĆö choice-set shape, the validation rule, the derivation table incl. order-independence and the unknown-choice degradation, the transition preview, the chip contract, the view-model, the verdict / amplification / snake_case ban-lists), `RespondToEvidenceForm.test.tsx` (radio selection, clarification show/hide, Post disabled-with-reason, draft-buffer preservation, own-evidence + observer gates, accessibility, rendered-text ban-list), `ApplicabilityChip.test.tsx` (per-status render, hidden-when-undisputed, color-independence, ban-list), `submitArgumentEvidenceResponse.test.ts` (the advisory pass-through contract ŌĆö block copied verbatim, never a hard block). Integration touch in `conversationMoves.test.ts` (the new optional `evidenceResponse` field leaves existing patch behaviour unchanged).
- **Operator follow-up (out of scope for this card ŌĆö deploy is a separate operator action):** `npx supabase functions deploy submit-argument --linked` so the function knows to pass the new optional `evidence_response` field through into the validation snapshot. The deploy is **backward-compatible** ŌĆö the field is optional, so an older client that omits it is unaffected. Until the deploy lands, the box still works (the move body posts) but the applicability status would not persist for other viewers. **No migration**, no new RLS policy, no new Edge Function directory, no env var, no `.env` change, no dependency install. QOL-030 (`respond_to_evidence` box chassis) and QOL-036 (`claimedApplicability` metadata) are upstream cards: per design ┬¦11 the form degrades gracefully where they are not yet built ŌĆö `claimedApplicability` renders "Not specified" and `request_source` still posts as an ordinary clarification when EV-003 debt tracking is absent.

## QOL-036 ŌĆö Payment / screenshot evidence metadata object (Epic 6 ŌĆö Evidence)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö an **additive extension** of the EV-001 `EvidenceArtifact` so a payment / transfer screenshot can be attached as a *structured* object (amount, date, redacted payer/payee, note, claimed applicability, a `confidence` pinned to `user_asserted`) instead of being pasted as un-disputable free text into the argument body. **Adapter-only**, per EV-001's path (b): **no migration, no `argument_evidence_artifacts` table, no Edge Function, no `submit-argument` change, no RLS change**. No Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no Supabase write, no service-role, no `.env` touched, no dependency install. Issue #205.

- **What it ships:** Extends the pure-TS model `src/features/evidence/evidenceModel.ts` ŌĆö appends `payment_screenshot` (the seventh `EvidenceArtifactKind`), the `EvidenceConfidence` type (one value, `user_asserted`) + `ALL_EVIDENCE_CONFIDENCES` + `PINNED_PAYMENT_CONFIDENCE`, the sub-shapes `EvidenceAmount` / `PaymentParty` / `ClaimedApplicability`, the optional `PaymentEvidenceMetadata` sub-object on `EvidenceArtifact` (every field optional except the pinned `confidence`), and the optional `payment` field on `EvidenceAttachmentInput`. New helpers: `detectRawAccountData` (conservative 12ŌĆō19 digit-run / IBAN-shape / routing-shape heuristic), `findRawAccountDataFields` (throw-free guard returning offending dotted field paths), `redactPaymentParty` (masks account-data runs to `ŌĆóŌĆóŌĆóŌĆó ` + last 4; role-only inputs pass through), `getPaymentEvidenceLabel` ("Payment record"), `summarizePaymentEvidence` (one-line redaction-safe summary). `classifyEvidenceKind` gains the payment branch (an explicit `kind` still wins); `isAttachmentEmpty` now counts `payment` as a fourth non-empty field; `buildEvidenceArtifacts` runs the redaction guard (raw account data ŌåÆ strip the `payment` sub-object + downgrade kind to `screenshot_redacted`), pins `confidence` to `user_asserted`, normalises the amount (negative ŌåÆ 0, NaN ŌåÆ absent), and clamps every text field. Barrel `src/features/evidence/index.ts` additively re-exports the new types + helpers.
- **Doctrine encoded:** a payment object is **inert** ŌĆö it carries no truth value and emits **no** `PointStandingDelta` (`evidenceModel.ts` imports nothing from `src/features/pointStanding/` ŌĆö a forbidden-imports test proves it). Existence ŌēĀ applicability: `amount` / `paidAt` / `noteText` / `claimedApplicability` are separate axes so a QOL-037 dispute can target one precisely; QOL-036 stores only the *claimed* side. `confidence` is pinned to `user_asserted` and the interface carries no `verified` / `confirmed` / `proven` / `valid` / `isTrue` / `truthValue` field (structural test). **No raw financial account data ŌĆö ever:** the adapter rejects (strips, never masks-and-stores) a `payment` object whose fields carry a card / account / routing / IBAN digit shape; a `JSON.stringify` digit-run scan proves no 12+ digit run survives a degraded artifact. A payment artifact runs the existing EV-001 source-chain table over `(url, sourceText, quote)` only ŌĆö alone it yields `unverified`, never auto-promoting to `source_and_quote` / `primary_present`. The change is strictly additive ŌĆö every existing `EvidenceArtifact` field keeps its name/type, and EV-002 / EV-003 / EV-005 / `ReceiptChip` / the timeline contract compile and behave identically (the one existing test that asserted "exactly six kinds" is updated to "exactly seven" ŌĆö the unavoidable enum-extension test-update the design's ┬¦11 calls for). All QOL-036 system-generated strings are plain English, ban-list-asserted (no `proof` / `true` / `winner` / `case closed`, no amplification or person-attribution token). Pure TS ŌĆö no React, no Supabase, no network, no `Date.now()` / `new Date()`.
- **+98 tests / +1 suite.** Full suite **7387 tests / 278 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate + terminology-audit clean (audit: 0 live prohibited). New suite `paymentEvidenceMetadata.test.ts` (full line + branch coverage ŌĆö type/enum coverage, `classifyEvidenceKind` payment branch, the adapter payment path, the redaction guard, redaction degradation, `redactPaymentParty`, amount normalisation, field clamping, `summarizePaymentEvidence` / `getPaymentEvidenceLabel`, receipt-chip + timeline integration, the no-truth / no-standing doctrine anchors, the ban-list, source purity). One existing test updated in `evidenceModel.test.ts` (six ŌåÆ seven kinds).
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. Downstream wiring (threading the `payment` object into the `submit-argument` request) is owned by the QOL-030 `add_evidence` box submit path or the EV-001 path-(c) persistence card ŌĆö QOL-036 is consumable as a pure model today.

## EV-003 ŌĆö Evidence debt tracker (Epic 6 ŌĆö Evidence)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö adds the **obligation axis** of the evidence model. EV-001 modelled the evidence *artifact* (existence / source-chain) and EV-002 gave it an inspection surface + a way to *ask*; EV-003 closes the ask loop by tracking whether a source / quote / receipt / context request was ever answered. Render-time-derived: **no migration, no `evidence_debt` table, no Edge Function, no `submit-argument` change**. No Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / X API call, no Supabase write, no service-role. Issue #16.

- **What it ships:** New pure-TS model `src/features/evidence/evidenceDebtModel.ts` ŌĆö `EvidenceDebt` (a structural obligation record), `EvidenceDebtKind` (5: `source` / `quote` / `receipt` / `context` / `primary_record`), `EvidenceDebtStatus` (8: `requested` / `supplied` / `challenged` / `accepted_by_participant` / `accepted_by_both` / `unresolved` / `stale` / `branched`), the per-node + per-room roll-up types, the `EvidenceDebtChipContract`. `deriveEvidenceDebts` derives every debt in a room from its argument rows (recognised request tag ŌåÆ opens a debt; later moves in the requested subtree resolve / challenge / branch / decline it; the close-condition table reads EV-001's `sourceChainStatus` only as a kind-named threshold; a still-`requested` debt past `STALE_DEBT_THRESHOLD_DAYS`=7 goes `stale`). `getNodeEvidenceDebtSummary` / `getRoomEvidenceDebtSummary` / `summarizeEvidenceDebtChip` / `getNodeEvidenceDebtChip` are pure roll-ups. New RN component `src/features/evidence/EvidenceDebtChip.tsx` ŌĆö the obligation-axis status chip, rendered on the timeline node beside the EV-002 receipt chip (a node can show both axes at once); non-pressable, self-hides on a node with no debt. Wiring: `timelineNodePopoverModel` + `TimelineNodePopover` render the chip; `ArgumentGameSurface` derives the room debts once per render (reusing the EV-002 artifact map + tag map ŌĆö no new fetch) and threads a per-node summary into the popover via a new `evidenceDebtSummaryFor` prop on `ArgumentTimelineMap`; the conversation gallery card gains an `evidenceDebtSummary`, an open debt is the authoritative `source_chain_fight` signal, and "Evidence requested" / "Source still owed" card signals appear.
- **Doctrine encoded:** an evidence debt is a **structural obligation marker**, never a verdict ŌĆö an open debt means "this point lacks X", never "this point is wrong"; a resolved debt is "settled", never "proven" / "case closed". The model is **advisory**: it imports nothing from `src/features/pointStanding/` (emits no `PointStandingDelta`) and nothing from the constitution validator (never enters `evaluateArgumentDraft`, never a flag, never disables Post ŌĆö a node with five open debts is just as postable-onto as one with none). It reads no heat / engagement / view / follower field ŌĆö a debt's status is a pure function of *moves*. Pure TS ŌĆö no React, no Supabase, no network, no `Date.now()` (the staleness clock is injected). The gallery precision fix: a room whose `source_request` debts all resolved is kept *out* of the source-trail lane (a tag count alone could not tell open from resolved). All chip / status-line copy is plain English, ban-list-asserted (no `proof` / `true` / `winner` / `case closed` / amplification / person-attribution tokens; `settled` is used at discharge).
- **+142 tests / +2 suites.** Full suite **7289 tests / 277 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + terminology-audit clean (audit: 0 live prohibited). New suites: `evidenceDebtModel.test.ts` (full line + branch coverage ŌĆö derivation, resolution scan per kind, staleness, roll-ups, chip copy, worst-status ordering, graceful degradation, doctrine anchors, ban-list), `EvidenceDebtChip.test.tsx` (pure-helper + source-scan). Integration touches in `timelineNodePopoverModel.test.ts`, `argumentGameSurface.test.ts`, `conversationGalleryModel.test.ts`.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install.

No test asserted any of the three strings; the `debates` table is **not** renamed.
