## IX-002 ŌĆö Timeline mini-map overview (Epic 8 ŌĆö Timeline Interaction Mechanics)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö adds a **mini-map overview rail** to `ArgumentTimelineMap`: a tiny, fixed-width strip that renders the whole conversation at a glance with a draggable / tappable viewport-window indicator plus jump-to affordances (Root ┬Ę Latest ┬Ę Hot zone ┬Ę one chip per side branch). For long debates the main timeline becomes a very wide horizontal scroll surface where the big picture is lost; the mini-map restores it. Tapping a mini-map region or chip pans / focuses the main map with **no route transition**. Issue #21.

- **What it ships:** New pure-TS model `src/features/arguments/timelineMiniMapModel.ts` ŌĆö a deterministic projection of the already-built `ArgumentTimelineMapModel` into a `TimelineMiniMapModel` (markers, branch clusters, hot zone, viewport window, summary line). Exports `buildTimelineMiniMapModel`, `buildViewportWindow`, `mapTemperatureToHeatTier`, `findHotZone`, `buildBranchClusters`, `resolveRegionJumpTarget`, `buildMiniMapSummaryLine` + layout constants. New thin RN component `src/features/arguments/TimelineMiniMap.tsx` ŌĆö RN primitives only (`View` / `Pressable` / `Text` / `PanResponder` from RN core), collapsed-by-default header chip, the mini rail with one marker per move, the viewport-window overlay, the jump-chip row, the summary line; every visual decision is an exported pure helper. `ArgumentTimelineMap.tsx` renders `<TimelineMiniMap>` as internal additive chrome under the controls row ŌĆö no new prop crosses the component boundary, so the room shell needs zero changes. Barrel `src/features/arguments/index.ts` additively re-exports the component + model symbols.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the mini-map is a **projection** ŌĆö it NEVER re-derives heat or branch logic. It re-labels the existing `temperatureBand` into a 4-tier `MiniMapHeatTier` (`quiet`/`mild`/`warm`/`hot`) and reads `branchId` / `branchRootMessageId` / `lane` verbatim. Heat is an **activity** signal, never a verdict: the hot zone is the *longest* warm/hot run, chosen by length, never by "hottest"; heat drives only a marker ring + a faint band and never feeds branch clustering or jump-target selection; the whole-mini-map a11y label explicitly says heat is "recent activity, not a result". A `pretty_wrong` move can show a `hot` ring ŌĆö proven by test ŌĆö and no standing band leaks into any mini-map field (the model never reads `standingBand`). All x-coordinates are normalized fractions in [0,1] so the mini-map is invariant to the main map's density (IX-001-proof). Mobile non-crowding: the mini-map renders nothing below a 12-move threshold and is collapsed by default above it. Visual grammar per timeline-grammar ŌĆö root = notch, latest = size+border, junction = hollow ring, active = size+border, heat = ring, branch cluster = band ŌĆö every signal survives grayscale. Every `Pressable` meets the 44px target via `hitSlop` and exposes role + label + state; the viewport window is `adjustable` with increment/decrement actions for keyboard scrubbing; reduce-motion snaps the expand transition + the scroll. Pure TS ŌĆö no React in the model, no Supabase, no network, no AI, no migration, no Edge Function.
- **+130 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite **7091 tests / 273 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install.

## GAME-003 ŌĆö Argument mode setup for 1v1 PvP (design + 4 templates) (Epic 12 ŌĆö Evidence-Enhanced Game Rules)

**Status:** Build complete (Part A), awaiting Review ŌĆö introduces **argument modes**, a consented, visible strictness profile both parties choose at room setup before a 1v1 PvP argument becomes interactive. A mode bundles a small set of room-rule fields (tone / evidence strictness, GAME-002 turn pacing, allowed informality, branch encouragement, source-request centrality, synthesis expectation, permanent-record warning, semantic-classification level, cooldown, observer access, invite-only) plus an optional plain-language disclaimer. Modes change **friction, never truth** ŌĆö no mode declares a winner/loser and no mode field can block a post. Part A (this card) ships the pure-TS model + 4 MVP templates + 9 design-only stubs + copy block + 3 test files; the mode setup screen is the named follow-up card **GAME-003B**. Issue #119.

- **What it ships:** New pure-TS model `src/features/modes/argumentModeModel.ts` ŌĆö the 13-mode `ArgumentMode` enum (`ALL_ARGUMENT_MODES` / `MVP_ARGUMENT_MODES` / `DESIGN_ONLY_ARGUMENT_MODES` / `DEFAULT_ARGUMENT_MODE`), the canonical `SemanticClassificationMode` (`off` / `metadata_only` / `metadata_and_chip`; default `off` ŌĆö fail-closed, consistent with MCP-012ŌĆ”MCP-016), the `ArgumentModeDefinition` per-mode field record, the `ArgumentModeTemplate` wrapper (`status` + `sensitive` + fully-typed `definition`), `ModeRuleRow`, the frozen 13-entry `ARGUMENT_MODE_TEMPLATES` registry, and the accessors `argumentModeTemplate` / `argumentModeDefinition` / `isShippedMode` / `isSensitiveMode` / `coerceArgumentMode` / `argumentModeDisplayName` / `argumentModeDescription` / `buildModeRuleRows` / `reviewModeForArgumentMode` / `_forbiddenArgumentModeTokens`. The 4 MVP modes (`casual_disagreement`, `court_record_strict`, `internet_fact_check`, `debate_club`) ship `status: 'shipped'`; the other 9 ship `status: 'design_only'` with complete, doctrine-justified definitions (design-only = not-yet-selectable, never "fields missing"). New `ARGUMENT_MODE_COPY` block in `gameCopy.ts` (display names, descriptions, plain-language rule rows, the 2 design-only sensitive disclaimers, setup-screen helpers), registered in `ALL_COPY`. Barrel re-exports added to `src/features/modes/index.ts`.
- **Doctrine encoded:** every mode's `pacing` is built via GAME-002's `createPacingRule(...)` ŌĆö never an object literal ŌĆö so clamping/freezing stays centralized; `cooldownEnabled` and `permanentRecordWarning` are derived from the constructed pacing rule so the two-place copies cannot drift (invariant-tested for all 13 modes). No mode field, no copy string, no helper produces a winner/loser/true/false/correct ŌĆö `argumentModeBanList.test.ts` scans every user-facing string (display names, descriptions, rule rows, disclaimers, every `ARGUMENT_MODE_COPY` value) for the verdict / amplification / block / person-attribution ban-list and asserts no raw mode-id or internal enum value leaks into UI copy. No GAME-003 export turns a mode field into a blocking result ŌĆö modes change friction, never permission to post. The 2 sensitive modes (`co_parenting_custody`, `relationship_repair`) carry plain-language disclaimers that state the app gives **no** legal / therapy advice and contain no advice themselves (`argumentModeNoLegalAdvice.test.ts`). `semanticClassification` defaults to `off` for low-stakes / sensitive modes. Pure TS ŌĆö no React, no Supabase, no network, no AI call, no migration.
- **+60 tests / +3 suites.** Full suite **6961 tests / 269 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure-TS model + copy block + 3 tests. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. Part B (`GAME-003B` ŌĆö the mode setup screen) and a later mode-persistence card (`debates.mode` column + RLS) are named follow-ups; the 2 sensitive-mode disclaimers are committed as design-only copy and need operator copy review only when a later card promotes those modes to live.

## EV-005 ŌĆö Evidence-to-evidence interaction (annotations on evidence) (Epic 6 ŌĆö Evidence)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö makes evidence a first-class object that can be *responded to with more evidence or context*, never with a truth verdict on the original author. Adds a thin annotation layer on top of the EV-001 `EvidenceArtifact`: a participant or admin attaches a small, source-descriptive note (`primary_source`, `retraction_attached`, `paywalled_source`, ŌĆ”), the model derives a status chip, the EV-002 `SourceChainPopover` surfaces the annotation stream + an interactive "Add an annotation" picker, and a new `annotate-evidence` Edge Function persists the add into the existing `client_validation` jsonb. **No DB migration** (V1 persists inside the existing jsonb; the `evidence_annotations` table is explicit V2). Issue #120.

- **What it ships:** Pure-TS model (append to `src/features/evidence/evidenceModel.ts`) ŌĆö the 18-kind `EvidenceAnnotationKind` enum (every value source/record-descriptive, never accusatory), the `EvidenceAnnotation` record, the plain-language label/helper map, `buildEvidenceAnnotation` / `buildEvidenceAnnotations`, `summariseAnnotations` (derived `EvidenceAnnotationStatusChip` with deterministic priority `conflict_open > context_open > broken > paywalled > anchored > unknown`), `enforceAnnotationDepthCap` (one-level nesting cap ŌåÆ "Summarise this evidence thread" synthesis prompt), the actor-eligibility table + `isAnnotationAllowed` + `eligibleAnnotationKinds`, and the `_forbiddenAnnotationTokens` ban-list seam. New `EvidenceAnnotationChip.tsx` (chip + read-only `EvidenceAnnotationStream`), `AddAnnotationSheet.tsx` (the interactive picker ŌĆö a `Modal` bottom-sheet from RN primitives only, 18/3 eligibility-gated radio options, Ōēż140-char note field with the hint "Describe the source, not the person."), `evidenceAnnotationApi.ts` (`addEvidenceAnnotation` write-path wrapper + `evidenceAnnotationsFromMeta` read adapter). New Edge Function `supabase/functions/annotate-evidence/index.ts` (`apply-manual-tag` shape: JWT-verified, caller-scoped eligibility check, service-role read-modify-write that spread-merges `evidenceAnnotations` into the existing `client_validation` jsonb ŌĆö no schema change) + the Deno mirror `supabase/functions/_shared/evidenceAnnotationEligibility.ts` + the additive `[functions.annotate-evidence]` `config.toml` block. EV-002 `SourceChainPopover` + `sourceChainPopoverModel` + `TimelineNodePopover` extended with additive optional annotation props; the annotation count reflects into the shared `ReceiptChip` contract so it surfaces in Cards + Timeline with no new component.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the 18 annotation tags are source/record-descriptive only ŌĆö no person-attribution (`misreporting_alleged` renders as "An alternate account exists"), no verdict/winner/truth token in any label or copy (`evidenceAnnotationBanList.test.ts` scans all 18 labels + 18 helpers + 6 status labels + 6 status helpers + the synthesis prompt + the picker copy against verdict / amplification / person-attribution lists). An annotation never converts popularity into factual standing and has no path to a `PointStandingDelta` ŌĆö `summariseAnnotations` reads only the annotation set, and the forbidden-imports test proves `evidenceModel.ts` imports nothing from `pointStanding` / `antiAmplification`. An annotation never blocks an ordinary post; no AI authors one (the constructor + Edge Function require an explicit human `addedByUserId`). The depth cap is proven by `evidenceAnnotationDepthCap.test.ts` (depth-0 accept, depth-1-with-resolving-parent accept + synthesis prompt, depth-2 / orphan / depth-1-on-depth-1 suppress). No service-role in client; the Edge Function is JWT-verified and caller-scoped; no migration; no new dependency; RN primitives only.
- **+168 tests / +7 suites.** Full suite **6901 tests / 266 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **Operator follow-up (out of scope for this card ŌĆö deploy is a separate operator action):** `npx supabase functions deploy annotate-evidence --linked` to deploy the new Edge Function. **No DB migration** (V1 persists into the existing `client_validation` jsonb). No new env var, no secret change ŌĆö `annotate-evidence` reuses the same `SUPABASE_URL` / `SUPABASE_ANON_KEY` / `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` Edge-Function secrets `apply-manual-tag` already relies on. Until the function is deployed, the "Add an annotation" flow surfaces a graceful `submitError`; the rest of EV-005 (model, chips, reading pre-existing annotations) works without it. No dependency install.

## BRAND-002 ŌĆö App-wide dark surface cohesion pass (UI/UX Behavior Repair Wave / Branding)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö a visual-only pass that extends `src/lib/designTokens.ts` with a reusable dark surface-token scale (`SURFACE_TOKENS`) and a control/button intent set (`CONTROL`), then replaces every raw light hex literal across 18 screen/component files (Account, Auth, Invite, the Admin screen + 9 tabs/panels, the 5 composer files) with a token reference so switching tabs no longer flashes from a dark game-board to a white form. No logic, copy, action, dependency, migration, or operator step. Issue #138.

- **What it ships:** `SURFACE_TOKENS` (14 keys ŌĆö `base`/`elevated`/`overlay`/`raised` backgrounds, `border`/`divider` hairlines, `textPrimary`/`textSecondary`/`textMuted`/`textInverse`, `inputBg`/`inputBorder`/`placeholder`, `focusRing`), `CONTROL` (`primary`/`secondary`/`danger`), both wired into the `TOKENS` aggregate and `getToken`. 18 converted files have zero raw light hex. New suite `__tests__/darkSurfaceTokens.test.ts` pins the token shape, the contrast pairs, the no-raw-light-hex screen scan, and the structural-name ban-list.
- **Design amendment applied (2026-05-20 finishing pass):** the designer's amended contrast table fixed three numerically-wrong ratios. `CONTROL.primary.bg` changed `#6366f1` ŌåÆ `#4f46e5` (indigo-600) and `CONTROL.primary.fg` changed from `SURFACE_TOKENS.textInverse` (`#0b1220`) to `#ffffff` ŌĆö white on indigo-600 measures 6.29:1 and clears the 4.5:1 body-text AA bar (`SURFACE_TOKENS.textInverse` is kept as a token; it is only no longer the primary button label). The three decorative hairlines (`border`/`divider`/`inputBorder`) are reclassified per WCAG 1.4.11 ŌĆö a card/input/table separator does not encode a required component boundary, so they carry no 3:1 ratio bar; `darkSurfaceTokens.test.ts` now asserts only the lighter-than-backdrop luminance ordering for them. The focus ring keeps the full 3:1 bar (clears it at ~9ŌĆō10:1). Every contrast-pair number in the suite is pinned to its real WCAG 2.x measured value.
- **Doctrine:** token names stay structural ŌĆö no verdict vocabulary (`CONTROL.danger` = "irreversible action", never "wrong"). No scoring/validation/post path touched. No secrets, no network, no AI call. No copy changed. cdiscourse-doctrine + accessibility-targets + expo-rn-patterns all hold.
- **+74 tests / +1 suite.** Full suite **6733 tests / 259 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client code. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install.

## MCP-016 ŌĆö Edge Function mock boundary scaffold (Release 6.8 / Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö implements MCP-009's server-side `semantic-referee` Edge Function boundary **in mock mode only**: the structural seam between the deterministic CDiscourse stack and a (future) AI provider, JWT-protected, schema-validated, and fully tested, with **no live AI in the loop**. Mock-only, no-deploy scaffold. No Anthropic / xAI / OpenAI / MCP-server call, no provider key read, no service-role, no `public.arguments` insert, no migration, no dependency install, no `.env` touched. Issue #183.

- **What it ships (1 new Edge Function + 8 new `_shared/semanticReferee/` modules + 1 `config.toml` block + the `classifyMove` client wrapper + 11 new test suites):** `supabase/functions/semantic-referee/index.ts` ŌĆö the new Edge Function entry point, mirroring `process-language-draft/index.ts` step-for-step (CORS ŌåÆ POST guard ŌåÆ JWT verify ŌåÆ JSON parse ŌåÆ `ClassifyMoveRequestSchema` validate ŌåÆ `debates` RLS room-access check via the caller-scoped client ŌåÆ defensive redaction ŌåÆ `classifyWithConfiguredProvider` ŌåÆ `ok(outcome)`; HTTP 200 for both `enabled: false` and `enabled: true`). No service-role client, no write. `_shared/semanticReferee/types.ts` ŌĆö the documented Deno-side mirror of MCP-011's canonical `src/features/semanticReferee/semanticRefereeTypes.ts` (the `SemanticRefereePacket` contract + the `ALL_*` arrays) plus the boundary-only transport types. `schema.ts` ŌĆö `npm:zod@4` validators: `ClassifyMoveRequestSchema` (inbound, `.strict()`) and `SemanticRefereePacketSchema` (outbound ŌĆö `authoritative` pinned to `z.literal(false)`, `value` to `z.union([z.literal(0), z.literal(1)])`, `scoreHints` integers to `0..3`, `.strict()` everywhere). `redaction.ts` ŌĆö the defensive second redaction pass (strips secret / handle / URL / email / post-id shapes). `mockProvider.ts` ŌĆö the deterministic `runMockClassifier` (same request ŌåÆ byte-identical schema-valid packet, `provider: 'mock'`, `authoritative: false`) + `buildFallbackPacket`. `fixtureProvider.ts` + `fixtures.ts` ŌĆö the local-dev fixture provider (checked-in fixture map keyed by `contentHash`; miss ŌåÆ falls through to the mock). `providerRouting.ts` ŌĆö the pure, zod-free routing core (`classifyWithProvider`); `providers.ts` ŌĆö the Deno wrapper `classifyWithConfiguredProvider` (reads `Deno.env`, runs the outbound schema ŌåÆ fallback gate). `src/lib/edgeFunctions.ts` ŌĆö the `classifyMove` client wrapper + its boundary-only Node types (`ClassifyMoveRequest` / `ClassifyMoveOutcome` etc.), appended next to `processLanguageDraft`. `supabase/config.toml` ŌĆö the additive `[functions.semantic-referee]` block with `verify_jwt = true`.
- **Doctrine encoded:** **mock-by-default** ŌĆö the registry defaults `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER` to `mock` (the deliberate deviation from `languageProcessing/providers.ts`, which defaults to `anthropic`); turning the flag on never starts a live call. **disabled-by-default is silent** ŌĆö `SEMANTIC_REFEREE_ENABLED` unset / not exactly `'true'` ŌåÆ `{ enabled: false, reason: 'disabled' }`, HTTP 200, checked before any provider is selected, no key read. The `anthropic` / `mcp` registry slots are **stubbed** ŌĆö a literal `{ enabled: false, reason: 'not_implemented' }` return with no `anthropicProvider.ts` / `mcpAdapter.ts` module behind them. The outbound `SemanticRefereePacketSchema` is `.strict()` with `authoritative: z.literal(false)` and no truth / `block` field ŌĆö a widened packet fails validation ŌåÆ deterministic minimal fallback packet, never a thrown error. The function builds only a caller-scoped (RLS) client, performs no privileged write, never inserts into `public.arguments`, never calls `submit-argument`. Reads no provider key. Logs no Authorization header / key / JWT / raw body. `semanticNoLiveCall.test.ts` source-scans the whole function + `_shared` tree for `fetch` / provider host literal / provider SDK import / a live-provider module ŌĆö zero. `semanticForbiddenSecrets.test.ts` proves no key is named in executable code. `semanticBoundaryBanList.test.ts` scans every produced string (reason codes, mock reason codes, fixture fields) for verdict / person tokens ŌĆö zero.
- **Node Ōåö Deno reconciliation (roadmap ┬¦6):** MCP-016 imports MCP-011's `semanticRefereeTypes.ts` as-is for the Node side and does NOT mint a second Node `types.ts` ŌĆö the boundary-only Node types live in `src/lib/edgeFunctions.ts` next to the wrapper. The Deno `_shared/semanticReferee/types.ts` is a documented mirror; `semanticDenoNodeParity.test.ts` reads both files as source text and fails the build if the contract surface drifts.
- **Implementer note ŌĆö test bridge for the Deno tree:** the Deno `_shared/semanticReferee` modules use Deno-only import syntax (`.ts`-extension specifiers; `npm:zod@4` in `schema.ts`) that the project's `tsc` cannot resolve and `supabase/functions` is excluded from compile ŌĆö the established repo convention (`adminSchemas.test.ts`, `pointTagsEligibilityMirror.test.ts`). The behavioural test suites load the **real** zod-free Deno modules through a typed `require()` bridge (`__tests__/_helpers/semanticRefereeDeno.ts`) ŌĆö Jest executes the real code with full coverage; `tsc` does not follow the bridge's `require()` into the Deno tree. `schema.ts` / `providers.ts` (which import `npm:zod@4`, unloadable by Jest) are covered by the `adminSchemas.test.ts`-style re-declared-schema + source-scan parity tests.
- **+210 tests / +14 suites.** Full suite **6659 tests / 258 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **Operator follow-up (out of scope for this card ŌĆö deploy is a separate operator action):** `npx supabase functions deploy semantic-referee --linked` to deploy the new Edge Function; optionally `npx supabase secrets set SEMANTIC_REFEREE_ENABLED=true SEMANTIC_REFEREE_PROVIDER=mock` to enable the layer with the safe deterministic provider (still no live call). Until then the function does not exist on any project and `classifyMove` callers fall back to layer 1 ŌĆö the safe default. No migration, no dependency install, no `.env` change. The live-provider pilot (`anthropic` / `mcp`) is a separate, explicitly operator-approved card.

## MCP-015 ŌĆö Semantic override UX model (no live provider) (Release 6.8 / Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö implements MCP-010 ┬¦5.2: the pure-TypeScript semantic override UX model that lets a participant reverse an *uncertain or conflicting* semantic routing suggestion without ever feeling caged. Pure-TS model only ŌĆö no Supabase, no React, no network, no `.env` read, no Edge Function, no migration, no live provider, no new dependency, no operator step. A strict pure consumer of three already-merged contracts (`src/features/semanticReferee/`, `src/features/refereeLedger/`, `src/features/metadata/`); the React choice surface (`SemanticOverrideChoiceSheet`) is deferred to a scoped follow-up card per the design. Issue #182.

- **What it ships (4 new source files in `src/features/semanticOverride/` + 2 append-only modified files + 5 new test suites):** `types.ts` ŌĆö `SemanticOverrideLane` (`mainline | branch | tangent`), `SemanticOverrideTriggerReason` (`low_confidence | l1_l2_conflict`), `SemanticOverrideActorRole` (mirrors META-001's `ManualTagActorRole`), the append-only `SemanticOverrideRecord`, the trigger-model output `SemanticOverridePrompt`, the in-memory `RepeatedOverrideSignal`, `SOFTEN_COPY_THRESHOLD = 3`, and the `ALL_*` frozen arrays ŌĆö type declarations + `const` arrays only, type-only imports. `overrideTriggerModel.ts` ŌĆö the pure `evaluateSemanticOverridePrompt` (actor gate ŌåÆ no-input gate ŌåÆ L1/L2 conflict check ŌåÆ low-confidence check ŌåÆ confident path) plus the exported `routeSuggestionToLane` mapping MCP-011's seven `SemanticRouteSuggestion` values onto the three lanes. `overrideRecordModel.ts` ŌĆö `buildSemanticOverrideRecord`, the `toSemanticOverrideMetadataEvent` / `toAnswersParentMetadataEvent` projectors, `bumpRepeatedOverrideSignal`, `emptyRepeatedOverrideSignal`, and `_forbiddenOverrideTokens()` (the doctrine ban-list source). `index.ts` ŌĆö public re-exports.
- **Doctrine encoded:** overriding is NEVER a penalty ŌĆö `SemanticOverrideRecord` / `SemanticOverridePrompt` / `RepeatedOverrideSignal` and both projected `MetadataEvent`s carry no `delta` / `score` / `penalty` / `block` / `flag` field, no "you were warned" copy (`semanticOverrideNoPenalty.test.ts` asserts the shape, the export names, and the source text). Observers are NEVER offered the override surface ŌĆö the actor gate is step 1 of `evaluateSemanticOverridePrompt`, before any packet inspection (`semanticOverrideTrigger.test.ts`). Override records are append-only ŌĆö every confirmed override produces a new record + a new `MetadataEvent` (`kind: 'add'`); there is no remove path. The `RepeatedOverrideSignal` is in-memory, per-room, per-session ŌĆö it only softens the prompt copy code; it is never persisted, never summed across rooms, never a training input. The trigger reads only packet confidence + the L1/L2 conflict signal + viewer role + the in-memory count ŌĆö never heat / engagement / popularity, and triggers no AI call. `semanticOverrideForbiddenImports.test.ts` statically proves the four files are pure TS (no provider SDK, no `fetch`, no Supabase, no React, no `Deno`, no `process.env`, no `console.log`, no `async`, no `Date.now()` / `new Date(`), that `types.ts` is type-only, and that the dependency points one way.
- **The one `MetadataEvent.codeFamily` extension (additive, in META-001's file):** `src/features/metadata/moveMetadataLedger.ts` ŌĆö `codeFamily` gains exactly one member, `'semantic_override'` (`manual_tag | auto_metadata | lifecycle_causation | semantic_override`). Purely additive ŌĆö no member removed, no field added or removed; the `MetadataEvent` interface keeps all its existing fields and gains none. The full metadata suite (553 metadata + referee tests) passes unchanged. Pinned to the *actual* merged three-member union, per the design's reconciliation note (MCP-010 ┬¦4.1's prose described a four-member union; the merged file had three).
- **Modified file (2):** `src/features/metadata/moveMetadataLedger.ts` (the one-member `codeFamily` extension) and `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` (append-only; 16 new `PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY` override copy codes ŌĆö `mainline` / `branch` / `answers_parent` + 13 category-prefixed `semantic_override_*` keys; `tangent` is reused from the existing META-001 key, not re-declared). Nothing existing changed in either file.
- **Deferred per the design:** `SemanticOverrideChoiceSheet.tsx` ŌĆö the React Native choice surface ŌĆö is a scoped follow-up card; MCP-015 ships the pure model + tests and specifies the component's contract so the follow-up is small. The design uses "referee" as the framing word in two copy strings (`semantic_override_confirm_keep`, `semantic_override_original_suggestion`).
- **+93 tests / +5 suites.** Full suite **6449 tests / 244 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure-TS model. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. The override model is not auto-wired into the live argument room ŌĆö the deferred `SemanticOverrideChoiceSheet` component card and a later room-wiring stage append the override events to the in-memory metadata ledger.

## MCP-014 ŌĆö Referee banner library implementation (Release 6.8 / Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö layer 4 of the semantic-referee architecture: the pure-TypeScript referee feedback banner library that turns already-classified move metadata into one short, encouraging, non-verdict banner ("Clean parent tie.", "Good pressure ŌĆö an evidence debt opened.", "This probably belongs on a branch."). Pure-TS string library + a deterministic pure selection function ŌĆö no Supabase, no React, no network, no `.env` read, no Edge Function, no migration, no live provider, no new dependency, no operator step. A strict pure consumer of two already-merged pure-TS type contracts (`src/features/semanticReferee/`, `src/features/refereeLedger/`); the render component is deliberately deferred (MCP-008 ┬¦15). Issue #181.

- **What it ships (6 new source files in `src/features/refereeBanners/` + 1 append-only `gameCopy.ts` extension + 7 new test suites):** `types.ts` ŌĆö `RefereeBannerCategory` (12 issue-named categories), `RefereeBannerTone` (`celebratory | nudge | routing_hint`), `RefereeBannerToneGlyph` (`star | arrow | branch` ŌĆö a non-color shape signal), `RefereeBannerConfidence`, the `RefereeBanner` library-entry interface (`bannerCode`, `headline` Ōēż64, optional `helperLine` Ōēż80, `toneGlyph`, frozen `accessibilityLabel`, `minConfidence`, `softenedSiblingCode`), `BannerSelectionInput`, `BannerSelectionResult`, and `ALL_REFEREE_BANNER_CATEGORIES`. `accessibilityLabel.ts` ŌĆö `buildBannerAccessibilityLabel(banner, framingWord='Referee')` + `BANNER_TONE_PREFIX`; a pure function ŌĆö same input ŌåÆ same output, no clock, no randomness. `refereeBannerLibrary.ts` ŌĆö the frozen 103-entry `REFEREE_BANNER_LIBRARY` (each entry's `accessibilityLabel` generated at module load so it cannot drift from the headline), `BANNER_BY_CODE` O(1) index, and `INTENTIONALLY_SILENT_CLASSIFIERS = { contains_unplayable_insult_only }`. `classifierBannerMap.ts` ŌĆö `CLASSIFIER_TO_BANNERS` keyed off all 23 `SemanticClassifierId` catalog ids (`contains_unplayable_insult_only` ŌåÆ `[]`) and `FEEDBACK_CODE_TO_BANNER` keyed off all 22 `RefereeFeedbackCode`s. `selectBanner.ts` ŌĆö the deterministic `selectBanner(input): BannerSelectionResult` entry point (candidate-pool build, conflict-routed short-circuit, confidence softening/suppression, the fixed `BANNER_CATEGORY_PRIORITY` order, single-winner selection, `selectionTrace`). `index.ts` ŌĆö public surface.
- **Doctrine encoded:** a banner describes a structural play property of the MOVE, never the person ŌĆö no `headline` / `helperLine` / `accessibilityLabel` / `bannerCode` carries a verdict / winner / loser / truth / right / wrong / person-label / popularity-praise token (`refereeBannerBanList.test.ts` scans every string whole-word, asserts a popularity token always co-occurs with a not-proof phrase, scans for second-person belittling, and asserts `RefereeBanner` carries no `block`/`winner`/`truthValue`/`score`/`authoritative` key). A low-confidence input softens to a `*_soft` hedged sibling or suppresses ŌĆö never a confident-sounding line; a `conflict_routed` reading forces exactly the `pacing_you_decide_the_lane` routing banner even against a co-occurring high-confidence celebratory binary. No raw `classifierId` / `feedbackCode` / `bannerCode` reaches a surface ŌĆö every `bannerCode` resolves through `gameCopy.toPlainLanguage` to its headline; an unmapped code returns `null` and is suppressed. There is no heat / engagement / popularity field anywhere in `BannerSelectionInput`. `selectBanner` is fully deterministic and never blocks posting / auto-acts. `refereeBannerForbiddenImports.test.ts` statically proves the six files are pure TS (no provider SDK, no `fetch`, no Supabase, no React, no `Deno`, no `process.env`, no `console.log`, no `async`) and that the only cross-feature imports are `import type` from MCP-011 / MCP-013.
- **Documented deviations (all from `docs/designs/MCP-014.md`, honored verbatim):** (1) `CLASSIFIER_TO_BANNERS` is keyed off the real 23-id `SemanticClassifierId` catalog (MCP-011), not MCP-008 ┬¦5's 90 seed ids ŌĆö the coverage test asserts the key set equals `ALL_SEMANTIC_CLASSIFIER_IDS`; (2) `FEEDBACK_CODE_TO_BANNER` is keyed off MCP-013's 22 `RefereeFeedbackCode`s; (3) `RefereeBanner` uses `softenedSiblingCode: string | null` instead of MCP-008's `hasSoftenedSibling: boolean`; (4) `BannerSelectionInput` drops MCP-008's redundant `category` / `routeSuggestion` fields and tightens every field to the merged union types. One implementer reword (within the design's ban-list scope): the design's `pacing_*` copy used the word "beat" ("a short beat") ŌĆö "beat" is on the MCP-014 ban-list (the verdict sense, "to beat someone"), so the two affected banners were reworded to "a short pause" / "worth it here" (`bannerCode` `pacing_take_a_short_beat` ŌåÆ `pacing_take_a_short_pause`); no logic change, ban-list clean.
- **Modified file:** one ŌĆö `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` (append-only; 103 new `PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY` `bannerCode` entries ŌĆö every value the banner's `headline` verbatim, every key category-prefixed and disjoint from the pre-MCP-014 key set). Nothing existing changed.
- **+122 tests / +7 suites.** Full suite **6356 tests / 239 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure-TS string library + selection model. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. The banner library is not auto-wired into the live argument room ŌĆö the render component (a thin `<View>`/`<Text>` card) is a deferred follow-up card (MCP-008 ┬¦15), and the upstream builder that assembles `BannerSelectionInput` from a live `SemanticRefereePacket` + `LedgerResult` is a later room-wiring card. One operator decision is carried forward unchanged from MCP-008 ┬¦17: the scoreboard framing word ŌĆö MCP-014 uses `Referee` as the default; `buildBannerAccessibilityLabel(banner, framingWord)` takes it as a one-argument parameter.

## MCP-013 ŌĆö Referee ledger adapter implementation (deterministic + mock semantic) (Release 6.8 / Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö layer 3 of the semantic-referee architecture: the deterministic, pure-TypeScript referee ledger that produces play-quality feedback per move. Pure-TS ŌĆö no Supabase, no React, no network, no `.env` read, no Edge Function, no migration, no live provider, no new dependency, no operator step. A strict pure consumer of two already-merged pure-TS modules (`src/features/pointStanding/`, `src/features/semanticReferee/`); modifies zero economy files. Issue #180.

- **What it ships (7 new source files in `src/features/refereeLedger/` + 1 append-only `gameCopy.ts` extension + 6 new test suites):** `types.ts` ŌĆö the 14 `RefereePointCategory` play-quality values, the 22-code `RefereeFeedbackCode` family, `ReconciliationOutcome`, `CategoryReading`, `LedgerCreditState`, the flat ledger-owned `DeterministicMoveMetadata` layer-1 fact bundle, `LedgerMoveInput`, and `LedgerResult` (no `block` / `winner` / `truthValue` / `score`-scalar / per-side aggregate field). `scoreHintMapping.ts` ŌĆö `HINT_STEP = 0.08`, `clampCategoryDelta`, and the six pure hint functions; every hint magnitude is `>= 0` ŌĆö a hint may only add credit, open a debt, or route, never subtract standing. `reconciliation.ts` ŌĆö `reconcileCategory` + the `CATEGORY_AUTHORITY` table; a layer-1/layer-2 conflict on a `neither`-authority category routes (`conflict_routed`, `delta: 0`) and an `l1`-conflict resolves `conflict_l1_dominant` ŌĆö never a penalty; the low-confidence gate runs first. `antiExploit.ts` ŌĆö `evaluateLedgerGate` (reuses the economy's `buildChallengeEligibility` / `buildRepairEligibility`) + `applyCreditState` (one credit per debt, keyed by the economy's `debtId`). `reconcileMove.ts` ŌĆö the single pure entry point; calls `gradeChallenge` / `gradeRepair` / `applyAntiAmplification` and adopts their deltas bit-for-bit. `refereeLedgerCopy.ts` ŌĆö the `RefereeFeedbackCode` ŌåÆ plain-language table, delegating to `gameCopy.toPlainLanguage`. `index.ts` ŌĆö public surface.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the ledger scores the rules of play, never truth ŌĆö `LedgerResult` has no winner / loser / block / score scalar / per-side aggregate (asserted by `refereeLedgerBanList.test.ts`). For the economy-owned categories (`narrowing`, `concession`, `evidence_debt_resolution`) the ledger consumes ŌĆö never re-derives ŌĆö the point-standing economy: `refereeLedgerEconomyParity.test.ts` proves the adopted reading delta is bit-for-bit equal (`toBe`, not `toBeCloseTo`) to `gradeRepair` / `gradeChallenge` output. A layer-1/layer-2 conflict routes to a reversible `conflict_routed` choice (`delta: 0`), never a penalty. A low-confidence semantic binary moves no standing. Engagement credit and factual-standing credit stay on separate axes (`CategoryReading.creditAxis`); factual-standing categories route through `applyAntiAmplification`; an amplification-only move earns engagement credit while factual gain is suppressed (rendered `evidence_debt_open`, never a penalty). `refereeLedgerForbiddenImports.test.ts` statically proves the seven files are pure TS (no provider SDK, no `fetch`, no Supabase, no React, no `Deno`, no `process.env`, no `console.log`, no `async`) and that the dependency points one way.
- **Two documented design deviations (both honored from `docs/designs/MCP-013.md`):** (1) the flat ledger-owned `DeterministicMoveMetadata` bundle, since the six layer-1 input models are not all merged on `main`; (2) the additive `broad_point_set_down` / `synthesis_named` feedback codes. One implementer note: the design prose says "21 feedback codes" but the design's own `RefereeFeedbackCode` union and `gameCopy` block both list 22 (MCP-003's 20 + the two new codes; 20 + 2 = 22) ŌĆö the code contract is 22; the "21" is an arithmetic slip in the design prose, not a real gap.
- **Modified file:** one ŌĆö `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` (append-only; 20 new `PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY` feedbackCode entries ŌĆö the 21st code `source_attached` reuses the existing META-001 key). Nothing existing changed.
- **+117 tests / +6 suites.** Full suite **6234 tests / 232 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure-TS model. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. The referee ledger is not auto-wired into the live argument room ŌĆö a separate future room-wiring stage calls `reconcileMove` alongside `gradeChallenge` / `gradeRepair`.

## MCP-012 ŌĆö Semantic call router implementation (mock-only) (Release 6.8 / Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö the pure-TypeScript semantic call router that realizes MCP-004's design (trigger gates, batching Ōēż5/call, in-memory LRU cache store, token budget, retry policy) and consumes ŌĆö not re-creates ŌĆö MCP-011's frozen contract. Pure decision/data logic only ŌĆö no provider call, no network call, no Supabase, no React, no Edge Function, no env-var read, no `Deno` reference, no migration, no new dependency, no operator step. Issue #179.

- **What it ships (5 new source files in `src/features/semanticReferee/` + 8 new test suites):** `triggerGates.ts` ŌĆö `evaluateTrigger(input)`, the single chokepoint that decides *whether/which moment* to classify, never *whether to post*; the six `SemanticTriggerMoment`s, the exhaustive eight-event `SemanticForbiddenEvent` enum, `SemanticClassificationMode` / `SemanticActorRole`, `TriggerReasonCode` (14 codes), `TriggerDecision`, and `SYNTHESIS_TRIGGER_MIN_EVENTS = 6`. Forbidden events are refused as the very first statement, before any flag/mode/role read. `classifierBatching.ts` ŌĆö `planClassifierBatches(requested)`, `BATCH_CAP = 5`, the frozen five A-E `SEMANTIC_BATCH_GROUPS` that partition MCP-011's 23-id catalog exactly; every emitted batch is Ōēż5 and lexically order-normalized. `semanticCache.ts` ŌĆö `SemanticPacketCache`, an in-memory LRU store keyed by MCP-011's `serializeSemanticCacheKey` (imported, never re-derived), `DEFAULT_CACHE_CAPACITY = 256`; `get` refreshes recency, `has` does not, no time-based TTL. `tokenBudget.ts` ŌĆö `estimatePacketTokens` / `isWithinBudget`, `SEMANTIC_PACKET_TOKEN_BUDGET = 1500`; a conservative tokenizer-free char heuristic that over-counts so it fails safe. `retryPolicy.ts` ŌĆö `SEMANTIC_RETRY_POLICY` (`maxAttempts: 2`, `backoffMs: [250]`, `attemptTimeoutMs: 8000`), `shouldRetry`, and the retryable/terminal `SemanticErrorClass` partition ŌĆö a pure descriptor, the executor is MCP-016's. `index.ts` ŌĆö append-only: five new `export *` lines beside MCP-011's four.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the router decides only whether/what to classify, never whether to post ŌĆö every "no call" path (a forbidden event, a room in `off` mode, an over-budget payload, an exhausted retry) degrades silently to deterministic layer 1; `submit-argument` never imports or calls the router. Forbidden events (`keystroke`, `hover`, `timeline_selection`, `observer_browsing`, `scroll`, `focus`, `blur`, `gallery_browsing`) produce ZERO provider calls ŌĆö proven by the `semanticNoCallOnDraftEdit` spy test against a `jest.fn()`-wrapped `mockFixtureProvider`. `TriggerEvaluationInput` carries no engagement / like-count / heat field. Four independent caps (trigger gating, LRU cache, batching Ōēż5, token budget) make an uncapped layer structurally impossible. `semanticRouterForbiddenImports.test.ts` statically proves the five files are pure TS (no provider SDK, no `fetch`, no Supabase, no React, no `Deno`, no `process`/env, no `console.log`, no `async`) and that `semanticCache.ts` value-imports `serializeSemanticCacheKey` and re-derives no key/hash. `semanticRouterBanList.test.ts` scans every `TriggerReasonCode` and batch-group label for verdict/person tokens ŌĆö zero matches.
- **Modified files:** one ŌĆö `src/features/semanticReferee/index.ts` (append-only; MCP-011's four exports untouched).
- **+158 tests / +8 suites.** Full suite **6117 tests / 226 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure-TS model. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install. The semantic-referee layer stays off until MCP-016's enable step; the mock provider is the default at every layer.

## MCP-011 ŌĆö Mock semantic-referee packet validator and fixture provider (Release 6.8 / Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö the first safe, no-live-call layer of the MCP semantic-referee stack. Pure-TypeScript and fixtures only. No provider call, no network call, no Edge Function, no env-var read, no user-facing UI, no new dependency (`zod@4` was already present), no migration, no Supabase write, no operator step. Issue #178.

- **What it ships (5 new source files in `src/features/semanticReferee/` + 4 new test suites + 1 doc):** `semanticRefereeTypes.ts` ŌĆö the canonical Node-side `SemanticRefereePacket` / `SemanticBinarySample` contract (re-stated verbatim from MCP-001 ┬¦7, 23-id catalog v0), constant arrays, and the `SemanticRejectionCode` vocabulary. `semanticRefereeValidator.ts` ŌĆö `parseSemanticPacket(raw: unknown)` (a `zod@4` `strictObject` structural schema plus a pure-TS content-safety scanner) that rejects every malformed / off-contract / unsafe provider output: non-JSON, top-level arrays, `authoritative: true`, unknown classifier / route / friction / confidence, non-`0/1` values, out-of-range score hints, unknown reason codes, verdict tokens, person labels, secret / JWT / Bearer / handle / URL / email / post-id shapes, chain-of-thought / raw-prompt / smuggled-copy fields, `block` fields, duplicate classifier ids ŌĆö plus `isCreditEligible` / `creditEligibleBinaries` / `looksLikeInternalCode`. `semanticRefereeFixtures.ts` ŌĆö 18 fixture groups (valid packets, malformed payloads tripping each rejection path, cache-key pairs) plus the deterministic `mockFixtureProvider` (a TEST/DEV fixture source, never wired into a screen). `semanticRefereeCacheKey.ts` ŌĆö `buildSemanticCacheKey` / `serializeSemanticCacheKey` / `hashClassifierSet` (the MCP-004 five-tuple superset `{roomId, parentId, contentHash, promptVersion, classifierSetHash, roomMode, selectedAction}`, FNV-1a hash, no `crypto` import). `index.ts` ŌĆö public re-exports. `docs/semantic-referee/mcp-011-fixture-contract.md` ŌĆö the one-page fixture catalog.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the validator is the wall that makes "advisory" structurally true ŌĆö an off-contract packet is rejected, the consumer falls back to deterministic layer 1, the post is unaffected (a rejection never blocks a post). `authoritative` is pinned to the literal `false`. No verdict / truth / winner field can validate; verdict + person tokens are scanned out of every string field. Rejection messages are sanitized ŌĆö `SemanticPacketRejection.detail` never echoes the offending raw value (proven by a test for the secret / PII fixtures). Malformed fixtures use synthetic, assembled strings ŌĆö no contiguous real-key-shaped literal sits in the committed source. `semanticRefereeNoLiveAi.test.ts` statically proves the whole directory is pure TS: no provider SDK, no `fetch` / network primitive, no Supabase, no React, no `Deno`, no `process.env`, only `semanticRefereeValidator.ts` value-imports `zod`.
- **Modified files:** none ŌĆö MCP-011 is a deliberately additive, zero-blast-radius card.
- **+146 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite **5959 tests / 218 suites passing**. Typecheck + lint + skills:validate clean.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure-TS model + fixtures. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency install.

## GAME-008 ŌĆö Bot public-room policy and public argument seeding (Release 6.7 / Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö a deterministic pure-TS bot-room policy model + a read-time bot-marking view contract + gallery bot-marker UI. Pure client-side ŌĆö no migration, no Edge Function, no Supabase write, no schema change, no `profiles.is_bot` column, no AI/xAI/Anthropic/network call, no live bot posting, no new dependency, no operator step. Issue #147.

- **Why this card exists:** bots are an explicit, doctrine-safe test surface for the public-room layer GAME-005 (6-seat cap, chime-in governance) and BR-004 (branch grammar) ŌĆö so the public-room mechanics can be exercised without pulling real users into untested flows. GAME-008 defines the product-level POLICY for bots in public rooms (the rules a normal user can rely on) and the UI MARKING that makes those rules visible. This card is policy + marking only ŌĆö it enables, triggers, and schedules ZERO live bot posting.
- **Card-vs-reality decisions (from design ┬¦0, honored verbatim):** there is no `profiles.is_bot` column ŌĆö the schema-of-record for bot identity (`auth.users.user_metadata`, `public.bot_user_registry`) is admin/service-role only and the production anon client cannot read it; so `isBotSeededRoom` is a PURE PREDICATE over already-derived per-argument `isBot` hints (the GAME-004 `RoomArgumentInput.isBot` seam, lifted to a per-user `BotParticipantHint`), never a DB query. v1's no-migration hint sources: the deterministic display-name/title convention the corpus runners already emit (`looksLikeBotSeedTag` reuses the gallery model `SUFFIX_TAG_PATTERNS` family) or an explicit caller hint. Absent hint => fail-safe-human (wrongly marking a human as a bot is a serious misrepresentation; wrongly omitting a bot marker only degrades a test surface). A first-class persisted bot flag is a named, deferred future migration card.
- **Deliverables (3 new production files + 4 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/debates/botRoomPolicyModel.ts` ŌĆö **pure TS** (no React / Supabase / network / AI; imports GAME-004 `roomContractModel` types + `BOT_MARKER_COPY`). Exports `BotRoomPolicy`, `BOT_ROOM_POLICY` (the single frozen app-wide policy constant), `BotParticipantHint`, `BotRoomInputs`, `BotParticipantMarking`, `BotMarkingViewModel`, `BotRoomAction`, `BotPolicyDenyReason`, `ALL_BOT_POLICY_DENY_REASONS`, `BotRoomEligibilityResult`, `AssertBotRoomEligibilityInput`, `isBotSeededRoom` (root-author predicate, fail-safe-human), `looksLikeBotSeedTag` (the no-migration title-tag hint helper), `buildBotMarkingViewModel` (the read-time bot-marking projection ŌĆö frozen, deterministic), `assertBotRoomEligibility` (the policy GATE ŌĆö four deny reasons, never a trigger), `_forbiddenBotMarkerTokens`. The module exports NO posting / scheduling / harvest function ŌĆö live-posting non-enablement is encoded by omission and proven by an API-surface test.
  - `src/features/debates/BotParticipantMarker.tsx` ŌĆö read-time RN component, the individual "Test bot" marker on a bot participant in-room; pure render over one `BotParticipantMarking`; renders nothing for a non-bot; non-interactive (no `Pressable`).
  - `src/features/debates/BotRoomMarker.tsx` ŌĆö read-time RN component, the non-alarming room-level "Test room" / "Bot-seeded test room" affordance for the gallery card + room header; pure render over a `BotMarkingViewModel`; renders nothing when the room has no bot; non-interactive.
  - 4 new test suites ŌĆö `botRoomPolicyModel` (54), `botRoomPolicyDoctrine` (16), `botParticipantMarker` (13), `botRoomMarker` (16) ŌĆö **83 tests**: the `BOT_ROOM_POLICY` shape + frozen, the `isBotSeededRoom` table incl. fail-safe-human, `looksLikeBotSeedTag` with `SUFFIX_TAG_PATTERNS` parity, `buildBotMarkingViewModel` across pure-bot / mixed / human / persona / banned-persona-fallback permutations, the full `assertBotRoomEligibility` matrix (each of the four deny reasons + the allowed paths), determinism + frozen-input no-mutation, the API-surface omission proof, the ban-list scan over every produced string, the no-deceptive-framing assertion ("not a person" allowlisted), `looksLikeInternalCode` false for every visible string + no enum-leak, the forbidden-import + no-service-role + no-Edge-Function + no-AI-provider source scans, and the component view-model + a11y render contracts.
- **Modified files (3):** `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` ŌĆö adds the frozen `BOT_MARKER_COPY` block beside `JUMP_BRANCH_COPY` (neutral "Test bot" / "Test room" / "Bot-seeded test room" labels + a11y strings + a gallery helper line; nothing existing changes). `src/features/debates/ConversationGalleryScreen.tsx` ŌĆö mounts `<BotRoomMarker context="gallery">` additively on a bot-seeded card via `looksLikeBotSeedTag` (the design's documented no-query degraded fallback); no existing card field removed. `src/features/debates/index.ts` ŌĆö re-exports the new model, components, and types in a `// GAME-008` block.
- **Implementer copy correction (within design OD-1 scope ŌĆö `BOT_MARKER_COPY` is a single frozen block so wording is a one-spot edit):** the design ┬¦1.5 `participant_a11y` was authored "...they never decide who is right." ŌĆö but the design ┬¦10 ban-list correctly forbids the verdict token "right". The phrase was reworded "...they never judge a debate." ŌĆö same doctrine meaning ("bots never decide who is right"), ban-list clean. No logic change. (See the Implementer note appended to `docs/designs/GAME-008.md`.)
- **Doctrine encoded:** a bot marker describes the ACCOUNT TYPE ("Test bot"), never a verdict ŌĆö bots never decide who is right; `BOT_ROOM_POLICY` carries no score, no band, no heat, no person-attribution field. Bots ŌåÆ public rooms only; never a private 1v1 with a real user; never the Primary Opponent of a real user in a way that misrepresents the bot as human. `assertBotRoomEligibility` is a policy GATE (a predicate), never a trigger ŌĆö GAME-008 ships no caller that posts a bot move; live bot posting stays operator-gated in `scripts/bot-fixtures/`. `botRoomPolicyModel.ts` imports nothing from any score / standing / heat / anti-amplification module (enforced by the forbidden-import test) ŌĆö a bot's presence is orthogonal to standing. The marker copy is neutral, non-alarming, non-deceptive ŌĆö never a "this is a human" framing (the ban-list test forbids `fake` / `troll` / `spam` / `danger` / `warning` and any `real user` / `real person` / `human` framing of the bot itself; the only permitted "person" use is the explicit negation "not a person"). Color is never the only signal ŌĆö the marker is a dashed-border shape + glyph + the literal word "Test bot" / "Test room", grayscale-legible.
- **+83 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite **5813 tests / 214 suites** (**5794 passing** in this bare worktree). Typecheck + lint clean. The 19 failing tests across 5 xAI/bot-fixture suites (`xaiSeededStancesLive`, `xaiAdversarialProvider`, `xaiAdversarialSourceHarvest`, `xaiAdversarialPipeline`, `aiDrivenBotCorpus`) are pre-existing and environmental (the gitignored `.env.engagement-intelligence` is absent from this isolated worktree) ŌĆö unrelated to GAME-008.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client-side code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency, no live bot posting. One operator decision is isolated and does not gate the build: **OD-1** ŌĆö the bot-marker copy + placement and the "bots yield seats" user-facing framing route through a copy review; the proposed `BOT_MARKER_COPY` strings shipped. A first-class persisted `public.profiles.is_bot` flag is a named, deferred future migration card ŌĆö the GAME-008 model already takes `BotParticipantHint[]` and is unchanged when it lands. The per-participant in-room marker mount (`<BotParticipantMarker>` beside a bot author + `<BotRoomMarker context="room">` in the room header) is a small additive follow-up step ŌĆö the design ┬¦5 marks it optional-prop, no-render-by-default.

## GAME-006 ŌĆö Jump Branch: once-per-room cross-branch participation (Release 6.7 / Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö a deterministic pure-TS Jump-Branch model that extends GAME-005's public-room seat layer and consumes GAME-004's RoomContract + BR-004's branch grammar, plus a thin read-time React layer. Pure client-side ŌĆö no migration, no Edge Function, no Supabase write, no schema change, no AI/network call, no new dependency, no operator step. Issue #144.

- **Why this card exists:** GAME-005 lets many voices chime in on a public room; uncontrolled cross-branch hopping would turn the structured board back into comment-thread chaos. GAME-006 defines the **Jump Branch** rule ŌĆö a bounded, deliberate, once-per-participant-per-room action that lets a chime-in move to engage a different branch (or the mainline) while preserving structure. A Jump describes structural MOVEMENT ŌĆö never a verdict, never a quality/truth signal, never anything about the person.
- **Derive-not-persist (design ┬¦4, honored verbatim):** a jump is not a separate event ŌĆö it IS a move whose branch placement differs from the participant's home branch. `JumpBranchRecord` and the once-per-room counter `jumpsUsed` are derived on every room load from existing `arguments` rows; there is no `jump_branch_records` table and no migration. A jump commits through the EXISTING, already-deployed `submit-argument` path ŌĆö GAME-006 adds no new write path, no Edge Function, no schema change.
- **Deliverables (3 new production files + 5 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/debates/jumpBranchModel.ts` ŌĆö **pure TS** (no React / Supabase / network / AI; imports GAME-004 `roomContractModel` types + `isQualifyingResponse`, GAME-005 `SeatRole` / `PublicRoomSeatMap`, BR-004 `BranchDirection` / `BranchGrammarNode` as types, and `JUMP_BRANCH_COPY`). Exports `JumpBranchRecord`, `JumpDenyReason`, `ALL_JUMP_DENY_REASONS`, `JumpEligibility`, `BranchEngagementState`, `JumpControlViewModel`, `JumpMarkerKind`, `JumpMarkerViewModel`, `MAX_JUMPS_PER_ROOM = 1`, `deriveParticipantHomeBranch`, `listJumpsForParticipant` (walks a participant's qualifying moves chronologically; a branch change is a jump ŌĆö `fromBranchId` / `toBranchId` / `at` / `viaArgumentId`), `jumpsUsed` (the card's named counter ŌĆö `listJumpsForParticipant(...).length`; defensive `roomId` check), `canJump` (the deterministic 7-reason predicate, fixed reason precedence, no clock), `buildBranchEngagementMap` (projects BR-004 direction + GAME-005 observer-fallback into per-branch `openToEngagement`), `buildJumpControlViewModel`, `buildJumpMarkers`, `jumpDenyReasonLabel`, `_forbiddenJumpBranchTokens`.
  - `src/features/debates/JumpBranchControl.tsx` ŌĆö read-time RN component, the confirm-required Jump action; tapping the action opens an inline confirm step (not a route, not a modal screen) ŌĆö only the confirm button commits via `onConfirmJump`; a disabled action still renders, visibly, with `accessibilityState={{ disabled: true }}` and the plain-language reason as visible text (no silent no-op); Ōēź44px hit targets via `hitSlop`; the enabled/disabled distinction is shape (dashed border) + text, not color alone.
  - `src/features/debates/JumpBranchMarker.tsx` ŌĆö read-time informational RN badge rendering one `JumpMarkerViewModel` ŌĆö the old-branch "Moved to another branch" departed badge or the destination "A chime-in joined this branch" arrival badge; non-interactive (no `Pressable`); departed/arrived distinction is glyph + dashed-vs-solid border.
  - 5 new test suites ŌĆö `jumpBranchModel` (44), `jumpBranchEligibility` (19), `jumpBranchDoctrine` (12), `jumpBranchControl` (12), `jumpBranchMarker` (9) ŌĆö **82 tests**: home-branch derivation, the `JumpBranchRecord` derivation (no-jump / one-jump / two-jumps / jump-back / same-branch-no-jump / unknown-branch-skip), the `jumpsUsed` counter + defensive `roomId`, the full `canJump` permutation matrix (every `JumpDenyReason` + the allowed path + the jump-into-mainline path with seat role unchanged + fixed reason precedence + no-clock determinism), `buildBranchEngagementMap` (mainline / active / collapsed / evidence), the marker derivation, determinism + frozen-input no-mutation, the API-surface omission proof (no `forceJump` / `resetJumps` / `setJumpCount`), the ban-list scan over every produced string, `looksLikeInternalCode` false for every visible string, the forbidden-import + no-service-role + no-Edge-Function source scans, and the component view-model + a11y render contracts.
- **Modified files (2):** `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` ŌĆö adds the frozen `JUMP_BRANCH_COPY` block beside `CHIME_IN_GOVERNANCE_COPY` (action label, confirm-step copy, one disabled reason per `JumpDenyReason`, marker copy, relative-time fragments; nothing existing changes). `src/features/debates/index.ts` ŌĆö re-exports the new model, components, and types in a `// GAME-006` block.
- **Implementer copy corrections (within design OD-3 scope ŌĆö `JUMP_BRANCH_COPY` is a single frozen block so wording is a one-spot edit):** `disabled_destination_closed` was authored "...open to join right now." ŌåÆ "...open to join at the moment." (the doctrine ban-list correctly flags the token "right"); `when_unknown` was authored "recently" ŌåÆ "a little while ago" (a single lowercase word trips `looksLikeInternalCode`'s snake-case heuristic ŌĆö the design ┬¦1.6 requires `looksLikeInternalCode` false for every visible string, so the fallback copy is multi-word). No logic change.
- **Doctrine encoded:** a Jump is a STRUCTURAL participation action ŌĆö `JumpBranchRecord` / `JumpEligibility` carry zero verdict words, zero score, zero band; `canJump` reads only seat role, used-jump count, and destination structural state ŌĆö never heat / popularity / reply count / standing (enforced by the forbidden-import test ŌĆö `jumpBranchModel.ts` imports nothing from any score / standing / heat / anti-amplification module). The Jump action is deliberate and CONFIRM-REQUIRED ŌĆö a two-step gate, never an accidental tap (`JumpControlViewModel` carries the confirm copy so the component cannot ship without it; the component test asserts tapping the action does not commit). No silent no-op ŌĆö every disabled state carries a visible plain-language reason. The old branch a participant jumps away from is NEVER deleted or hidden ŌĆö the `departed_from` marker is purely additive. No AI call ŌĆö deterministic pure TS. No notification / alert / push (the arrival is an on-timeline marker ŌĆö push is a v1 scope ban). A jump never changes which seat a participant holds ŌĆö a chime-in who jumps to the mainline is still a `chime_in` seat (GAME-004 governs seats).
- **+82 tests / +5 suites.** Full suite **5730 tests / 210 suites** (**5711 passing** in this bare worktree). Typecheck + lint clean. The 19 failing tests across 5 xAI/bot-fixture suites (`xaiSeededStancesLive`, `xaiAdversarialProvider`, `xaiAdversarialSourceHarvest`, `xaiAdversarialPipeline`, `aiDrivenBotCorpus`) are pre-existing and environmental (the gitignored `.env.engagement-intelligence` is absent from this isolated worktree) ŌĆö unrelated to GAME-006.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client-side code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency. Three operator decisions are isolated and do not gate the build: **OD-1** ŌĆö `MAX_JUMPS_PER_ROOM` shipped at the proposed `1` (a flat per-room cap, no reset); **OD-2** ŌĆö no destination arrival-approval gate in v1 (`destination_needs_approval` exists as an inert future hook only); **OD-3** ŌĆö the `JUMP_BRANCH_COPY` strings shipped pending a copy review.
