## GAME-005 ŌĆö Public room participant seats and chime-in governance (Release 6.7 / Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö a deterministic pure-TS public-room participant-seat + chime-in governance model that extends GAME-004's 1v1 RoomContract and consumes BR-004's branch grammar, plus a thin read-time React layer. Pure client-side ŌĆö no migration, no Edge Function, no Supabase write, no schema change, no AI/network call, no new dependency, no operator step. Issue #142.

- **Why this card exists:** GAME-004 defined the 1v1 OPŌåöPrimary-Opponent spine; GAME-005 lets a public argument room scale past it without (a) drowning that spine, (b) letting the two primaries silence a good challenger, or (c) introducing any popularity-as-evidence / public-shaming / person-verdict mechanic. A public room has a 6-seat active cap ŌĆö seat 1 the Initiator, seat 2 the Primary Opponent, seats 3-6 chime-in participants; everyone past the cap is an observer with no failure state. The two primary parties (and only them) can apply four structural governance reactions; when both mark the same chime-in `off_track` inside a bounded window, that participant moves to observer-only ŌĆö a structural transition, never a "boot".
- **Card-vs-reality decisions (from design ┬¦0, honored verbatim):** (D1) `src/features/rooms/` does not exist ŌĆö the model ships at **`src/features/debates/publicSeatModel.ts`** beside GAME-004's `roomContractModel.ts`; (D3) `debate_participants.side` is CHECK-constrained (`affirmative/negative/observer/moderator`) ŌĆö `chime_in` is a **derived read-time role only**, never a DB value, so GAME-005 ships no migration; (D4) `SeatRole = 'initiator' | 'primary_opponent' | 'chime_in'` reuses GAME-004's `PrimarySeat` vocabulary; (D5) the rule window is a single frozen constant `CHIME_IN_GOVERNANCE_WINDOW_MS = 24h` (OD-1 tunes it); (D7) a frozen `CHIME_IN_GOVERNANCE_COPY` block routes all user-facing labels (OD-2).
- **Deliverables (4 new production files + 5 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/debates/publicSeatModel.ts` ŌĆö **pure TS** (no React / Supabase / network / AI; imports GAME-004 `roomContractModel` types + `isQualifyingResponse`, BR-004 `CollapsedBranchSummary`, and `CHIME_IN_GOVERNANCE_COPY`). `SeatRole`, `PublicSeat`, `ChimeInStanding`, `PublicRoomSeatMap`, `MovedToObserverRecord`, `ObserverFallbackReason`, `GovernanceReaction`, `GovernanceReactionKind`, `ALL_GOVERNANCE_REACTION_KINDS`, `GovernanceDenyReason`, `GovernanceActorResult`, `PublicRoomMetricsViewModel`, `GovernanceControlViewModel`, `PUBLIC_ROOM_SEAT_CAP = 6`, `PRIMARY_SEAT_COUNT = 2`, `CHIME_IN_GOVERNANCE_WINDOW_MS = 24h`, `buildPublicRoomSeatMap` (seats 1-2 from the GAME-004 contract; chime-ins fill 3-6 in first-qualifying-move claim order; 7th+ ŌåÆ overflow; governance fallback recomputed every render), `evaluateChimeInStanding` (returns `observer_only` only when two DISTINCT primaries apply a non-retracted `off_track` within one window span; `useful`/`needs_source`/`move_to_tangent` never demote; a retracted reaction never counts; a 1-element `primaryUserIds` can never demote), `canApplyGovernanceReaction` (actor matrix), `buildPublicRoomMetricsViewModel` / `buildGovernanceControlViewModel`, `governanceReactionLabel`, `_forbiddenChimeInGovernanceTokens`.
  - `src/features/debates/ChimeInGovernanceControl.tsx` ŌĆö read-time RN component, the small constrained governance control shown ONLY to the OP + Primary Opponent on a chime-in branch; four reaction `Pressable`s driven by `GovernanceControlViewModel`; applied state is shape + text (`Ō£ō Applied` tag + filled border), not color alone; Ōēź44px hit targets via `hitSlop`; calm non-punitive observer-fallback notice.
  - `src/features/debates/PublicRoomMetricsStrip.tsx` ŌĆö read-time informational RN strip (seat count, chime-in count, branch-state chips from BR-004 `CollapsedBranchSummary`); no `Pressable`.
  - `src/features/debates/useChimeInGovernance.ts` ŌĆö thin hook holding the in-session `GovernanceReaction[]` with `apply` / `retract` / `toggle`; **no I/O** ŌĆö v1 reactions are ephemeral; `retract` is per-actor and keeps the row (`retracted: true`) for audit, never hard-deletes.
  - 5 new test suites ŌĆö `publicSeatModel` (45), `chimeInGovernanceActorMatrix` (11), `chimeInGovernanceDoctrine` (12), `chimeInGovernanceControl` (15), `publicRoomMetricsStrip` (12) ŌĆö **94 tests**: the seat cap + claim order + 9-swarm overflow + governance fallback, the full `evaluateChimeInStanding` table (single/both/window/same-party/retracted/advisory-kinds/single-primary), the `canApplyGovernanceReaction` actor├Śtarget├Śseat-state matrix (every `GovernanceDenyReason`), retraction reversibility, the ┬¦9 edge cases, determinism + frozen-input safety, the ban-list scan over every produced string, `looksLikeInternalCode` false for every visible string (no `off_track` enum leak), the forbidden-import + no-service-role + no-schema-write source scans, the BR-004 + GAME-004 consumption proof, and the component view-model + a11y render contracts.
- **Modified files (2):** `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` ŌĆö adds the frozen `CHIME_IN_GOVERNANCE_COPY` block beside `BRANCH_GRAMMAR_COPY` (reaction labels, explainers, observer-fallback copy, seat/metrics copy; nothing existing changes). `src/features/debates/index.ts` ŌĆö re-exports the new model, components, hook, and types.
- **Implementer copy correction (within OD-2 scope):** `overflow_observer_body` was reworded "...active seats right now..." ŌåÆ "...active seats at the moment..." ŌĆö the design ┬¦10 ban-list test correctly flags the doctrine token "right". No logic change; the design routes all reaction copy through `CHIME_IN_GOVERNANCE_COPY` precisely so OD-2 wording can be adjusted without touching logic.
- **Doctrine encoded:** a seat describes a structural game ROLE, never the person ŌĆö labels are role-relative; a governance reaction describes participation STRUCTURE, never correctness ŌĆö the four kinds are not votes and carry no verdict; losing a seat (observer-fallback) is a STRUCTURAL TRANSITION, never a penalty ŌĆö a moved-to-observer user keeps every byte of their content on the record and retains full observer rights, and their branch collapses into "Side branches" via BR-004's `buildCollapsedBranchSummary` (never hidden, never deleted). Heat / popularity / reply count / standing are NEVER inputs ŌĆö seat order is the chronological order of the first qualifying move only; `publicSeatModel.ts` imports nothing from any score / standing / heat / anti-amplification module (enforced by the forbidden-import test). The both-parties requirement, the bounded window, and per-actor reversibility are the anti-abuse core; governance pauses when a primary seat is open. No AI call ŌĆö deterministic pure TS. `chime_in` is a derived role only ŌĆö never written to `debate_participants.side`.
- **+94 tests / +5 suites.** Full suite **5648 tests / 205 suites** (**5629 passing** in this bare worktree). Typecheck + lint clean. The 19 failing tests across 5 xAI/bot-fixture suites (`xaiSeededStancesLive`, `xaiAdversarialProvider`, `xaiAdversarialSourceHarvest`, `xaiAdversarialPipeline`, `aiDrivenBotCorpus`) are pre-existing and environmental (the gitignored `.env.engagement-intelligence` is absent from this isolated worktree) ŌĆö unrelated to GAME-005.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client-side code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency. Three operator decisions are isolated and do not gate the build: **OD-1** ŌĆö `CHIME_IN_GOVERNANCE_WINDOW_MS` shipped at the proposed `24h` and `PUBLIC_ROOM_SEAT_CAP` at `6`; **OD-2** ŌĆö the four reaction labels + observer-fallback copy shipped at the proposed values, pending a copy review; **OD-3** ŌĆö a first-class re-entry / appeal UI for moved-to-observer participants is deliberately deferred to a future card (v1's re-entry path is reaction-retraction). A future migration card may add a `public.chime_in_governance_reactions` table to persist reactions across sessions ŌĆö the model is forward-compatible with zero change. Room-shell wiring (mounting the metrics strip + governance control) is a small additive follow-up step.

## BR-004 ŌĆö Branch grammar: mainline, vertical chime-in, diagonal tangent (Release 6.6 / Epic 3 ŌĆö Branches)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö a deterministic pure-TS branch-grammar layer that sits between BR-001's topology classification and the timeline renderer, plus a minimal additive wiring step in the existing timeline map + collapse stub. Pure client-side ŌĆö no migration, no Edge Function, no Supabase write, no AI/network call, no new dependency, no operator step. Issue #143.

- **Why this card exists:** the Timeline Tree appended every move "somewhere" ŌĆö a new participant's chime-in and a topic drift landed structurally indistinguishable from the 1v1 spine. BR-004 defines a teachable **direction grammar** so the board reads at a glance: the **mainline** is the horizontal OPŌåöPrimary 1v1 spine (always the most prominent path), a **chime-in** is a vertical offshoot meaning "a new voice on the same topic", a **tangent** is a diagonal offshoot meaning "a side issue routed off the mainline so it cannot derail it". BR-004 is the grammar + rendering-contract layer ŌĆö it does not detect tangents (BR-003 does) and does not classify topology edges (BR-001 does).
- **Card-vs-reality corrections (from design ┬¦0, honored verbatim):** (D1) `src/features/branches/` does not exist ŌĆö both new files ship at **`src/features/arguments/`** beside `branchTopologyModel.ts` / `tangentRoutingModel.ts`; (D2) `BranchDirection` is BR-004's **own new presentational enum**, kept distinct from BR-001's locked `RailBranchKind` topology enum ŌĆö the `evidence_passthrough` value makes "do not restyle evidence/source branches" a type-level guarantee; (D3) `BranchGrammarNode`'s `lastActivityAt` / `unresolvedAxisCount` are derived deterministically from existing timeline-map fields ŌĆö no per-branch aggregation state, no DB column; (D4) IX-004's readout panel is not modified ŌĆö branch selection resolves to a message id fed into IX-004's existing `activeMessageId` channel; (D5) BR-004 consumes BR-003's `suggestedAction` ŌĆö it never runs `assessTangentRisk`; (D7) the depth cap is a deterministic frozen constant + a non-AI advisory flag.
- **Implementer note (recorded in `docs/designs/BR-004.md`):** the design assumed MCP-010's `SemanticOverrideLane` is an importable merged type. In reality MCP-010 (#165) is a **design-only card** ŌĆö no `SemanticOverrideLane` exists in `src/`. Resolved without redesign: `branchGrammarModel.ts` defines `SemanticOverrideLane = 'mainline' | 'branch' | 'tangent'` locally as a verbatim mirror of MCP-010 ┬¦0's documented vocabulary; `overrideLaneToBranchDirection`'s semantics are exactly as the design specifies. When the MCP-010 implementation card lands a real export the local alias can be re-pointed with no behavior change.
- **Deliverables (2 new production files + 4 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/arguments/branchGrammarModel.ts` ŌĆö **pure TS** (no React / Supabase / network / AI; type-only imports + the frozen `BRANCH_GRAMMAR_COPY` block + `formatRelativeShort`). `BranchDirection` (`mainline | chime_in_vertical | tangent_diagonal | evidence_passthrough`), `ALL_BRANCH_DIRECTIONS`, `BranchOrigin`, `BranchGrammarNode`, `CollapsedBranchSummary`, `BranchSelectionHandoff`, `SemanticOverrideLane` (local mirror), `TANGENT_DEPTH_CAP = 3`, `deriveBranchDirection` (a 5-rule ordered derivation ŌĆö evidence pass-through wins; the mainline is structural; explicit tangent signals from BR-001 topology / a user tag / a BR-003 route / an MCP-010 override draw a diagonal; everything else is a vertical chime-in; reads ONLY structural fields, never heat / popularity / reply count / participant count / recency / strength bands), `buildBranchGrammarMap` (O(n), frozen output, derives `participantCount` / `lastActivityAt` / `unresolvedAxisCount` / `primaryPartyEngaged` / `offshootDepthCapReached` from existing timeline-map data), `buildCollapsedBranchSummary`, `resolveBranchSelectionHandoff`, `suggestedActionToBranchDirection` / `overrideLaneToBranchDirection`, `branchDirectionLabel`, `_forbiddenBranchGrammarTokens`.
  - `src/features/arguments/branchGrammarRenderContract.ts` ŌĆö **pure TS** render-token layer. `BranchDirectionVisual`, `buildBranchDirectionVisual` (maps each direction to VG-001/VG-002's existing shape/position/stroke vocabulary ŌĆö `horizontal`/`vertical_offset`/`diagonal_kink`; `spine`/`bracket`/`kink`; `solid_prominent`/`solid_subordinate`/`dashed` ŌĆö `evidence_passthrough` returns `inherit` for every token; introduces no new color token, shape primitive, or stroke weight), `ALL_BRANCH_*_TOKENS`.
  - 4 new test suites ŌĆö `branchGrammarModel` (~60), `branchGrammarRenderContract` (~18), `branchGrammarNoVerdict` (~9), `branchGrammarSelectionHandoff` (~9) ŌĆö **96 tests**: the `deriveBranchDirection` rule table (rules 1ŌĆō5, tangent via each of the four signals), the doctrine guards (the mainline never auto-promotes ŌĆö a chime-in with 10├Ś the messages stays a chime-in; heat does not move a direction; evidence pass-through priority; an MCP-010 override beats a disagreeing BR-003 route), `buildBranchGrammarMap` aggregation, the offshoot depth cap, the collapsed-summary pluralization, `resolveBranchSelectionHandoff`, the two advisory bridges, determinism + frozen-input safety, edge cases (empty room / root-only / missing-origin fallback / empty principals / inbound-kind absent); the render-token coverage + color-independence (the three non-evidence directions are pairwise-unique on every token axis) + closed-vocabulary; the ban-list scan over every produced string + every `BRANCH_GRAMMAR_COPY` value; the IX-004-shaped hand-off + the no-route + pure-TS static scans.
- **Modified files (3):** `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` ŌĆö adds the `BRANCH_GRAMMAR_COPY` frozen block beside `TANGENT_ROUTING_COPY` (direction labels, explainers, summary fragments, the depth-cap prompt; nothing existing changes). `src/features/arguments/ArgumentTimelineMap.tsx` ŌĆö minimal additive wiring: builds `buildBranchKindMap` + `buildBranchGrammarMap` once per render (memoized on the tree topology, not activity) + a `CollapsedBranchSummary` per collapse stub; a new optional `principalActorLabels` prop feeds `primaryPartyEngaged` (omitting it degrades that field to `false`, never throws); the existing stub-tap ŌåÆ `onActivate` channel is unchanged. `src/features/arguments/BranchCollapseStub.tsx` ŌĆö a new optional, additive `summary` prop: when supplied the stub uses the four-field verbose accessibility label + exposes the summary line; when absent it falls back to BR-001's `+N` label exactly as shipped.
- **Doctrine encoded:** a branch direction describes a move's **structural position**, never its truth / heat / popularity / author ŌĆö `deriveBranchDirection` reads only topology classification, the evidence-thread boolean, explicit qualifier codes, and advisory routing inputs; a chime-in never auto-promotes to the mainline however active it becomes (the mainline is structural by construction). The three directions are distinguishable without color (each carries a pairwise-unique position+shape+stroke triple). `evidence_passthrough` returns `inherit` for every render token ŌĆö BR-004 never restyles an evidence/source branch. Every user-facing string is read from `BRANCH_GRAMMAR_COPY`; the ban-list test scans for verdict / amplification / person-attribution tokens and `looksLikeInternalCode` is false on every visible string ("Side issue", never "wrong" / "dodge"). The depth-cap prompt is advisory copy only ŌĆö BR-004 has no post path, no validation, no block. No AI call ŌĆö deterministic pure TS; the "summarize this offshoot" affordance is a plain-language prompt code, not an AI summary. BR-001's `RailBranchKind`, the BR-003 routing model, MCP-010, RULE-005's channel model, IX-004's panel, and the rules engine are all consumed read-only and untouched.
- **+96 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite **5554 tests / 200 suites** (**5535 passing** in this bare worktree). Typecheck + lint clean. The 19 failing tests across 5 xAI/bot-fixture suites (`xaiSeededStancesLive`, `xaiAdversarialProvider`, `xaiAdversarialSourceHarvest`, `xaiAdversarialPipeline`, `aiDrivenBotCorpus`) are pre-existing and environmental (the gitignored `.env.engagement-intelligence` is absent from this isolated worktree) ŌĆö unrelated to BR-004.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client-side code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency. Two operator decisions are isolated and do not gate the build: **OD-1** ŌĆö `TANGENT_DEPTH_CAP` shipped at the proposed `3`; **OD-2** ŌĆö the direction labels ("Main thread" / "Chime-in" / "Side issue") and the shape/stroke token mapping shipped at the proposed values, pending a `timeline-grammar` token review. A human pass of the four-field collapsed-branch stub summary on Expo web and native is recommended before merge.

## BR-003 ŌĆö Tangent / outer-orbit routing (structural redirect, no person labels) (Release 6.6-adjacent / Epic 3 ŌĆö Branches)

**Status:** Build complete, awaiting Review ŌĆö a deterministic pure-TS tangent-routing model plus an additive one-advisory extension of RULE-004's merged pre-send review. Advisory only ŌĆö it adds zero new blocking rules; no migration, no Edge Function, no persistence, no new dependency, no operator step. Issue #117.

- **Why this card exists:** when a participant's draft does not respond to the point it replies to, picks up a brand-new issue, or shifts the disagreement axis, the app should *offer* to route the move into a side branch ŌĆö keeping the mainline clear without forcing the participant to abandon the structured room. BR-003 builds the deterministic assessment for that offer and surfaces it as ONE advisory inside RULE-004's existing `PreSendReviewSheet`. The user can always continue; nothing is blocked.
- **Card-vs-reality corrections (from design ┬¦0, honored verbatim):** (D1) `src/features/branches/` does not exist ŌĆö the model ships at **`src/features/arguments/tangentRoutingModel.ts`** beside the BR-001 topology model it reads and the RULE-004 model it composes with (the same call RULE-004 ┬¦0 D1 / RULE-005 ┬¦0 D1 made); (D3) no `outer_realm` / `outer_orbit` identifier is introduced even internally ŌĆö the type is `RedirectRisk`, the user-facing term is **"Side issue"**; (D4) `repeated_off_path` is a BR-003-owned `RedirectReason` derived by BR-003's own deterministic counter, not a META-001 code; (D5) "Send to side branch" is *carried, not executed* by BR-003 ŌĆö it routes through RULE-005's existing `branch_tangent` channel + the existing `branch_this_off` qualifier and the unchanged `submit-argument` path, BR-004 is a downstream consumer; (D6) the tangent advisory surfaces *inside* RULE-004's sheet by extending its `AdvisoryKind` union by exactly one member, not as a parallel surface; (D7) the strict-mode "Are you sure?" upgrade is specified but inert in v1 (GAME-003 has not shipped).
- **Deliverables (1 new production file + 4 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/arguments/tangentRoutingModel.ts` ŌĆö **pure TS** (no React / Supabase / network / AI; type-only imports + the frozen `TANGENT_ROUTING_COPY` block). `RedirectRisk` (`none | possible | strong`), `RedirectReason` (5 ŌĆö `introduces_new_axis` / `no_signal_about_parent` / `mode_demands_response` / `repeated_off_path` / `user_marked_tangent`, each describing the move's structural relationship to its parent, never the person), `RedirectSuggestedAction`, `TangentRoutingAssessment` / `AssessTangentRiskInput` / `TangentLifecycleContext` / `TangentThreadContext` / `TangentThreadMove` / `MainlineDemotionAdvisory`, `assessTangentRisk` (a 7-step ordered deterministic derivation ŌĆö first reason wins; reads typed argument type / RULE-005 channel / qualifier tag codes / parent META-001 auto-metadata / parent LIFE-001 axis / BR-001 `RailBranchKind` only ŌĆö never raw body text for keyword matching, never heat / strength / engagement), `countRecentTangentMoves` (BR-003's own per-side off-path counter over BR-001 topology, `REPEATED_OFF_PATH_THRESHOLD = 3`), `buildMainlineDemotionAdvisory` (reversible, person-free ŌĆö names the thread, not the participant), `suggestedActionToQuickAction` (reuses the existing `branch` / `clarify` quick actions ŌĆö adds none), `tangentAdvisoryPlainLanguage` / `tangentReasonPlainLanguage`, `ALL_REDIRECT_RISKS` / `ALL_REDIRECT_REASONS`, `_forbiddenTangentTokens`.
  - 4 new test suites ŌĆö `tangentRoutingModel` (Ōēł70), `tangentRoutingNoPersonLabel` (Ōēł55), `tangentRoutingNoBlock` (Ōēł12), `mainlineDemotion` (Ōēł19): every `assessTangentRisk` derivation step + priority order + every `(risk, reason) ŌåÆ suggestedAction` mapping + root/direct-move fast paths + null tolerance + determinism + the copy resolvers + `ALL_*` exhaustiveness; the ban-list scan over every produced string (no verdict / amplification / block / person-attribution token, no snake_case leak); the advisory-never-blocks guarantee (`risk: possible` / `strong` never produce a `PreSendStructuralBlock`, "Post anyway" always offered) + the byte-identical regression guard for an omitted / null / none-yielding `tangentContext`; the `repeated_off_path` threshold boundary + reversal with no persisted flag + the deterministic-no-AI, no-keyword-on-body, and no-heat doctrine guarantees.
- **Modified files (3):** `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` ŌĆö adds the `TANGENT_ROUTING_COPY` frozen block beside `PRESEND_ADVISORY_COPY` (move-level / thread-level copy, never person-level; nothing existing changes). `src/features/arguments/preSendReviewModel.ts` ŌĆö `AdvisoryKind` + `ALL_ADVISORY_KINDS` gain `tangent_redirect`; `ADVISORY_DEFINITIONS` gains one `soft` entry; `PreSendReviewInput` gains one optional `tangentContext` field; `buildPreSendReview` gains derivation step 9 (calls `assessTangentRisk`, appends a `tangent_redirect` advisory when `risk` is `possible` / `strong`, suppresses it under the `asks_new_question` de-dup rule). When `tangentContext` is omitted the review is byte-identical to merged RULE-004. `__tests__/preSendReviewModel.test.ts` + `__tests__/preSendReviewBanList.test.ts` ŌĆö extended for the new step-9 derivation, the de-dup rule, and to exercise the new advisory kind. `PreSendReviewSheet.tsx` is **not** modified ŌĆö its generic advisory loop renders the new kind.
- **Doctrine encoded:** BR-003 adds **zero** new blocking rules ŌĆö `tangent_redirect` is `severity: 'soft'`; the only thing that hides "Post anyway" is a pre-existing `evaluateArgumentDraft` structural block. "Structural redirect, no person labels" ŌĆö every `RedirectReason` describes the move's relationship to its parent; the copy describes "this move" / "the thread"; the mainline-demotion advisory names the thread, never the participant; the ban-list test enforces zero verdict / person-attribution tokens. No keyword-only gating ŌĆö `assessTangentRisk` reads typed structural fields only, and a test proves charged vs benign bodies of equal structure yield identical assessments. No heat / popularity / strength / engagement input ŌĆö a test proves identical-structure / different-mock-heat parents get identical assessments. No AI call ŌĆö deterministic pure TS (the semantic AI tangent classifier is explicitly RULE-006). Soft-delete only ŌĆö routing a move to a side branch posts it *as a branch* (collapsed-capable, fully accessible); mainline demotion is reversible with no persisted flag. Every string is read from `TANGENT_ROUTING_COPY`; no snake_case leak.
- **+139 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite **5458 tests / 196 suites** (**5439 passing** in this bare worktree). Typecheck + lint clean. The ~19 failing tests across the xAI/bot-fixture suites (`xaiSeededStancesLive`, `xaiAdversarialProvider`, `xaiAdversarialSourceHarvest`, `xaiAdversarialPipeline`, `aiDrivenBotCorpus`) are pre-existing and environmental (the gitignored `.env.engagement-intelligence` is absent from this isolated worktree) ŌĆö unrelated to BR-003.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client-side code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency. BR-003 produces no new visible component (the advisory renders through RULE-004's existing sheet); a human pass of the `tangent_redirect` advisory card inside the pre-send review sheet on Expo web and native is recommended before merge once a caller assembles `tangentContext`. The strict-mode "Are you sure?" upgrade and a dedicated always-on "thread has drifted" banner remain inert / future-card scope (design ┬¦6 / OD-2).

## RULE-004 ŌĆö Pause-before-send move review (advisory friction with payoff) (Release 6.6 / Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX / composer)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö a deterministic pure-TS pre-send review model + a thin presentational sheet shown by the COMPOSER-002 dock on the Post intent. Advisory only ŌĆö it adds zero new blocking rules; no migration, no Edge Function, no persistence, no new dependency, no operator step. Issue #114.

- **Why this card exists:** CDiscourse keeps a permanent record, and the most valuable friction point for civil-discourse quality is *before* the move leaves. A user about to post a sweeping claim, drift off the resolution, attach an "Evidence" move with no source, or open a brand-new question inside someone else's thread should get one short, non-judgemental review chance ŌĆö and that pause must always hand back something useful (a narrower framing, a branch, a source field, the option to save a draft). RULE-004 builds the structural scaffolding for that pause.
- **Card-vs-reality corrections (from design ┬¦0, honored verbatim):** (D1) `src/features/composer/` does not exist ŌĆö both new files ship at **`src/features/arguments/`** beside the other composer files (the same call RULE-005 ┬¦0 D1 made); (D2) `structuralBlocks[]` is **not produced** by RULE-004 ŌĆö it is a read-only projection of `evaluateArgumentDraft`'s already-computed `blockingErrors` (RULE-004 implements no block, invents no rule); (D3) GAME-003's strict mode has not shipped ŌĆö `mode` is a typed parameter (`'casual' | 'strict'`) for forward-compat but is **always `'casual'`** in v1; the strict branch is fully specified + unit-tested but inert (OD-1); (D4) `cooldown_active` is a **reserved** `StructuralBlockKind` with no v1 producer ŌĆö GAME-002's pacing is advisory-only today (OD-2); (D6) the `channel_mismatch` advisory **absorbs** RULE-005's already-shipped channel-mismatch ŌĆö RULE-004 reuses RULE-005's `suggestChannelFromDraft` / `ChannelSuggestion` and modifies neither `channelModel.ts` nor `ChannelChipRow.tsx`; (D7) `asks_new_question`'s transformation is `branch_tangent` (not a non-existent `ask_question` preset).
- **Deliverables (2 new production files + 4 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/arguments/preSendReviewModel.ts` ŌĆö **pure TS** (no React / Supabase / network / AI; type-only imports + frozen gameCopy tables). `AdvisoryKind` (7 ŌĆö `broad_claim` / `topic_drift` / `asks_new_question` / `no_source_attached` / `depth_warning` / `permanent_record_warning` / `channel_mismatch`), `AdvisorySeverity` (exactly `'info' | 'soft'` ŌĆö no blocking severity), `AdvisoryTransformation`, `StructuralBlockKind`, `ReviewMode`, `PreSendReview` / `PreSendReviewInput`, `ADVISORY_DEFINITIONS` + `advisoryDefinition`, `buildPreSendReview` (an 8-rule ordered deterministic derivation ŌĆö block projection, then the 7 advisory rules), `projectBlockKind` (maps an existing `FLAG_CODES` blocking code to a display kind; unknown ŌåÆ `invalid_transition`), `transformationToQuickAction` (maps onto existing `QuickActionLabel`s ŌĆö adds none), `channelMismatchPlainLanguage`, `ALL_ADVISORY_KINDS`, `_forbiddenPreSendTokens`. The one body read is a deterministic **length / `?`-shape** read ŌĆö never keyword gating.
  - `src/features/arguments/PreSendReviewSheet.tsx` ŌĆö thin presentational overlay (scrim + a panel above the composer body, NOT a nested RN `<Modal>`, so the composer stays mounted and the draft is never lost). Renders the structural-block section first (with "Post anyway" hidden when a block is present), then the advisory cards with their actionable transformation buttons, and the footer "Post anyway" / "Save draft" / "Back to editing". Exports pure helpers (`isPostAnywayVisible`, `isPostAnywayEnabled`, `transformationButtonLabel`, `buildAdvisoryAccessibilityLabel`, `actionableTransformations`) for the UI test suite. Accessibility: button roles + labels + a Ōēź 44├Ś44 hit target on every Pressable; severity spoken as a word and shown via a glyph (color is not the only signal); the sheet snaps (no enter animation) so it is reduce-motion safe; `accessibilityViewIsModal`. The strict-mode per-advisory dismiss branch is built + reachable for tests but inert in v1.
  - 4 new test suites ŌĆö `preSendReviewModel` (42), `preSendReviewBanList` (7), `preSendReviewNoBlockOnKeywords` (15), `preSendReviewSheetUi` (20) ŌĆö 84 tests: the per-rule derivation table for all 8 rules, `ADVISORY_DEFINITIONS` coverage, `projectBlockKind` / `transformationToQuickAction`, clean / root / null-evaluation edge cases, determinism, the casual/strict severity split; the doctrine ban-list over every produced advisory / block / sheet string + the non-punitive (no dodge / evade) + honest-`permanent_record_warning` (no fear token) requirements; the no-keyword-block guarantee (charged vs benign bodies of equal shape give identical advisories), the heat-independence guarantee, the `AdvisorySeverity`-is-exactly-`info|soft` guarantee, the advisory-never-hides-"Post anyway" guarantee; and the sheet's pure helpers + a source scan (button roles, hit slop, "Post anyway" gated on `isPostAnywayVisible`, color-independent section markers, reduce-motion snap, dock wiring with no AI / no service-role, `channel_mismatch` absorbed, `mode: 'casual'`).
- **Modified files (3):** `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` ŌĆö adds `PRESEND_ADVISORY_COPY` / `PRESEND_BLOCK_COPY` / `PRESEND_SHEET_COPY` frozen blocks (nothing existing changes). `src/features/arguments/ArgumentComposer.tsx` ŌĆö two additive optional props: `onBeforeSubmit` (the Post-intent gate ŌĆö return `false` to suppress the composer's own submit) and `postSignal` (a one-shot "Post anyway" counter ŌĆö the `bypassReview` recommendation of OD-3, no `useImperativeHandle`); every existing caller that omits them behaves identically and the `evaluateArgumentDraft` / `submit-argument` path is untouched. `src/features/arguments/ArgumentComposerDock.tsx` ŌĆö owns the review state, builds the `PreSendReview` on the Post intent from the active draft (read from session) + the already-computed Constitution evaluation, renders `<PreSendReviewSheet>`, wires Post anyway / Save draft / Back to editing / advisory-transformation handlers, and passes RULE-005's existing `channelSuggestion` into `buildPreSendReview` so `channel_mismatch` is absorbed, not duplicated.

No keyword-only gating ŌĆö the body is read for length / `?`-shape only, and a test proves charged vs benign bodies of equal shape yield identical reviews. No heat / popularity / strength / reply-count input ŌĆö a test proves identical-structure / different-mock-heat parents get identical reviews. No AI call ŌĆö deterministic pure TS (RULE-006 owns semantic advisories). Every advisory / block / sheet string is read from a frozen `gameCopy` block; the ban-list test scans for verdict / amplification / block / punitive / fear tokens and asserts no internal-code leak; the `permanent_record_warning` copy is honest ("Posted moves stay on the record. Take a beat if you need it.") ŌĆö never fear-based. `preSendReviewModel.ts` imports types only. RULE-005's `channelModel.ts` / `ChannelChipRow.tsx` and the Constitution engine / `FLAG_CODES` are untouched.

The 19 failing tests across 5 xAI/bot-fixture suites (`xaiSeededStancesLive`, `xaiAdversarialProvider`, `xaiAdversarialSourceHarvest`, `xaiAdversarialPipeline`, `aiDrivenBotCorpus`) are pre-existing and environmental (the gitignored `.env.engagement-intelligence` is absent from this isolated worktree) ŌĆö unrelated to RULE-004.

## RULE-005 ŌĆö Structured argument channels (move-type field model) (Release 6.6 / Epic 12 ŌĆö Rules UX / composer)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö a thin, plain-language "channel" layer above the 8 Constitution argument types. Pure-TS model + two presentational components wired into the COMPOSER-002 dock; no migration, no Edge Function, no persistence, no new dependency, no operator step. Issue #115.

- **Why this card exists:** the room exposed argument **types** (the 8 Constitution types) and a move **navigator** (`conversationMoves.ts`), both of which describe what the rules engine validates. RULE-005 adds a layer *above* that: **channels** ŌĆö a small vocabulary describing the *structural purpose* of a move ("you are challenging", "you are asking for a source", "you are conceding a narrow point") so the composer can (a) deterministically suggest the channel that fits the draft + parent and (b) optionally reveal helper fields. A channel is never a verdict ŌĆö it labels what a move *does*, never whether it is right, popular, or strong.
- **Card-vs-reality corrections (from design ┬¦0, honored verbatim):** (D1) `src/features/composer/` does not exist ŌĆö the model ships at **`src/features/arguments/channelModel.ts`** beside the other composer models; (D2) `PreSendReviewSheet` / RULE-004 is not built ŌĆö the channel-mismatch advisory ships **inline** in the dock chip row, forward-compatible with RULE-004 (OD-1); (D3) META-001's `ManualTagCode` vocabulary is **locked** ŌĆö the channel is a **draft-time advisory field** that does NOT persist; a posted move's channel is re-derived at render time (OD-2); (D4) the `MoveChannel` enum ships **12 active channels + 2 reserved** (`evidence_interaction` ŌåÆ EV-005, `mode_specific` ŌåÆ GAME-003 ŌĆö stub definitions, never suggested in v1); (D5) the `mode` parameter is accepted for GAME-003 forward-compat but never changes the suggestion in v1; (D6) `suggestChannelFromDraft` reads the **parent's** already-derived LIFE-001 / META-001 surface plus the draft's own typed fields ŌĆö it invents no draft-level deriver.
- **Deliverables (3 new production files + 5 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/arguments/channelModel.ts` ŌĆö **pure TS** (no React / Supabase / network / AI; type-only imports + the frozen gameCopy tables). `MoveChannel` (12 + 2), `ALL_MOVE_CHANNELS` / `ACTIVE_MOVE_CHANNELS` / `RESERVED_MOVE_CHANNELS`, `CHANNEL_DEFINITIONS` + `channelDefinition`, `suggestChannelFromDraft` (a 6-rule ordered deterministic derivation ŌĆö type match / tangent qualifier / parent-demands-evidence / lifecycle-state / plain-reply / no-signal ŌĆö first match wins, no body-text inspection), `channelToDraftPatch` (mirrors `mapMoveToDraftPatch`; reuses the now-exported `resolveChallengeType`), `deriveChannelForPostedMove` (render-time reverse map sharing one private `classifyByTypeAndTags` helper with the forward map so they cannot drift), `_forbiddenChannelTokens`.
  - `src/features/arguments/ChannelChipRow.tsx` ŌĆö horizontally-scrolling single-select radio group of channel chips. The suggested chip carries a text "Suggested" affordance + a heavier border (never color alone); a one-line rationale renders under the row; a non-punitive re-route advisory with a "Switch channel" action appears only on a mismatch. `accessibilityRole="radio"` + `accessibilityState` + `accessibilityLabel` (incl. "suggested") + 44├Ś44 hit target. Load-bearing decisions extracted into pure helpers.
  - `src/features/arguments/ChannelHelperFields.tsx` ŌĆö collapsed optional-field block; one labelled `TextInput` per `ChannelOptionalField`; renders nothing for a no-field channel (`meta_process` / `concede` / `branch_tangent`). Fields are advisory in casual mode (v1) ŌĆö leaving one empty never blocks a post.
  - 5 new test suites ŌĆö `channelModel`, `channelSuggestionDerivation`, `channelNoKeywordBlock`, `channelCopyBanList`, `ChannelChipRow` (123 tests): the vocabulary + definitions + `channelToDraftPatch` per channel, the full 6-rule derivation table + isMismatch + determinism + forward/reverse parity, the advisory-not-block guarantee (no `structuralBlock` field, no body field on the input, identical suggestions for identical-structure / different-heat parents), the doctrine ban-list over every produced string + the branch_tangent non-punitive requirement, and the chip-row / helper-field pure helpers (suggested affordance, accessibility labels, advisory visibility, hit target).
- **Modified files (3):** `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` ŌĆö adds `CHANNEL_LABEL_COPY` / `CHANNEL_PURPOSE_COPY` / `CHANNEL_RATIONALE_COPY` frozen blocks; channel codes are deliberately distinct from existing `PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY` keys (`synthesize` ŌēĀ `synthesis`, `branch_tangent` ŌēĀ `tangent`) so no key collides. `src/features/arguments/conversationMoves.ts` ŌĆö exports `resolveChallengeType` (a 1-word `export`) so the channel model reuses the single rebuttal/counter_rebuttal resolution. `src/features/arguments/ArgumentComposerDock.tsx` ŌĆö renders `ChannelChipRow` below the handle strip, holds `selectedChannel` in dock-local state (OD-3 ŌĆö the smaller diff, no `MoveDraftPatch` change), calls `suggestChannelFromDraft`, and merges `channelToDraftPatch` onto the caller `initialPatch`; the COMPOSER-001 preset round trip is preserved (the merged `composerInitialPatch` equals the caller `initialPatch` when no channel is picked).
- **One existing test updated:** `__tests__/composerDockPresetWiring.test.ts` had a source-scan asserting the dock forwards `initialPatch={initialPatch}` verbatim ŌĆö RULE-005 deliberately forwards the merged `composerInitialPatch`. The test now asserts the new wiring and that the merge falls back to the caller `initialPatch` when no channel is picked; the COMPOSER-001 preset invariant is unchanged.
- **Doctrine encoded:** a channel describes a move's *structural purpose*, never its truth or strength ŌĆö `ChannelSuggestion` has no blocking field; `suggestChannelFromDraft` cannot prevent a post; a mismatch is an advisory the user may ignore. The suggestion reads `argumentType`, qualifier codes, and the parent's *structural* lifecycle state only ŌĆö never heat, strength bands, reply counts as popularity, or engagement (a test feeds two identical-structure parents with different mock activity counts and asserts identical suggestions). Deterministic ŌĆö no Anthropic / xAI / Edge Function (RULE-006 owns AI channel detection). Every label / purpose / rationale is read from `gameCopy`; the ban-list test scans every produced string for verdict / amplification / block tokens and asserts the `branch_tangent` copy is non-punitive (no dodge / evade). `channelModel.ts` imports types only. META-001's locked vocabulary is untouched.
- **+123 tests / +5 suites.** Full suite **5235 tests / 188 suites** (**5216 passing** in this bare worktree). Typecheck + lint clean. The 19 failing tests across 5 xAI/bot-fixture suites (`xaiSeededStancesLive`, `xaiAdversarialProvider`, `xaiAdversarialSourceHarvest`, `xaiAdversarialPipeline`, `aiDrivenBotCorpus`) are pre-existing and environmental (the gitignored `.env.engagement-intelligence` is absent from this isolated worktree) ŌĆö unrelated to RULE-005.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client-side code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency. RULE-005 is a visible-UI card; a human pass of the channel chip row + helper fields (suggested affordance, re-route advisory, 44├Ś44 targets, reduce-motion, the collapsed helper-field disclosure) on Expo web and native is recommended before merge. **OD-2** (a persisted `arguments.channel` column distinct from the re-derivation) remains a future migration card if the product needs the author's *stated* channel intent preserved.

## META-1C ŌĆö Admin metadata-event audit log surface (Release 6.8 / Rules UX ŌĆö Metadata / admin)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö a new admin **Metadata Events** tab that lists META-1A `point_tags` manual-tag events chronologically for a selected debate. Pure client-side admin-RLS read; no migration, no Edge Function, no new dependency. Issue #78.

- **Why this card exists:** META-1A persisted the manual-tag vocabulary as `public.point_tags` (a participant marking a move `needs_source` / `tangent` / etc. writes a durable row with a `created_at` apply moment and a nullable `removed_at` soft-delete moment). META-1C adds the admin investigation surface that consumes that table ŌĆö an evidence trail for tag-misuse reports ("who keeps spam-tagging room X").
- **Card-vs-reality corrections (from the design doc ┬¦0):** the card asked for a `list-metadata-events` Edge Function + an admin-only RLS migration + a "lifecycle transition" filter chip + an apply-time actor role. The design corrected all four: (1) **no Edge Function** ŌĆö the established repo pattern is a direct caller-scoped admin-RLS read (`AdminArgumentsTab` / `adminArgumentsApi`), and an Edge Function that only does a caller-scoped SELECT is a redundant deploy dependency with no security benefit; (2) **no migration** ŌĆö admins can already SELECT every `point_tags` row transitively via the `arguments` RLS admin clause; (3) the **applied-vs-removed** chip replaces the dropped "lifecycle transition" chip (auto-metadata / lifecycle-causation events are render-time-derived in memory and were never persisted ŌĆö nothing to audit); (4) the actor-role column shows the actor's **current** role (`profiles.role` + their `debate_participants.side`), honestly labeled "current role" with a legend ŌĆö `point_tags` stores no apply-time role and META-1C must not fabricate one.
- **Deliverables (3 new production files + 2 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/admin/adminMetadataEventsApi.ts` ŌĆö the data layer. Caller-scoped `point_tags` select with embedded `arguments` / `debates` / dual-`profiles` (tagger + remover, disambiguated by FK constraint name) joins; the **pure `expandPointTagRowToEvents` adapter** that expands each `point_tags` row into 1 `applied` event (always) + 1 `removed` event (when `removed_at` is set); a `debate_participants` actor-side enrichment query; `sortMetadataAuditEvents` (post-expansion chronological sort ŌĆö required because a `removed` event's `occurredAt` is `removed_at`); `loadAuditDebateOptions` + `dedupeDebateOptions` for the debate selector. No `createClient`, no service-role, no `.rpc` bypass, no write path.
  - `src/features/admin/adminMetadataEventsView.ts` ŌĆö **pure TS** view-model helpers: `filterMetadataAuditEvents` (tag-code / actor-role / event-kind / search composition), `formatActorRole` (honest current-role labels ŌĆö `Admin` / `Moderator` / `Participant ┬Ę Affirmative` / `Participant` / `ŌĆö`, never a fabricated side), `eventMatchesRoleFilter`, the `AuditRoleFilter` vocabulary + labels.
  - `src/features/admin/AdminMetadataEventsTab.tsx` ŌĆö the tab component. Debate-selector chip strip, three filter-chip rows (tag code / actor role / event kind), sortable Created column, horizontally-scrollable column table, loading / error / empty / filtered-empty / no-debate states, the honest actor-role legend, the fact-only footnote. The applied/removed badge distinguishes by **text + border shape** (solid vs dashed), not color alone; chips meet the 44├Ś44 hit target; every interactive element carries `accessibilityRole` + `accessibilityLabel` + `accessibilityState`.
  - 2 new test suites ŌĆö `adminMetadataEventsApi`, `adminMetadataEventsTab` (91 tests): the pure adapter across applied-only / applied+removed / null-remover / bad-code / malformed-row / soft-deleted-argument / cross-debate / body-truncation cases, the committed select-string shape, the loader call shape + post-expansion sort + actor-side enrichment, the view-model filters / sort / role formatting, the component source-scan (testIDs, a11y attributes, status states, legend, footnote), and the doctrine ban-list.
- **Modified files (2):** `src/features/admin/types.ts` ŌĆö `AdminTab` union + `ADMIN_TAB_LABELS` extended with `metadata_events: 'Metadata Events'`. `src/features/admin/AdminScreen.tsx` ŌĆö `metadata_events` added to the `TABS` array + the import + the render branch.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the surface states neutral facts ŌĆö who applied/removed a tag, when, on which move ŌĆö and renders no verdict about any person (the footnote says so verbatim; a ban-list test scans model-emitted strings + user-facing copy against `_forbiddenMetadataTokens()`). No heat / popularity input, no count-weighting, no ranking ŌĆö events are listed chronologically only. All tag labels go through `getManualTagPlainLabel` ŌåÆ `gameCopy.PLAIN_LANGUAGE_COPY`; no raw `tag_code` reaches a user-facing string; no new copy token. Access is enforced by existing admin RLS (`pt_select_read_access` deferring to the `arguments` admin clause); no service-role anywhere in client code; the surface is read-only ŌĆö zero writes to `point_tags`.
- **+91 tests / +2 suites.** Full suite **5112 tests / 183 suites** (**5093 passing** in this bare worktree). The 19 failing tests across 5 xAI/bot-fixture suites (`xaiSeededStancesLive`, `xaiAdversarialProvider`, `xaiAdversarialSourceHarvest`, `xaiAdversarialPipeline`, `aiDrivenBotCorpus`) are pre-existing and environmental (the gitignored `.env.engagement-intelligence` is absent from this isolated worktree) ŌĆö unrelated to META-1C. Typecheck + lint clean.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no Edge Function, no dependency. META-1C ships live on merge (provided META-1A's migration is already applied to the target environment ŌĆö it must be, since META-1A is merged). A post-merge admin RLS smoke (an admin sees the global per-debate event list incl. both `Applied` and `Removed` rows for a soft-deleted tag; a non-admin reaching the tab sees only their own visible debates' tags) is recommended; META-1C is a visible-UI card, so a human pass of the tab on Expo web and native is advised before merge.

## SC-005 ŌĆö Collapsed observer action dock and contextual pop-outs (Epic 4 / Sidecars, Popovers, Quick Tools / argument-room)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö the observer action set renders as a single collapsed contextual dock instead of a dense flex-wrap grid plus a separate bottom actionBar. LAYOUT only; no migration, no Edge Function, no new dependency. Issue #112.

- **Why this card exists:** the argument room rendered the observer action set as a flex-wrap grid of full-width buttons (helper text on every button) and *also* a separate bottom `actionBar` for "Start an argument" ŌĆö together ~30% of vertical space on a phone, pushing the active timeline node off-screen. SC-005 keeps the exact Stage 6.4 action-set definitions and the SC-001 category taxonomy unchanged and only changes *layout*.
- **Deliverables (1 new production file + 5 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/arguments/ObserverActionDockLayout.ts` ŌĆö **pure TS** (no React / Supabase / network / AI; type-only re-use from `ArgumentSideActionRail`). Exports `DockLayoutVariant` / `DockExpansionState` / `DockContext` / `CollapsedDockLabel` / `DockCategorySection` / `ExpandedDockViewModel`; the functions `resolveObserverDockVariant` (mirrors `resolveDockLayoutVariant`: width Ōēż 0 / non-finite ŌåÆ `'side'`, 0 < width < 720 ŌåÆ `'sheet'`, Ōēź 720 ŌåÆ `'side'`), `deriveDockContext`, `buildCollapsedDockLabel` (the four collapsed primaries ŌĆö "Watch" / "Actions on this point" / "On your message" / "Reply"), `buildExpandedDockViewModel` (wraps `groupRailActionsByCategory`, computes `showCategoryHeaders` = Ōēź 2 non-empty sections + the verbatim Stage 6.4 dock title), and `resolveSheetMaxHeightPx` (28% of the viewport, clamped to a 168 px floor, never Ōēź the viewport height).   - 5 new test suites ŌĆö `sideActionDockCollapsed`, `sideActionDockCategoryGrouping`, `sideActionDockMatrix`, `sideActionDockA11y`, `sideActionDockNoVerdictCopy` (63 tests): the breakpoint resolver / four-way context derivation / sheet-height cap, category ordering + empty-category suppression, the Stage 6.4 action-set regression lock (own-bubble stays `[qualifiers, request_deletion]` only), the accessibility contract (44px targets, roles/labels/states, header role on category headers, reduce-motion = no slide, web Escape), and the doctrine ban-list scan over every visible dock string + `looksLikeInternalCode`.
- **Modified files (4):** `src/features/arguments/ArgumentSideActionRail.tsx` ŌĆö the Stage 6.4 action-set definitions (`RailActionCode` ŌĆ” `railActionToBubbleControl`) stay byte-for-byte unchanged; only the collapsed + expanded render is rewritten ŌĆö a context-aware collapsed pill, an ordered list of category sections (headers only when Ōēź 2 non-empty), short-label-only chips with helper demoted to `accessibilityHint` + a transient long-press hint line, a `ScrollView` body inside the 28% sheet cap, the reduce-motion `AccessibilityInfo` read + `Animated` slide (snap when reduced or side-anchored), and a web Escape keydown listener. `src/features/arguments/ArgumentGameSurface.tsx` ŌĆö passes viewport size / reduce-motion / `hasSelectedNode` (an explicit SC-002/SC-004 node selection) / `isAnyPanelOpen` / the `startArgumentAction` CTA to the rail, and enforces one-open-at-a-time exclusion with the timeline node selection. `src/features/arguments/ArgumentTreeScreen.tsx` ŌĆö threads the optional `startArgumentAction` prop through to `ArgumentGameSurface` (one pass-through per intermediate, the existing pattern). `App.tsx` ŌĆö the separate bottom `actionBar` block and its four styles are deleted; the "Start an argument" CTA folds into the rail's expanded dock as `startArgumentAction`.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the dock surfaces *moves*, never verdicts ŌĆö the four collapsed labels and the category headers are activity words (`sideActionDockNoVerdictCopy.test.ts` scans every visible string against the ban-list and `looksLikeInternalCode`). The dock reads only `viewerRole` / `bubbleActor` / `participantSide` / `hasSelectedNode` / viewport size ŌĆö never heat, lifecycle, score bands; "Actions on this point" describes *selection*, never *standing*. The own-bubble matrix stays `[qualifiers, request_deletion]` only (no edit / disagree / flag / score). No AI call, no service-role, no migration, no Edge Function, no `.env`, no new dependency.
- **Implementer decisions:** (1) **Path A** taken for the App.tsx actionBar fold ŌĆö the prop chain (`ArgumentTreeScreen` ŌåÆ `FullRoomGameSurfaceMount` ŌåÆ `ArgumentGameSurface` ŌåÆ `ArgumentSideActionRail`) already forwards several optional pass-through props, so threading `startArgumentAction` is the same one-line-per-file pattern; the separate bottom bar is gone. (2) The design floated a parent-owned `railExpanded` boolean in `ArgumentGameSurface`; the rail is the source of truth for its own expansion and self-collapses via the `isAnyPanelOpen` prop, so the parent only clears the SC-002/SC-004 node target on rail-expand ŌĆö no dead duplicated state. (3) The rail keeps its `collapsed` `useState` (rather than the design's suggested `expanded` rename) so the SC-001 contract-lock `railActionGrouping.test.ts` regex (`useState(initialCollapsed)`) stays green with zero changes; SC-005 dock semantics treat `expanded = !collapsed && !isAnyPanelOpen`.
- **One existing test updated:** `__tests__/composerDockInRoom.test.ts` had a COMPOSER-002 positional assertion ("the dock is rendered after the action bar") that anchored on `styles.actionBar` ŌĆö which SC-005 deliberately deletes. The assertion now anchors on the room surface (`<ArgumentTreeScreen>`); the COMPOSER-002 invariant (the dock is a sibling inside the room view, after the room surface) is unchanged.

## GAME-004 ŌĆö 1v1 PvP room contract and Primary Opponent model (Epic 12 / Game Rules / argument-room)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö a deterministic, derived 1v1 room contract + a read-time seat strip in `DebateDetailHeader`. Pure model + read-only UI; no migration, no persistence, no Edge Function, no new dependency. Issue #141.

- **Why this card exists:** a room had `debate_participants` rows with sides and a Stage 6.4 observer/participant split, but no notion of *who the two primary parties are*. Every later PvP card (GAME-005 chime-in seats, BR-004 branch governance, GAME-007 resolution) needs a well-defined two-party contract so "whose move is it" and "who governs the mainline" are answerable. GAME-004 defines that contract and the Primary Opponent assignment rule.
- **Deliverables (3 new production files + 3 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/debates/roomContractModel.ts` ŌĆö **pure TS**, no React / Supabase / network / AI / score / heat import (JSON-serializable). Exports `RoomType` (`'private' | 'public'`), `PrimarySeat` (`'initiator' | 'primary_opponent'`), `RoomContract`, the input/view-model types, and the functions `buildRoomContract`, `resolvePrimaryOpponent` (the single source of truth for the opponent seat), `isQualifyingResponse` + `explainQualifyingResponse` (deterministic predicate ŌĆö a qualifying response is a real mainline argumentative move, not spam / a bare flag-carrying move / an off-topic one-liner / an immediately-deletion-requested move / a bot move / the Initiator's own move), `isPrimaryOpponentSeatStale` (advisory inactivity detector), `buildRoomContractViewModel`. Constants: `ROOM_TYPE_DEFAULT` (`'public'`), `PRIMARY_OPPONENT_INACTIVITY_MS` (72h), `MIN_QUALIFYING_BODY_CHARS` (40 ŌĆö the anti-sniping body-length gate), `MAINLINE_RESPONSE_TYPES`, `SEAT_BLOCKING_FLAG_CODES`, and the frozen `ROOM_CONTRACT_COPY`.
  - `src/features/debates/RoomContractSeatStrip.tsx` ŌĆö read-time presentational RN component (`View` + `Text` only, no `Pressable`, no new dependency). Renders a room-type chip (shape/text glyph, not color alone), two role-only seat pills (`You` / `Initiator` / `Opponent` / `Open seat ŌĆö first reply takes it`), and a turn label. Strip root carries an `accessibilityLabel`.
  - `src/features/debates/useRoomContract.ts` ŌĆö thin **read-only** hook: one RLS-bound `select` on `debate_participants` + `listArgumentsForDebate`, then builds the pure contract + view-model. No insert/update, no service-role, no Edge Function. A read failure returns `viewModel: null` ŌåÆ the header degrades to its prior render.
  - 3 new test suites ŌĆö `roomContractModel`, `roomContractSeatStrip`, `roomContractDoctrine` (67 tests): the full `resolvePrimaryOpponent` edge table (spam-first / flag-first / deletion-first / off-topic-first / OP-self / bot-first never claim the seat; invited-private overrides post order; private-without-invite falls through; `id` tie-break), the full `isQualifyingResponse` predicate table incl. the 39/40-char boundary, `buildRoomContract` / `buildRoomContractViewModel` / `isPrimaryOpponentSeatStale`, determinism, no-mutation, the anti-griefing assertion that no `reject`/`set`/`override` function exists, the ban-list across all viewer permutations, and the forbidden-import / no-service-role scan.
- **Modified files (3):** `src/features/debates/DebateDetailHeader.tsx` ŌĆö one new **optional** prop `roomContract?`; absent ŌåÆ the header is byte-identical to before (no existing caller or test affected). `App.tsx` ŌĆö calls `useRoomContract` at the room mount (unconditionally, Rules-of-Hooks-safe; an empty `roomId` makes the hook a no-op) and threads the projection into the header. `src/features/debates/index.ts` ŌĆö barrel re-exports.
- **Doctrine encoded:** seat labels describe a game ROLE relative to the viewer, never the person, never a verdict word (`roomContractDoctrine.test.ts` ban-list). The contract carries no score, no band, no heat ŌĆö `roomContractModel.ts` imports nothing from any score / standing / heat module (forbidden-import test). The model is derived on every load, never persisted, so it cannot drift on a stale column. There is **no write path** ŌĆö no re-open mutation, no "set opponent", no "reject opponent"; the Initiator cannot reject a qualifying first responder (anti-griefing default, encoded by the deliberate absence of any such function). No AI call, no service-role, no migration, no Edge Function, no `.env`, no new dependency.
- **Scope notes:** `roomType` has no persisted source in v1 ŌĆö it is a caller-supplied input defaulting to `'public'` (the doctrine-safe direction: a public room leaves the opponent seat open and claimable; a wrong `'private'` guess would freeze it). A future migration card adds `debates.room_type` and threads the real value through `BuildRoomContractInput` ŌĆö the model is unchanged when it does. Public chime-in seats (GAME-005), branch grammar (BR-004), resolution / enough-tags (GAME-007), turn *pacing* (GAME-002 ŌĆö GAME-004 ships only a minimal turn label), and bot-vs-human seats (GAME-008) are out of scope.
- **+67 tests / +3 suites.** Full suite **4958 tests / 176 suites** (**4939 passing**). Typecheck + lint clean. The 19 failing tests across 5 xAI/bot-fixture suites (`xaiSeededStancesLive`, `xaiAdversarialProvider`, `xaiAdversarialSourceHarvest`, `xaiAdversarialPipeline`, `aiDrivenBotCorpus`) are pre-existing and environmental (missing `.env.engagement-intelligence` in this worktree) ŌĆö unrelated to this card and outside its scope.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no dependency. GAME-004 adds a visible-UI strip; a human pass of the header (seat pills + room-type glyph + turn label + screen-reader announcement) on Expo web and native is recommended before merge.

## IX-004 ŌĆö Timeline selected-message readout and active-context detail pane (Epic 8 / UI-UX Behavior Repair Wave / argument-room)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö the selected-message detail is now a prominent, persistent instrument panel above the timeline map. Pure UI over already-loaded data; no migration, no Edge Function, no new dependency. Issue #135.

- **Why this card exists:** the selected-message detail (SC-003's `ArgumentReplySidecar`) rendered *below* `ArgumentTimelineMap` inside the timeline branch ŌĆö visually subordinate, frequently off-screen, with no unmistakable confirmation of *which* node was selected or *which* message the action dock would act on. IX-004 elevates the readout into a prominent, persistent panel that sits **above** the timeline map and the action dock, refreshes on every selection change, shares one selection id across Timeline and Cards, follows Prev/Next/Latest/Back-to-root, and degrades gracefully when the selected message disappears.
- **Deliverables (2 new production files + 6 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/arguments/timelineSelectedReadoutModel.ts` ŌĆö pure-TS projection over the SC-003 `SidecarViewModel`. No React, no Supabase, no network, no AI. Exports `ReadoutSelectionStatus` (`explicit` / `entry_hint` / `default_latest` / `stale_fallback`), `TimelineSelectedReadoutViewModel`, `buildTimelineSelectedReadoutViewModel`, the `buildReplyCountLabel` / `buildActingOnShortLabel` helpers, and the frozen `TIMELINE_READOUT_COPY`. It re-derives no standing / lifecycle / metadata ŌĆö those flow through the reused SC-003 view-model. It adds the direct-reply count (immediate children only ŌĆö `parentId === selectedMessageId`, never descendants), the plain-language reply-count label, the `"<kind> ┬Ę #<ordinal>"` dock target label, the verbatim stale-fallback banner, and the panel a11y label + live-region announcement string.
  - `src/features/arguments/TimelineSelectedReadoutPanel.tsx` ŌĆö the prominent, read-only RN panel. Wraps `ArgumentReplySidecar` rather than re-implementing its six sections. No callbacks, no dispatch. Renders the stale banner (when present), the reply-count line, and the wrapped sidecar. Adds **no animation** (reduce-motion unaffected ŌĆö the panel snaps); the unmistakable click feedback is the panel content refresh itself plus VG-004's existing node glow. Selection changes announce via `accessibilityLiveRegion="polite"` (web) / `announceForAccessibility` (native, `Platform`-gated so a web build never double-announces).
  - 6 new test suites ŌĆö `timelineSelectedReadout`, `timelineSelectedReadoutNav`, `timelineSelectionSharedAcrossModes`, `timelineStaleSelection`, `timelineReadoutBanList`, `timelineReadoutNoRoute` (93 tests).
- **Modified files (3):** `ArgumentGameSurface.tsx` ŌĆö added the `selectionStatus` companion state (initialised `entry_hint` when a gallery entry hint is present, else `default_latest`); `activeMessageId` stays the single selection source of truth shared across Timeline and Cards. Every explicit selection mutation (tap, Prev, Next, Latest, Back-to-root, dock open-cards) sets `selectionStatus = 'explicit'`; the existing stale-snap effect sets `stale_fallback` when the active message vanishes. The SC-003 sidecar view-model is now memoized once in the shell and the readout projection is built from it; the prominent `TimelineSelectedReadoutPanel` renders above the map and the subordinate sidecar render below it is removed. `ArgumentTimelineMap.tsx` ŌĆö new optional `actingOnLabel` prop renders an `"Acting on: <kind ┬Ę #ordinal>"` line inside the existing action-dock wrapper (purely additive chrome; the dock model is untouched); `handleStubPress` now also selects the branch root so the readout follows a collapsed-stub tap (BR-001 contract). `__tests__/inRoomNoRoute.test.ts` ŌĆö the `onJumpLatest` / `onJumpToRoot` scan is now window-based; IX-004 expanded those inline arrows into block bodies, so the old single-line regex no longer matched (the intent ŌĆö callbacks call `setActiveMessageId`, no routing ŌĆö is preserved).
- **Doctrine encoded:** the readout renders standing / tone / heat **bands** already produced by `buildSidecarViewModel` in non-verdict language; the panel is read-only and cannot block anything. Reply count is a plain activity count, never cross-derived into the standing band and carrying no verdict word (`timelineReadoutBanList.test.ts` enforces the no-verdict / no-`snake_case` rule). The selection cue is **color-independent** ŌĆö VG-004's 2px glow stroke + 3px halo ring (border weight) + geometry + the panel content refresh. No route transition on selection (`timelineReadoutNoRoute.test.ts` proves it statically and behaviorally). No AI call, no service-role, no migration, no Edge Function, no new dependency.
- **Out of scope (per the approved design):** a separate cluster-level readout; rendering the panel in Stack/Cards mode (the shared-selection requirement is already met because `activeMessageId` persists across the mode toggle); a responsive side-by-side wide layout (the room has no breakpoint infrastructure ŌĆö IX-004 ships the "above the map" placement, which satisfies "prominent and persistent, not below").

## GAME-002 ŌĆö Turn pacing, daily messages, cooldown (Epic 12 / Game Rules / pacing layer)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö mode-level turn pacing model + `PacingChip` mounted in the COMPOSER-002 dock header. Pacing is in-memory only; no migration, no persistence. Issue #118.

- **Why this card exists:** argument modes need a way to make moves feel consequential ŌĆö cooldowns, a daily message cap, response windows ŌĆö without ever becoming an invisible punishment. GAME-002 ships the pacing layer as a pure-TS deterministic model plus a small status chip. The v1 default is **casual** (no pacing at all), so the chip is inert until GAME-003 supplies non-casual mode templates.
- **Deliverables (3 new production files + 3 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/modes/pacingModel.ts` ŌĆö pure TS, no React, no Supabase. Exports `PacingRule` / `PacingMoveRecord` / `PacingEvaluationInput` / `PacingEvaluation` / `PacingBlockReason` / `PacingChipViewModel`; `DEFAULT_CASUAL_PACING_RULE` (the provable no-op baseline); `createPacingRule` (merges over the casual default, clamps negatives, freezes); `isNoPacingRule`; `evaluatePacing` (deterministic core covering every reason path ŌĆö `ok` / `cooldown_active` / `daily_limit_hit` / `response_window_expired` ŌĆö with the documented precedence `daily_limit_hit > response_window_expired > cooldown_active`); `formatCountdown` (`M:SS` / `H:MM:SS`, NaN-guarded); `buildPacingChipViewModel` (render-ready plain-language view model); `describePermanentRecord` (the deferred RULE-004 seam ŌĆö exported + tested, no production caller); and a `__DEV__`-guarded `getDevPacingOverride` / `setDevPacingOverride` pair (dead-code-eliminated from production bundles, never surfaced in any UI).
  - `src/features/modes/PacingChip.tsx` ŌĆö presentational RN component (`View` + `Text`). Non-interactive status display: `accessibilityRole="text"`, `accessibilityLiveRegion="polite"`, full `accessibilityLabel`. Returns `null` for the casual / no-pacing view model. `remainingLabel` and `countdownLabel` render as separate `<Text>` children; a non-color glyph (`ŌÅ│` / `ŌĆó`) carries meaning so the chip is legible in grayscale.
  - `src/features/modes/index.ts` ŌĆö barrel.
- **Modified files (1 production):** `src/features/arguments/ArgumentComposerDock.tsx` ŌĆö two new **optional, defaulted** props (`pacingRule?` defaults to `DEFAULT_CASUAL_PACING_RULE`, `pacingRecentMoves?` defaults to `[]`), so omitting both keeps today's behavior exactly. The chip renders in the existing `headerRow` between the header label and Cancel. A 1-second tick advances `now` **only** while the dock is visible and the chip is in a countdown state; the interval clears on close, unmount, and when the countdown reaches zero (no idle ticking).
- **Doctrine encoded:** pacing is **neither** a score **nor** a validation gate ŌĆö it is a consented, visible room rule. `canSendNow` is **advisory chip-tone metadata only**; the model exposes no posting-gate output and the dock never disables the composer or the Post button (save-draft is always available). `pacingNoHiddenBlock.test.ts` proves this. All chip copy is plain language: no verdict / person tokens, no internal `PacingBlockReason` codes, no threatening / punitive wording (`pacingCopyBanList.test.ts` enforces the ban-list ŌĆö extended with `punish` / `penalty` / `banned` / `blocked` / `locked out`). Pacing never reads room heat, score, or strength band ŌĆö the input shape has no field for them. `weightedByCooldown` is carried as data only; applying weight to point standing is GAME-003 + a point-standing change, out of scope here. No AI call, no service-role, no migration, no Edge Function, no `.env`, no new dependency.
- **Scope notes:** `PreSendReviewSheet` is **not** created (it does not exist; RULE-004 owns it) ŌĆö `describePermanentRecord` ships as the documented deferred seam. GAME-003 mode templates and the non-casual `PacingRule` instances are out of scope; GAME-002 ships only `DEFAULT_CASUAL_PACING_RULE` + `createPacingRule`. The room-setup rule-summary surface (issue scope item 4) is deferred ŌĆö there is no non-casual rule to summarize until GAME-003.

## COMPOSER-002 ŌĆö In-room composer dock for Stack and Timeline (Wave 2 / Composer / argument-room)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö the composer renders as an in-room dock; no normal-user action routes to a full-page "Your Move" screen. Issue #111.

- **Why this card exists:** opening *Start argument / Reply / Challenge / Ask source / Narrow / Concede / Synthesize* unmounted the entire argument room. `App.tsx` rendered `<ArgumentTreeScreen>` only when `!composerOpen` and `<ArgumentComposer>` only when `composerOpen` ŌĆö two mutually-exclusive branches. The user landed on a detached light-themed full-screen "Your Move" form that lost the timeline, the active node, observer/participant context, and scroll position; browser/hardware back stranded them. COMPOSER-002 removes that regression by keeping the room mounted and rendering the composer as an in-room dock.
- **Deliverables (1 new production file + 4 new test suites):**
  - `src/features/arguments/ArgumentComposerDock.tsx` ŌĆö presentational dock shell built from RN primitives only (`Modal`, `Animated`, `Pressable`, `View`, `Text`, `useWindowDimensions`, `AccessibilityInfo`, `Platform`). Bottom sheet on narrow viewports (width < 720), fixed right-side panel on wide ones; `width <= 0` first paint resolves to the side panel (mirrors `resolveHeaderBreakpoint`). Slide-up/in animation with a reduce-motion **opacity-only fade path** (no translate when reduced). Esc (web `keydown`, scoped to `visible`) + hardware-back (`Modal.onRequestClose`) both close the dock with **no route change**. Exports a pure `resolveDockLayoutVariant(width)` breakpoint helper. An inert full-bleed scrim shields background touches so a stray tap cannot lose a half-typed draft.
  - `__tests__/composerDockInRoom.test.ts` / `composerDockPresetWiring.test.ts` / `composerDockNoRoute.test.ts` / `composerDockA11y.test.ts` ŌĆö 77 tests following the repo's component-test discipline (static source-scan + pure-helper invariants).
- **Modified files (2):** `App.tsx` (the room render guard drops the `!composerOpen` term so `ArgumentTreeScreen` stays mounted; the standalone full-page composer branch is deleted; `<ArgumentComposerDock>` is mounted as a sibling inside the room view, `visible={composerOpen}`); `src/features/arguments/ArgumentComposer.tsx` (new `mode?: 'dock' | 'page'` prop, default `'dock'`; the legacy "Your Move" page header survives only behind `mode === 'page' && __DEV__`).
- **State preservation by construction:** `viewMode`, the active node, the entry-hint micro-moment, and scroll position survive a compose-cancel round trip because `ArgumentTreeScreen` (and through it `ArgumentGameSurface`) is never unmounted. No room state was lifted into `MainAppShell` ŌĆö preservation is "do not unmount," not a state-lifting refactor.
- **Doctrine encoded:** the dock relocates the composer; it adds no score, no verdict, no band. The post gate (`canSubmit` ŌåÆ `evaluateArgumentDraft`) and the `submit-argument` path are byte-identical; COMPOSER-001 preset wiring (narrow / confirm / synthesize / EV-002 presets) flows unchanged through `composerPreset` ŌåÆ the dock's `initialPatch`. The dock's only new copy is the handle label + `Cancel`; a ban-list test scans it. No AI call, no service-role, no migration, no Edge Function, no new dependency. The composer dark re-skin is explicitly out of scope (deferred to BRAND-002).

## QOL-026 ŌĆö Fix Admin All Arguments loader (Behavior Repair Wave / QOL ŌĆö admin data layer)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö the Admin ŌåÆ All Arguments loader no longer requests columns that do not exist on `public.arguments`. Issue #137.

- **Why this card exists:** the Admin ŌåÆ All Arguments tab was fully broken ŌĆö it showed "Could not load argument activity" with detail `column arguments.selected_tag_codes does not exist`. The loader at `src/features/admin/adminArgumentsApi.ts` requested **two columns that have never existed** on `public.arguments` in the same `.select()` call: `selected_tag_codes` and `attached_evidence`. PostgREST reports unknown columns one at a time, so fixing only the first would leave the page broken on the second.
- **Fix ŌĆö two columns, two treatments:**
  - `selected_tag_codes` ŌåÆ replaced with a correct PostgREST nested embed `argument_tags(tag_code)`. Tags live in the existing `public.argument_tags` join table (admins already have RLS SELECT). A new exported pure helper `asTagCodes` flattens the embed into `AdminArgumentRow.selectedTagCodes` (`string[] | null`), so the category/qualifier badge derivers now receive real tag data instead of the broken `null`.
  - `attached_evidence` ŌåÆ dropped entirely. There is no evidence table or column to join to. `hasEvidence` and the evidence badge (which had never shown real data) were removed cleanly rather than hardcoded to `false`; a future `EV-*` Evidence card reintroduces an evidence indicator deliberately against a real table.
- **Modified files (3 production + 2 test):** `src/features/admin/adminArgumentsApi.ts` (`.select()` list, `RawArgumentRow`, new `asTagCodes` helper, `.map` result), `src/features/admin/types.ts` (`hasEvidence` removed from `AdminArgumentRow`), `src/features/admin/AdminArgumentsTab.tsx` (evidence badge + unused `evidence` palette entry removed); `__tests__/adminArguments.test.ts` (query-shape contract assertions for both removed columns + the new embed) and new `__tests__/adminArgumentsTagJoin.test.ts` (`asTagCodes` unit tests + type contract).
- **Doctrine:** tags are advisory category/qualifier signals, never truth verdicts; removing the evidence badge removes a signal, adds no verdict. SELECT-only loader on the shared anon RLS-scoped `supabase` client ŌĆö no migration, no Edge Function, no service-role, no AI path. Non-admin access stays blocked by the existing RLS on `arguments` + `argument_tags` and the `AdminScreen` tab gating.
- **+15 tests / +1 suite.** Full suite **4623 tests / 160 suites** (4604 passing). Typecheck + lint clean. The 19 failing tests across 5 xAI/bot-fixture suites (`xaiSeededStancesLive`, `xaiAdversarialProvider`, `xaiAdversarialSourceHarvest`, `xaiAdversarialPipeline`, `aiDrivenBotCorpus`) are pre-existing and environmental (missing `.env.engagement-intelligence` in this environment) ŌĆö unrelated to this card and outside its scope.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure client-code change, no `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration. After merge, the operator should verify in the running app that Admin ŌåÆ All Arguments loads without the `selected_tag_codes` / `attached_evidence` errors and that rows + category/qualifier badges render.

## META-1A ŌĆö Persisted manual-tag ledger (Release 6.8 / Epic Rules UX / Metadata)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö `point_tags` table migration, `apply-manual-tag` Edge Function, Deno eligibility mirror, client wrapper, and room-shell loader extension all delivered and green. Migration written-not-applied; Edge Function written-not-deployed (operator runs both post-merge). Issue #76.

- **Why this card exists:** META-001 shipped the manual-tag vocabulary + eligibility matrix but only as an *in-memory* ledger ŌĆö a tag a participant applied lived in React state, vanished on reload, and was invisible to everyone else. META-1A elevates the manual-tag ledger to a persisted, shared gameplay artifact.
- **Deliverables (8 new files):**
  - `supabase/migrations/20260517000009_meta_1a_point_tags.sql` ŌĆö the `point_tags` table (9 columns incl. `removed_at` soft-delete + `removed_by`; `tag_code` `CHECK IN` listing the 10 META-001 `ManualTagCode` values verbatim; FKs to `debates` / `arguments` / `public.profiles`), two partial indexes on active rows, a partial unique index `point_tags_one_active_per_tagger`, RLS enabled, and exactly 3 named policies (`pt_insert_eligible`, `pt_select_read_access`, `pt_update_soft_delete`) ŌĆö **no `for delete` policy** (soft-delete only).
  - `supabase/functions/apply-manual-tag/index.ts` ŌĆö the single write path. Two actions (`apply` / `remove`), CORS / JWT verify, caller-scoped client for the argument lookup + insert/update, server-side eligibility enforcement, service-role client used **only** for a best-effort `admin_audit_events` row. A duplicate apply (`23505`) is idempotent; `remove` soft-deletes via `removed_at` (admins may remove others' tags).
  - `supabase/functions/_shared/pointTagEligibility.ts` ŌĆö the Deno-side mirror of META-001's `MANUAL_TAG_ELIGIBILITY_TABLE` + `isApplyAllowed` (Edge Functions cannot import from `src/`); guarded against drift by `pointTagsEligibilityMirror.test.ts`.
  - `src/features/metadata/pointTagsApi.ts` ŌĆö client wrappers `applyManualTag` / `removeManualTag` (route through `supabase.functions.invoke`), the `PersistedPointTag` interface, and the pure `persistedTagsToManualTagEntries` adapter.
  - 4 new test suites (`pointTagsMigration`, `applyManualTagEdgeFunction`, `pointTagsApi`, `pointTagsEligibilityMirror`) ŌĆö 64 tests, including the 80-case eligibility matrix executed directly against the mirror's `isApplyAllowed`.
- **Modified files (6):** `argumentsApi.ts` (`fetchArgumentRelations` now reads active `point_tags`), `arguments/types.ts` (`pointTags` on `ArgumentRelations`), `useArgumentRoomMessages.ts` (`pointTagsByArgumentId` map), `ArgumentGameSurface.tsx` (replaced the empty `manualTagsByMessageId` placeholder with the hydrated map; exposes the write-path wrappers), `ArgumentTreeScreen.tsx` (threads the prop), plus `composerHandoff.ts` / `useArgumentViewport.ts` / `argumentCache.test.ts` updated for the additive `pointTags` field on `ArgumentRelations`.

META-1A wires the persisted-tag **read path** (the room shell hydrates persisted tags) and exposes `applyManualTag` / `removeManualTag` so a thin follow-up card can wire the apply trigger. The card's "UI reflects persisted state" criterion is met by the read path.
- **Doctrine encoded:** a manual tag is a participant gameplay annotation, never a verdict ŌĆö the `point_tags` table has no count / score / engagement column; the doctrine ban-list test scans the migration, the function, and the mirror. The Edge Function is the only write path (the room-shell `select` is the documented read exception); soft-delete only ŌĆö no `.delete()` on `point_tags` anywhere, no `for delete` RLS policy. No AI call, no service-role in client code, no new dependency.
