## IX-003 ŌĆö Keyboard and accessibility navigation (Release 6.7 / Epic 8 Interaction)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö pure-TS keyboard-traversal model, web `onKeyDown` wiring on the argument timeline, screen-reader label upgrade, and tests all delivered and green. Issue #22.

- **Why this card exists:** the horizontal argument timeline (`ArgumentTimelineMap.tsx`) was operable only by touch, and its node screen-reader label was missing two of the four signals the card requires ŌĆö strength and branch. IX-003 makes the timeline fully keyboard-operable on web and completes the per-node accessibility contract, with no change to the native touch path.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/arguments/keyboardNavigationModel.ts` ŌĆö new pure-TS model (no React / Supabase / network / AI). `resolveTimelineNavEffect` is the traversal resolver: Arrow L/R walk the chronological prev/next node (no wrap at the ends), Home/End jump to root/latest, Enter/Space resolve to `open_detail` for the active node, Escape resolves to `close_overlay` only when an overlay is open; with no active node Left/Home go to root and Right/End go to latest. `buildNodeAccessibilityLabel` is the single source of truth for the plain-language node label ŌĆö it now exposes type, side, ordinal, **strength** (`STANDING_BAND_SOFT_LABEL`, plain-language gameplay standing ŌĆö never a verdict) and **branch** (`deriveBranchLabel`: mainline / side branch / detached). The model inlines the chronological prev/next index logic so its dependency on `argumentGameSurfaceModel` stays type-only ŌĆö no runtime import cycle.
  - `__tests__/keyboardNavigationModel.test.ts` (60 tests) ŌĆö pure-model coverage: arrow traversal, Home/End, cold-start (null active), Enter/Space, Escape, unhandled keys, empty/single-node/detached edge cases, no-mutation guard, `isTimelineNavKey`, `deriveBranchLabel`, and `buildNodeAccessibilityLabel` including a per-band strength assertion (all 9 bands) and a verdict-token ban-list test.
  - `__tests__/ix003KeyboardA11yWiring.test.ts` (13 tests) ŌĆö source scan: `ArgumentTimelineMap` wires the model in (`onKeyDown`, `Platform.OS === 'web'` guard, `preventDefault`, Prev/Next `accessibilityState` disabled, `tabIndex`), keeps the node `accessibilityRole="button"` + `selected` contract, adds no new dependency, and `keyboardNavigationModel` stays React-free with a type-only dependency on `argumentGameSurfaceModel`.
- **Modified files (2):** `src/features/arguments/ArgumentTimelineMap.tsx` (web-only `onKeyDown` + `tabIndex=0` on the timeline group `<View>`; `tabIndex=-1` on node Pressables so the Tab sequence is one stop; Prev/Next gain a disabled `accessibilityState` + dimmed style at the ends; `NodeDot` builds its label via the shared helper); `src/features/arguments/argumentGameSurfaceModel.ts` (Pass 4 now calls the same `buildNodeAccessibilityLabel` helper so the model's stored label and the rendered label never drift).
- **Scope:** keyboard nav drives the SAME `onActivate` / `handleInfoTap` callbacks tap already uses ŌĆö no parallel selection path. All key handling is `Platform.OS === 'web'`-guarded; native is untouched (tap + VoiceOver/TalkBack rotor). Up/Down arrow keys are explicitly out of scope (deferred ŌĆö risks colliding with page scroll). No new npm dependency ŌĆö web key capture uses RN-web's existing `onKeyDown` / `tabIndex` props, spread via a `Platform.OS === 'web' ? {...} : {}` object (no `as` cast).
- **Doctrine encoded:** the screen-reader "strength" exposure is plain-language gameplay standing (`STANDING_BAND_SOFT_LABEL`), never a verdict ŌĆö a ban-list test locks it. Keyboard nav only changes *selection*; it cannot post, score, flag, or block. No Supabase, no migration, no Edge Function, no AI path, no service-role.
- **One existing test updated:** `__tests__/argumentTimelineMapRootOnboarding.test.ts` ŌĆö the node label format changed (`position N of M` replaces `Message N of M`, plus strength / branch / "opening claim"), so the one assertion against the old string was updated to the new format. This is a design-anticipated label change, not a regression. No other existing test changed.
- **+73 tests / +2 suites.** Full suite passes **4544 tests / 155 suites** (4471 / 153 pre-card baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no dependency.
- **Browser verification:** IX-003 is a visible-UI card; the design's ┬¦"Browser verification checklist" (14 items ŌĆö Expo web + keyboard + screen reader) is a human pass to walk before merge.

## PR-002 ŌĆö Profile tag popout (Release 6.7 / Epic 9 Profile)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö closed-vocabulary profile-tag feature, ProfileTagPopout Modal, preferences-popout entry row, App wiring, and tests all delivered and green. Issue #24.

- **Why this card exists:** a signed-in user had no way to add lightweight identity-light profile tags (interests, debate style, availability, accessibility self-description). PR-002 ships an optional, doctrine-safe tag picker reached from a new row inside PR-001's "My preferences" popout.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/profileTags/` ŌĆö new feature module, 8 files: `profileTagModel.ts` (pure TS ŌĆö the versioned `ProfileTagSelection` blob, `schemaVersion: 1`, `MAX_PROFILE_TAGS = 5`, defensive `mergeTagSelectionWithDefaults`, immutable `toggleTag` / `canAddTag` / `isTagSelected` / `getTagsByCategory` / `resolveTagLabel` / `selectedTagDefinitions`); `profileTagVocabulary.ts` (the frozen, closed, curated 28-tag vocabulary across 4 categories ŌĆö 10 topic interests, 8 debate styles, 5 availability, 5 accessibility self-description); `profileTagsStorage.ts` (AsyncStorage glue ŌĆö best-effort load/save, never throws, runs every load through `mergeTagSelectionWithDefaults`); `useProfileTags.ts` (hook ŌĆö loads the blob, optimistic `toggleTag` / `clearTags`); `profileTagCopy.ts` (all user-facing strings); `ProfileTagChip.tsx` (multi-select chip ŌĆö `accessibilityRole="checkbox"`, check glyph + filled style, Ōēź44 hit target); `ProfileTagPopout.tsx` (core `Modal` bottom-sheet reusing the `PreferencesPopout` / `DeletionRequestSheet` pattern); `index.ts` barrel.
  - The vocabulary is **closed by doctrine design** ŌĆö there is no free-text tag entry and no "custom / other" escape hatch anywhere; users select only from the fixed 28-tag set. This is the mechanism that makes the card's DISALLOWED list (protected-class / party-affiliation / unverified-"expert" / hostile-label / ideology-personality-scoring tokens) exhaustively test-enforceable.
- **Persistence:** device-local AsyncStorage, one versioned JSON blob keyed `cdiscourse:profile-tags:<userId>` ŌĆö a SEPARATE blob from PR-001's preferences blob (different shape, different defensive-parse need). No migration, no Supabase column, no Edge Function, no service-role, no AI path.
- **`MAX_PROFILE_TAGS = 5` enforced in three places:** on read (`mergeTagSelectionWithDefaults` truncates an over-cap stored blob), in the model (`toggleTag` is a no-op when adding past the cap), and in the UI (unselected chips disable at the cap). Tags are optional ŌĆö 0 is valid, there is no floor.
- **v1 visibility:** tags are device-local and **self-visible only** ŌĆö they appear in the user's own popout. There is no other-user profile surface in the app; shared/other-user visibility is an explicit v2 follow-up (a Supabase column + RLS + an other-user profile screen). The `schemaVersion` field keeps that migration path open.
- **Doctrine encoded ŌĆö proven by tests:** profile tags never affect truth / score / heat / point standing and never change validation gates. `profileTagValidationImmutability.test.ts` runs the real Constitution engine (`validateTransition` / `validateDepth` / `validateBodyLength` / `runDeterministicChecks`), `argumentScoreModel.computeStatementStanding`, and `antiAmplification.applyAntiAmplification` twice ŌĆö once with no tag state and once after a full 5-tag selection is persisted to AsyncStorage ŌĆö and asserts byte-identical (`JSON.stringify`) output; it also source-scans both directions of import isolation (no gate module imports `profileTags`; no `profileTags` file imports a gate/score/validation module). `profileTagVocabularySafety.test.ts` exhaustively scans every id and label in the 28-tag vocabulary for protected-class / party / "expert" / hostile-label / verdict tokens and confirms no `TextInput` exists in the popout or chip. `profileTagDoctrine.test.ts` covers the copy verdict ban-list, internal-code leak, role-escalation surface, secrets, and accessibility scans.
- **Modified files (3):** `src/features/session/sessionKeys.ts` (new `profileTagsKey` builder, mirrors `userPreferencesKey`); `src/features/preferences/PreferencesPopout.tsx` (one new "Profile tags" `Pressable` row ŌĆö `pref-field-profile-tags` / `pref-profile-tags-open` ŌĆö plus `onOpenProfileTags` + `profileTagCount` props; still exactly one `TextInput`, so PR-001's `preferencesDoctrine.test.ts` stays green); `App.tsx` (mounts `useProfileTags` + `<ProfileTagPopout>` as a second core `Modal` in the signed-in shell).
- **+87 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite passes **4471 tests / 153 suites** (4384 / 149 pre-card baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean. No existing test required a change ŌĆö PR-002 is purely additive plus two back-compatible props on `PreferencesPopout`.
- **No operator step** ŌĆö pure code change. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration, no new dependency (the React Native AsyncStorage package was already in `package.json` via PR-001).
- **Browser verification:** PR-002 is a visible-UI card; the design's ┬¦"Browser verification checklist" (15 items) is a human Expo-web pass to walk before merge.

## AN-003 ŌĆö Tree playability diagnostics (Release 6.7 / Epic 13 Analytics)

**Status:** Complete ŌĆö pure model, test suite, and the ┬¦5 dev-script snapshot generator all delivered and green. Issue #66.

- **Why this card exists:** GAME-001 shipped exhaustion / moved-on advisories with v1 threshold constants. AN-003 produces a deterministic, verdict-free `TreePlayabilityDiagnostics` record so an operator can look at real rooms and see whether those thresholds are firing sensibly ŌĆö is the lifecycle-mapped tree playable, where is it stuck, and what advisory state dominates.
- **Deliverables (this card):**
  - `src/features/analytics/treePlayabilityDiagnostics.ts` ŌĆö new pure-TS deriver (no React / Supabase / network / AI / clock). `computeTreePlayabilityDiagnostics`, `TreePlayabilityClass` (`empty` / `healthy` / `unresolved_dominant` / `stalled` / `mixed`), `TreePlayabilityDiagnostics` + input/config types, `DEFAULT_TREE_PLAYABILITY_CONFIG`, `renderTreePlayabilityMarkdown` (pure string builder, no file I/O), `_forbiddenTreePlayabilityTokens`, and an `_internal` namespace for test access. Consumes the already-built `PointLifecycleMap`, `ArgumentTimelineMapModel`, GAME-001 advisories, EV-001 contracts, and SC-004 dock models ŌĆö never re-derives any of them. Does NOT import AN-001's `boardDiagnostics.ts` (non-duplication is a card acceptance criterion).
  - `__tests__/treePlayabilityDiagnostics.test.ts` ŌĆö new pure-model suite, 29 tests: empty/deterministic/total counts, unresolved + exhausted/stale derivation, `branch_recommended` excluded from both sets, branch overload + max/median depth, active-unresolved-point reachability, evidence-debt concentration (with and without an EV-001 contract), the no-actionable-suggestion dock scan + detached-node exclusion, dominant-advisory GAME-001 + lifecycle-fallback paths, playability classification, fraction guards, the verdict-token ban list, the no-duplication structural assertion against AN-001, and purity. Fixtures are inline consts including a 55-node / 36-cluster deep tree.
- **R1 (`node.depth` semantics) resolved:** `buildArgumentTimelineMap` sets `depth = 0` for roots and `parent.depth + 1` for replies ŌĆö depth is ABSOLUTE from the timeline root, so cluster-relative depth = `node.depth - clusterRoot.depth` (the design's assumption). Pinned by test #8.
- **D7 adapted metric implemented:** SC-004's dock always keeps `open_cards_detail` enabled so a literally-empty dock is unreachable; AN-003 counts non-root, non-detached nodes whose dock has no enabled POST-producing action instead. D5 honored ŌĆö the breakdown iterates the exported `ALL_POINT_LIFECYCLE_STATES` (19 entries).
- **Doctrine encoded:** no verdict tokens in any produced string; no popularity / engagement / heat / standing input anywhere; pure model, no Supabase / migration / Edge Function / service-role / AI path; AN-001's `boardDiagnostics.ts` untouched and never imported.
- **┬¦5 dev-script delivered (mechanism: `tsc` precompile, no new dependency):** the revised ┬¦5 of `docs/designs/AN-003.md` is now implemented. `scripts/diagnostics/buildTreePlayabilitySnapshot.ts` (authored in TypeScript) builds the four consumed models from a room fixture via the shipped builders (`buildArgumentTimelineMap`, `buildPointLifecycleMap`, `buildExhaustionTimeoutInputFromLifecycle` + `deriveExhaustionTimeoutAdvisory`, `getTimelineEvidenceContract`, `buildMoveMetadataLedger`, `buildTimelineNodeActionDockModel`), then calls AN-003's `computeTreePlayabilityDiagnostics` + `renderTreePlayabilityMarkdown` ŌĆö it re-derives nothing. A standalone `tsconfig.diagnostics.json` (CommonJS-targeted; does NOT extend the Expo-based root tsconfig, which carries an incompatible `customConditions`) compiles the script + its verified React-Native-free closure to the gitignored `artifacts/diagnostics/tree-playability-build/` dir; a bare `node` run then emits the snapshot to the gitignored `artifacts/diagnostics/tree-playability/` tree. Four npm scripts added (`diagnostics:tree-playability:build` / `:dry` / `:fixture` / base). `eslint.config.js` `ignores` gained `artifacts/**` so the generated emit dir is never linted. No new dependency ŌĆö `typescript` was already a devDependency. `npm run typecheck` (root tsconfig), `npm run lint`, and `npm run test` are untouched by the diagnostics tsconfig.
- **+29 tests / +1 suite** (delivered earlier; ┬¦5 is non-test, purely additive). Full suite passes **4287 tests / 146 suites**. Typecheck + lint clean. No existing test required a change ŌĆö AN-003 is purely additive.
- **No operator step** for the merged code. Optional QA convenience: `npm run diagnostics:tree-playability:dry` prints a snapshot to stdout; `npm run diagnostics:tree-playability -- --fixture <room.json>` writes one to the gitignored `artifacts/` tree.

## VG-004 ŌĆö High-tech board visual polish without new dependencies (Release 6.6 / Epic 2 Visual Grammar)

**Status:** Complete (pure client UI ŌĆö no operator step). Issue #113.

- **Why this card exists:** the horizontal argument board (`ArgumentTimelineMap`) read as a flat form. VG-004 adds six render-only refinements so it reads as a playable map: a node-level active-path glow, a selected-node halo, an evidence "receipt" inner mark, a branch-stub glyph refinement, a tone tint on active-path nodes, and density-aware inter-node spacing.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/arguments/timelineNodeVisualModel.ts` ŌĆö new pure-TS model (no React / Supabase / network). `TimelineDensityMode`, `TIMELINE_NODE_GAP_BY_DENSITY`, `resolveNodeGapPx`, `deriveTimelineNodeVisualStyle`, `NodeGlowTier`, `TimelineNodeVisualStyle`.
  - `src/features/arguments/ArgumentTimelineMap.tsx` ŌĆö `NodeDot` gains the active-path glow, selected-node halo, evidence receipt mark, and tone-tint `<View>` layers, all derived via the pure helper. New reduce-motion state reads `AccessibilityInfo.isReduceMotionEnabled()` with a `reduceMotionChanged` subscription and the existing try/catch discipline. New `StyleSheet` entries `nodeGlow` / `nodeHalo` / `nodeToneTint` / `receiptMark` / `receiptMarkInner`.
  - `src/features/arguments/BranchCollapseStub.tsx` ŌĆö new pure helper `buildBranchCollapseStubLabelParts`; the stub now renders a decorative branch-kind glyph + the count as two `<Text>` spans (glyph hidden from screen readers).
  - `src/lib/designTokens.ts` ŌĆö extended (not replaced) with `GLOW` (active-path indigo + selected cream halo) and `RECEIPT_MARK` (reuses the `ARGUMENT.evidence` family). `TOKENS` aggregate gains `glow` + `receiptMark`.
  - `src/features/arguments/argumentGameSurfaceModel.ts` ŌĆö `BuildTimelineMapInput` gains optional `density?: TimelineDensityMode`; `xStep` now calls `resolveNodeGapPx(input.density)`.
  - `src/features/arguments/ArgumentGameSurface.tsx` ŌĆö passes `density: 'normal'` explicitly.
  - `__tests__/argumentNodeVisualVG004.test.ts` ŌĆö new pure / style-rule suite (47 tests) covering `resolveNodeGapPx`, glow / halo / receipt / tone-tint derivation, doctrine strength-independence, the `accessibilityFragment` ban-list, `buildBranchCollapseStubLabelParts`, token assertions, source-scan invariants, the VG-001 contract, and density-preserves-active-node.
- **Operator Q1 ŌĆö answered (option b):** the default board density was deliberately loosened. `TIMELINE_NODE_GAP_BY_DENSITY = { compact: 28, normal: 44, expanded: 64 }`; `resolveNodeGapPx(undefined) === 44`. The exported `TIMELINE_NODE_GAP` constant was changed `28 ŌåÆ 44` to stay consistent with the new `'normal'` default (it had exactly one consumer ŌĆö line 1206 of the same file ŌĆö which now calls `resolveNodeGapPx`).
- **Doctrine encoded:** the glow + halo are strength-independent ŌĆö they read only navigation / selection state, never `standingBand` / `heat` / any score. The tone tint is the only field reading `toneBand` / `temperatureBand`; it is applied to active-path nodes only and capped at alpha Ōēż 0.18. Every new state has a non-color signal (geometry / stroke / text) and a plain-English `accessibilityFragment` with zero verdict / amplification / snake_case tokens. No new color token (reuses existing hex). No `react-native-svg`, no new npm dependency. No Supabase / migration / Edge Function / AI path. VoiceOver / TalkBack verification of the new announcements is a deferred follow-up per `accessibility-targets`.
- **+47 tests / +1 suite.** Full suite passes **4258 tests / 145 suites** (4211 / 144 pre-card baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean. One existing test updated: `__tests__/designTokens.test.ts` ŌĆö the `TOKENS` aggregate key-set assertion now expects the two new VG-004 categories (`glow`, `receiptMark`). No timeline x-coordinate test required a change: `argumentTimelineMap.test.ts` asserts node `x` only with relative comparisons (`toBeLessThan` / `toBeGreaterThan` / two-map equality), never hardcoded literals, so the 28ŌåÆ44 default gap change did not break any assertion.
- **No operator step:** pure client UI. No `db push`, no `functions deploy`, no env var, no migration.

## QOL-024 ŌĆö Admin user invite/create workflow (Release 6.5 / admin tooling)

**Status:** Complete (code-only ŌĆö Edge Function deploy is an operator step). Issue #110.

- **Why this card exists:** the admin Create-user form could only mint an already-confirmed user with a password ŌĆö there was no path that emails a new human tester a self-serve first-sign-in link, forcing the operator to hand-issue credentials out-of-band.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `supabase/functions/admin-users/index.ts` ŌĆö new `handleInviteUser` handler + `case 'invite_user'` in the switch. Uses `inviteUserByEmail` (not generate-link) so the invite link/token never enters function memory or the response; the response is `{ ok, invited, notification }` only ŌĆö no link, token, email, or userId.
  - `supabase/functions/_shared/adminSchemas.ts` ŌĆö new `InviteUser` zod object in the `AdminUsersRequestSchema` discriminated union. `role` is `z.enum(['user','moderator'])` ŌĆö `'admin'` is rejected (an invite can never mint an admin).
  - `supabase/functions/_shared/adminAudit.ts` ŌĆö `'invite_user'` appended to `WHITELISTED_ACTIONS`.
  - `supabase/functions/_shared/adminInvitePayload.ts` ŌĆö new pure, Deno-import-free builders `buildInviteAuditPayload` / `buildInviteResponse`. The audit payload stores `emailDomain` (domain only, never the raw email) and `redirectToProvided` (boolean, never the URL).
  - `src/lib/edgeFunctions.ts` ŌĆö `'invite_user'` added to the client `AdminUsersAction` union.
  - `src/features/admin/adminApi.ts` ŌĆö new `adminInviteUser` wrapper. Derives the invite callback URL via `buildAuthRedirectUrl({ kind: 'invite' })` with the same fail-soft try/catch as `adminSendPasswordReset`; passes an explicit field list (no `...input` spread).
  - `src/features/admin/adminHelpers.ts` ŌĆö `adminErrorMessage` maps the `invite_email_not_configured` code to plain operator-directed copy; new pure UI helpers `isInvitingHuman` / `isModeToggleVisible` / `isPasswordFieldVisible` / `resolveCreateUserDispatch`.
  - `src/features/admin/AdminCreateUserForm.tsx` ŌĆö new Invite/Password mode toggle for the human branch (invite is the default); invite mode hides the password field and shows an "Invite sent." status line. The Human/Bot toggle and the entire Bot branch are untouched.
  - 3 new test suites: `adminInviteUserClient.test.ts` (12), `adminInviteUserAuditShape.test.ts` (14), `AdminCreateUserForm.test.tsx` (22); `adminSchemas.test.ts` extended with the `InviteUser` mirror (+4).
- **Doctrine encoded:** an invite can only create `user` / `moderator` ŌĆö `admin` is a 422 at schema validation. No service-role in client code (the invite call runs on the service client built inside the Edge Function, after the admin check). No invite link / token / raw email / userId in the response or any log. Audit row stores `emailDomain` + `redirectToProvided` only. Plain-language copy ŌĆö the user never sees `invite_user` / `invite_email_not_configured`. Fail-soft ŌĆö a bad redirect origin degrades to no `redirectTo`, never blocks the invite.
- **No migration:** verified `admin_audit_events.action` is a `text` column (not a Postgres enum), so the new audit action needed only a JS-array edit. No xAI / Anthropic / X API calls; no Supabase write by Claude; no real email sent; no new dependency.
- **+52 tests / +3 suites.** Full suite passes **4211 tests / 144 suites** (4159 / 141 pre-card baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean. No existing tests required changes.
- **Operator follow-up (post-merge):** the feature is effective only after the operator runs `npx supabase functions deploy admin-users --linked` and enables the Supabase "Invite user" email template + the `/auth/callback` redirect allow-list entry. See `docs/admin-email-validation-plan.md` ┬¦ "QOL-024 ŌĆö admin user invite-by-email runbook". No `db push`.

## QOL-023 ŌĆö Supabase auth redirect helper (Release 6.5 / deployment hardening)

**Status:** Complete. Auth emails sent by Supabase (signup confirmation, magic link, password reset, admin-triggered reset) now carry an `emailRedirectTo` / `redirectTo` pointing at the deployed origin instead of the dashboard `localhost` Site URL. Issue #109.

- **Why this card exists:** `signUpWithEmailPassword` never passed `emailRedirectTo`, so a user invited to the deployed dev app received a link pointing at `http://localhost:8081` and bounced ŌĆö onboarding was broken in the deployed environment.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/lib/auth/buildAuthRedirectUrl.ts` ŌĆö new pure-TS helper (no React / Supabase / network imports). `buildAuthRedirectUrl(input)` deterministically computes the redirect URL from a runtime origin + `isDev` flag. Origin-resolution fallback (runtime origin ŌåÆ hosted fallback `https://dev.cdiscourse.com` in non-dev ŌåÆ `http://localhost:8081` only in a true dev build). Scheme/host validation (rejects `file:`/`javascript:`/`data:`/`vbscript:`/`blob:` in every build; rejects `http://` in non-dev; rejects hostless origins). Normalization (trim, strip trailing slashes, lowercase scheme + host, preserve port, discard path). Exports `AuthRedirectKind`, `DEFAULT_AUTH_ROUTES`, `DEV_FALLBACK_ORIGIN`, `HOSTED_FALLBACK_ORIGIN`, `InvalidAuthRedirectOrigin` (error carries only a `reason` enum, never the offending origin string).
  - `src/lib/auth/resolveRuntimeOrigin.ts` ŌĆö new impure boundary. `resolveRuntimeOrigin()` reads `window.location.origin` ŌåÆ `__CDISCOURSE_RUNTIME_ENV__.EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN` ŌåÆ `process.env.EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN`. `getIsDev()` fail-closes to `false` when `__DEV__` is undefined.
  - `src/features/auth/authApi.ts` ŌĆö `signUpWithEmailPassword` passes `options.emailRedirectTo`; new exported `sendPasswordResetEmail(email)` wrapper; `mapAuthError` gains a `redirect_invalid` branch; private `safeBuildRedirect` catches `InvalidAuthRedirectOrigin` and degrades to `null` (Supabase falls back to the dashboard Site URL ŌĆö a bad origin never blocks signup). Exports `REDIRECT_INVALID_MESSAGE` plain-language copy.
  - `src/features/auth/types.ts` ŌĆö `'redirect_invalid'` added to the `AuthError` union.
  - `src/features/admin/adminApi.ts` ŌĆö `adminSendPasswordReset` derives a default `redirectTo` from `buildAuthRedirectUrl` when the caller omits it (signature unchanged; the `admin-users` Edge Function already forwards `redirectTo` ŌĆö no Edge Function change).
  - `src/lib/supabase.ts` ŌĆö `CDiscourseRuntimeEnv` + `readRuntimeEnv()` gain the optional `EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN` field.
  - `scripts/build/inject-runtime-env.{mjs,ps1,sh}` + `scripts/runtime/server.mjs` ŌĆö extend the HOST-001b runtime-env injector with an optional `--app-origin` / `-AppOrigin` flag + `EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN` env read; new `looksLikeHttpOrigin` validator (exit 10 on garbage); the `looksForbidden` secret-shape check covers the new value; absence is NOT a build failure (the helper fallback covers it).
  - `.env.example` ŌĆö adds the `EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN=` key name (empty placeholder; a public URL, not a secret).
  - `docs/admin-email-validation-plan.md` ŌĆö appends the QOL-023 redirect-URL operator runbook to the Supabase / Auth settings checklist.
  - 4 new test suites: `__tests__/buildAuthRedirectUrl.test.ts`, `__tests__/authApiRedirect.test.ts`, `__tests__/noLocalhostInProdAuthPaths.test.ts` (static scan with a vacuous-pass guard), `__tests__/buildAuthRedirectUrl.doctrine.test.ts`.
- **Doctrine encoded:** Fail-soft ŌĆö a bad runtime origin degrades (`emailRedirectTo` omitted), never blocks signup. The redirect origin is a PUBLIC URL, never read from `.env*` at runtime. `InvalidAuthRedirectOrigin` carries only the reason enum (no origin leak into logs). Plain-language copy (`redirect_invalid` ŌåÆ "We couldn't open that linkŌĆ”") with no internal code. No service-role anywhere in client code. `buildAuthRedirectUrl.ts` imports nothing.
- **No xAI, Anthropic, or X API calls; no Supabase writes; no service-role; no migration; no Edge Function change; no new dependency. The `admin-users` Edge Function was read-only confirmed (it already forwards `redirectTo`).**
- **+54 tests / +4 suites.** Full suite passes 4159 tests / 141 suites with zero failures (4105 / 137 main baseline + this card). Typecheck + lint clean. (The xAI / engagement-intelligence suites are gated on the gitignored operator file `.env.engagement-intelligence`; they pass in a working tree that has it and fail only in a fresh worktree that does not ŌĆö this card does not touch those scripts.) One existing test updated: `__tests__/hostOneBuildScripts.test.ts` ŌĆö the runtime-env shim source-scan assertion was updated to match the refactored `buildRuntimeEnvFileContents` (now assembles an `env` object then `JSON.stringify(env)` so the optional `EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN` key is included only when present). The JSON-encode safety property still holds.
- **Operator follow-up (post-merge):** the feature is end-to-end effective only after the operator (1) sets Supabase Dashboard Auth ŌåÆ URL Configuration Site URL = `https://dev.cdiscourse.com` and adds `ŌĆ”/auth/callback` + `ŌĆ”/auth/reset` to Additional Redirect URLs, and (2) sets the Cloud Run `EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_ORIGIN` secret. See `docs/admin-email-validation-plan.md` ┬¦ "QOL-023 ŌĆö auth redirect URL configuration". No `db push`, no `functions deploy`.

The LIFE-001 review flagged the alias as removable "right after GAME-001" to avoid two-name confusion in downstream consumers (SC-004 / ST-002 / GAME-001). GAME-001 has landed using only the canonical name, so the alias has zero callers in `src/` or `__tests__/` and can be removed safely.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**

- **Doctrine encoded:** None ŌĆö pure naming hygiene. The canonical `hasAdditiveAxisInformation` semantics are untouched. GAME-001's `exhaustionTimeoutModel.ts` was already using `hasAdditiveAxisInformation`, not the alias, so it is unaffected.
- **Boundary enforcement:** No semantic change. No new helper, no helper signature change, no doctrine surface change. `grep -r moveAddsAxisInformation src/ __tests__/` returns zero matches after the edit.
- **No xAI, Anthropic, or X API calls; no Supabase writes; no service-role; no migration; no Edge Function change; no new dependency; no `.env*` touched; no hosting file touched; no test file modified (no alias-equivalence test existed); the constitution engine remains sacred.**

## GAME-001 ŌĆö Point exhaustion + timeout rules (Release 6.6 / Wave 3)

**Status:** Pure-TS sibling deriver landed alongside LIFE-001. New module `src/features/lifecycle/exhaustionTimeoutModel.ts` exports `deriveExhaustionTimeoutAdvisory(input): ExhaustionTimeoutAdvisory` ŌĆö a fixture-friendly single-purpose advisory deriver for the seven exhaustion / timeout / synthesis advisory states. Issue #64.

- **Why this card exists:** LIFE-001's `composeClusterState` already fires the exhaustion / moved-on / ignored / synthesis-ready states inside its 1.2 KLOC cascade, but it does not accept a flat cluster-level input object, does not accept override thresholds, and pins `synthesis_ready` to the stricter "explicit synthesis-shape move" semantics. AN-003's "sweep thresholds at low cost" diagnostic mode, and SC-003 / ST-002 follow-ups that want the broader "concession + no debt ŌåÆ synthesis_ready" reading, need a standalone deriver ŌĆö building this on top of LIFE-001 would bloat a file that is already past 1.2 KLOC and blur the canonical-state vs advisory-deriver contracts.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/lifecycle/exhaustionTimeoutModel.ts` ŌĆö new pure-TS module. `ExhaustionTimeoutAdvisoryState` 7-value union (`synthesis_ready` / `exhausted` / `ignored_by_both` / `ignored_by_affirmative` / `ignored_by_negative` / `moved_on_by_affirmative` / `moved_on_by_negative`). `ExhaustionTimeoutInput` flat 14-field input shape (cluster-level signals + override config + optional upstream state). `ExhaustionTimeoutConfig` with `minClusterAgeForTimeoutAdvisory` floor (default 2) ON TOP OF the four LIFE-001-shared thresholds. `ExhaustionTimeoutAdvisory` output with compile-time-pinned `blocksSubmit: false` + `appliesPointStandingPenalty: false` literal-type fields. `DEFAULT_EXHAUSTION_TIMEOUT_CONFIG` frozen defaults (mirror LIFE-001 for the four shared values). `ALL_EXHAUSTION_TIMEOUT_ADVISORY_STATES` frozen array (iteration order = priority cascade). `deriveExhaustionTimeoutAdvisory` pure / total / deterministic function. `buildExhaustionTimeoutInputFromLifecycle` convenience adapter that pulls the six cluster-level signals from a `PointLifecycleClusterSummary` + members + side-turn sequence + artifact-status map. `_forbiddenExhaustionTimeoutTokens` test-only export (LIFE-001 ban list + GAME-001 amplification / penalty / person-attribution extras).
  - `src/features/lifecycle/index.ts` ŌĆö barrel re-exports for every GAME-001 public surface.
  - `__tests__/exhaustionTimeoutModel.test.ts` ŌĆö 103 new tests. 5 fixture suites (exhaustion / one-party ignored / two-party ignored / synthesis-ready / moved-on) with threshold-boundary coverage. No-blocking + no-penalty doctrine pin across every state. Copy ban-list scan (verdict / popularity / amplification / person-attribution tokens forbidden). Person-attribution scan ("the user" / "they ignored" / "Affirmative ignored" forbidden in helper lines). Priority cascade verified by stripping prereqs. N / M / K / J threshold boundaries (N-1 / N / N+1 for each). `minClusterAgeForTimeoutAdvisory` floor pin (defeats the "cluster posted turn 4, by turn 5 no reply ŌåÆ moved_on_by_negative" false-positive). Override-threshold coverage + defaults-parity with LIFE-001. Adapter field-by-field coverage, idempotency, no-mutation, round-trip with the deriver. Purity / determinism / source-scan (no React / Supabase / Anthropic / xAI / fetch / Date / Math.random / process.env / console / engine import).
- **Resolved design questions (designer-confirmed):**
  1. Sibling deriver in a NEW module ŌĆö LIFE-001's `composeClusterState` is NOT modified.
  2. Input shape is flat: 14 cluster-level fields, no DAG / no member walk. AN-003's threshold sweep runs at constant cost.
  3. `synthesis_ready` broadened to "concession-or-narrowing + no unresolved evidence debt". Coexists with LIFE-001's stricter semantics; consumers choose which one to display.
  4. Reads RULE-003's `LIFECYCLE_UX_MAP` for label + helperLine ŌĆö never authors copy.
  5. Adapter `buildExhaustionTimeoutInputFromLifecycle` ships in the same module so it shares thresholds.
  6. Priority order: `synthesis_ready > exhausted > ignored_by_both > ignored_by_<side> > moved_on_by_<side> > null`.
- **Doctrine encoded:** `blocksSubmit: false` and `appliesPointStandingPenalty: false` are compile-time-pinned literal-type fields. The deriver returns `null` (no advisory) when upstream state is `archived_or_resolved` / `conceded` / `narrowed` / `confirmed` / `rebutted` / `synthesis_ready` / `sourced` ŌĆö those upstream states already classify the cluster better than any advisory could. The deriver never authors a plain-language string ŌĆö every label + helperLine comes from RULE-003. The input shape contains no heat / popularity / engagement / amplification fields. Every produced helper line is scanned for "the user" / "the author" / "the poster" / "your opponent" / verb-form "Affirmative ignored" / "they ignored" patterns. The four shared thresholds inherit from `DEFAULT_LIFECYCLE_ADVISORY_CONFIG` so the two derivers agree out of the box.
- **Boundary enforcement:** Pure / total / deterministic ŌĆö no `Date.now()`, no `Math.random()`, no module-level mutable state. No import from `src/lib/constitution/engine` (sacred ŌĆö doctrine ┬¦5). No import from React / React Native / Expo / Supabase / Anthropic / xAI / fetch / XMLHttpRequest. No `process.env` read. No `console.*` call. No `submit-argument` / `validation/` import.
- **No xAI, Anthropic, or X API calls; no Supabase writes; no service-role; no migration; no Edge Function change; no new dependency; no `.env*` touched; no hosting file touched; no `pointLifecycleModel.ts` / `pointLifecycleAdvisoryInputs.ts` / `pointLifecycleClusters.ts` / `lifecycleUxMap.ts` / `moveMetadataLedger.ts` / `point-standing/*` source touched. The constitution engine remains sacred.**
- **+103 tests / +1 suite** (3980 ŌåÆ 4083 passing baseline). The 19 pre-existing xAI / Anthropic / engagement-intel suite failures remain unrelated to this card and operator-gated by missing `.env.engagement-intelligence` in this worktree. Typecheck + lint clean. `skills:validate` clean.
- **No operator follow-up** ŌĆö pure local change. No deploy step. The deriver is NOT auto-wired into any rendered surface; SC-003 / ST-002 / AN-003 follow-up cards plumb it where they want it.

## RULE-002 ŌĆö Evidence symmetry between validation and visuals (Release 6.6 / Wave 3)

**Status:** Pure-TS UX adapter + ComposerValidationPanel chip render + ArgumentComposer wiring + 67 new doctrine-anchored tests landed. The constitution engine's `FlagCode` vocabulary (16 codes) and the Stage 6.2 / 6.4 advisory codes (7 codes) now map through a single source of truth into render-ready `ValidationActionUx` tuples ŌĆö `{ code, chipLabel, helperLine, suggestedMove, dockAction, presetKey }` ŌĆö that surface a one-click chip in the composer validation surface. Issue #33.

- **Why this card exists:** Stage 6.2 made the validation rails advisory (no more hard `OFF_TOPIC` / `PARENT_NONRESPONSIVE` blocks) but the warning rows in `ComposerValidationPanel` stayed plain text. A player who saw "Topic coverage is light." had no one-click way to fix it. RULE-002 routes every engine flag + Stage 6.2/6.4 advisory code into the existing ST-002 / SC-004 / COMPOSER-001 plumbing so the chip pre-seeds the composer with the right move shape.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/rulesUx/validationActionMap.ts` ŌĆö new pure-TS module. `ValidationActionCode` union (23 entries ŌĆö every `FLAG_CODES` value + the 7 Stage 6.2/6.4 advisory codes). `ValidationActionUx` interface. `VALIDATION_ACTION_MAP` frozen catalog. `ALL_VALIDATION_ACTION_CODES` frozen array. `getValidationAction(code)` (compile-time exhaustive reader). `mapValidationActionOrSuppress(code)` (defensive normalising reader ŌĆö returns `null` for unknown / `null` / `undefined` / `''`). `shouldRenderValidationActionChip(action)` (true iff at least one routing field is non-null ŌĆö codes with no clean repair return false here, suppressing the chip). `_forbiddenValidationActionTokens()` test-only export. NEVER value-imports `constitution/engine` (sacred ŌĆö doctrine ┬¦5); the cross-walk between `FLAG_CODES` and the union is enforced by a runtime test that iterates the engine's enum.
  - `src/features/arguments/ComposerValidationPanel.tsx` ŌĆö adds optional `onSuggestedMove?: (action: ValidationActionUx) => void` prop, co-located `ValidationActionChip` subcomponent, `chipFor(detail)` derivation. The chip renders **next to** (not in place of) every warning + blocking-error row when the engine flagCode resolves to a chip-emitting `ValidationActionUx`. Codes that suppress (e.g. `invalid_transition`, `civility_risk`, `missing_parent`) keep their engine warning text but render no chip. New `actionChip` / `actionChipText` styles; neutral surface (color is not the only signal ŌĆö accessibility-targets).
  - `src/features/arguments/ArgumentComposer.tsx` ŌĆö new `handleValidationAction` callback routes the chip press through the existing `quickActionToPreset(action.presetKey, parentType)` + `handleMovePatch(patch)` pipeline (COMPOSER-001 + EV-002). Adds NO new execution paths. The submit-button gate `canSubmit` is **unchanged** ŌĆö `evaluationResult?.allowPost ?? false` continues to drive it (doctrine ┬¦1).
  - `__tests__/validationActionMap.test.ts` ŌĆö 67 new tests covering catalog completeness (16 engine + 7 advisory = 23), field-shape & length caps (`chipLabel` Ōēż 32, `helperLine` Ōēż 80, `looksLikeInternalCode === false`), ban-list (verdict / amplification / person-attribution tokens), issue acceptance criteria (weak_topic ŌåÆ "Sharpen the topic link"; parent_nonresponsive ŌåÆ "Reconnect to parent"; evidence_required ŌåÆ "Attach a source"; source_chain ŌåÆ "Ask for the source"), submit-gate additivity, normalisation parity (uppercase / hyphen / whitespace / `null` / `undefined`), RULE-001 coordination (shared labels match verbatim across the two maps), render contract (chip-emitting vs suppressed codes), code-shape hygiene, doctrine self-check (engine module never value-imported; no `fetch` / Supabase / Anthropic / xAI literal in source).
- **Resolved design questions (designer-confirmed):**
  1. Chip renders in `ComposerValidationPanel`, NOT the SC-004 timeline dock.
  2. No new engine flag codes ŌĆö the adapter reads existing engine output only. Engine stays sacred.
  3. `parent_nonresponsive` routes to `branch_tangent` `suggestedMove` + `clarify` `dockAction` + `clarify` `presetKey` (ST-002 `preset_gap` pattern; ST-002 has no clarify-shaped `SuggestedMoveCode` in v1).
  4. Codes with no clean repair (`invalid_transition`, `civility_risk`, `missing_parent`, `ad_hominem_possible`, `duplicate_argument_possible`, `excessive_length`, `unclear_claim`, `needs_moderator_review`, `validation_failed_after_retries`) ŌåÆ all-null UX. Chip suppressed; engine warning still renders.
  5. The doctrine-canonical phrase "Popularity is not proof" survives ŌĆö the `_forbiddenValidationActionTokens()` ban-list scans `\\bpopular\\b` (standalone token), not the noun `popularity`. The `anti_amplification` helper line avoids the standalone `engagement` token by using "Reach does not equal support" instead.
- **Doctrine encoded:** Every produced string passes verdict / amplification / person-attribution ban-list scans (test ┬¦3). `looksLikeInternalCode` returns `false` for every chipLabel + helperLine (no `off_topic`-shape internal code leaks). The doctrine-self-check test reads the validationActionMap source file and asserts: no `fetch(`, no Supabase / Anthropic / xAI import, no `process.env.*API_KEY` literal, no React / `useState` / `async` / `await`, no value-import of `constitution/engine`. Score never gates posting (┬¦1) ŌĆö pinned by a "Ordinary replies remain postable" acceptance test that mounts a synthetic `EvaluationResult { allowPost: true, warnings: [weak_topic_satisfaction] }` and verifies `allowPost` stays `true` after the chip lookup. Popularity is not evidence (┬¦3) ŌĆö `anti_amplification` and `platform_support_warning` chips route to `ask_source` / "Hold off on scoring", never to "accept because popular".
- **Boundary enforcement:** `validationActionMap.ts` is pure constants + two readers + one boolean helper. No mutable state. No `Date.now()` / `Math.random()` / `fetch` / `anthropic` / `xai`. `ComposerValidationPanel.tsx` source-scan is clean. `ArgumentComposer.tsx` adds one new `useCallback` that delegates entirely to existing functions; no new state, no new effect, no Supabase / fetch.
- **No xAI, Anthropic, or X API calls; no Supabase writes; no service-role; no migration; no Edge Function change; no new dependency; no `.env*` touched; no hosting file touched; no `src/domain/constitution/*` file touched (engine sacred ŌĆö doctrine ┬¦5); no `pointLifecycleModel.ts` / `moveMetadataLedger.ts` / `lifecycleUxMap.ts` / `ruleToUiMap.ts` / `timelineNodeActionDockModel.ts` / `suggestedMovesModel.ts` / `quickActionPresets.ts` source touched (RULE-002 reads their types and frozen exports only).**
- **+67 tests / +1 suite** (3913 ŌåÆ 3980 passing baseline). The 19 pre-existing xAI / Anthropic / engagement-intel suite failures remain unrelated to this card and operator-gated by missing `.env.engagement-intelligence`. Typecheck + lint clean.
- **No operator follow-up** ŌĆö pure local change. No deploy step.

## GAL-001 ŌĆö Upgrade gallery sections into scrum-like play lanes (Release 6.6 / Wave 4)

**Status:** Pure-TS model + screen wiring + 148 new doctrine-anchored tests landed. The Conversation Gallery's section grouping is now a 10-lane "scrum board": each lane invites a specific kind of next move. Issue #30.

- **Why this card exists:** Stage 6.4 shipped a 6-section catalogue (`jump_in` / `needs_rebuttal` / `source_trail` / `hot_unresolved` / `easy_first_move` / `my_rooms`) but the lanes blurred together ŌĆö `hot_unresolved` mixed active live disputes with stuck deep chains, and the catalogue did not surface evidence / definition / synthesis / branch-pressure as their own lanes. GAL-001 expands the catalogue to 10 lanes matching the kind of move a user wants to make, makes lane derivation deterministic (lifecycle > bucket > heat priority chain), and replaces the bucket chip row with a lane chip filter row.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/arguments/gameCopy.ts` ŌĆö replaces `GALLERY_SECTIONS` (6 entries) with `GALLERY_SECTION_DEFINITIONS` (10 frozen entries, each carrying `label` Ōēż 64 chars / Ōēż 8 tokens, `helperLine` Ōēż 80 chars, `emptyCopy` Ōēż 120 chars). Adds `GallerySectionDefinition` interface. Keeps `GALLERY_SECTIONS` as a one-release alias so the existing `seamlessConversationEntry.test.ts` import keeps compiling.
  - `src/features/debates/conversationGalleryModel.ts` ŌĆö expands `ConversationGallerySection` union to 10 values: `my_rooms` / `needs_rebuttal` / `jump_in` / `source_trail` / `evidence_needed` / `definition_fights` / `logic_traps` / `tangents_branches` / `almost_synthesis` / `quiet_beginner_rooms`. Exports frozen `SECTION_ORDER`, re-exports `GALLERY_SECTION_DEFINITIONS`, and exports the previously-private `classifyCardToSection` so unit tests assert the priority chain directly. `GallerySectionGroup` gains a `helperLine` field. `classifyCardToSection` uses the documented 14-row priority chain (joined > no-rebuttal > 4 lifecycle priorities > 5 bucket priorities > overheated-heat fallback > 2 SW-002 entryOpportunity tie-breakers > quiet_beginner_rooms fallback).
  - `src/features/debates/ConversationGalleryScreen.tsx` ŌĆö replaces `BucketChip` with `LaneChip`: single-select chip row keyed by `ConversationGallerySection`. "All lanes" chip resets the filter; tapping the active lane chip toggles back to "all". Each chip carries `accessibilityRole="button"`, `accessibilityState.selected`, an `accessibilityHint` populated from the lane helperLine, and a `hitSlop` lifting the effective tap target to ~48px (>= 44 per accessibility-targets). New `LaneSectionHeader` renders the lane label + helperLine above the card list. In single-lane filter mode the screen renders only that lane's cards (paginated). In all-lanes mode it groups the paginated cards via `groupGalleryCardsBySection` so each non-empty lane gets a section heading. Style names `bucketRowInner` / `sortRowInner` renamed to `laneRowContent` / `sortRowContent` to avoid an incidental "winner" substring on the plain-language source scan.
  - `__tests__/seamlessConversationEntry.test.ts` ŌĆö updates the catalogue assertion to the 10-lane list. Rewrites the two affected routing assertions (`hot_now` ŌåÆ `jump_in`, `pedantic_plain + cold` ŌåÆ `quiet_beginner_rooms`). Adds 3 new routing assertions for `evidence_needed` / `definition_fights` / `almost_synthesis`.
  - `__tests__/galleryLaneDerivation.test.ts` ŌĆö 63 new tests covering every row of the priority chain, cross-priority interactions (joined > lifecycle > bucket > heat), `groupGalleryCardsBySection` ordering / elision / one-card-one-lane invariants, `SECTION_ORDER` totality with an exhaustive-switch compile-time guard, back-compat assertions for the surviving Stage 6.4 routing rows + the documented `hot_unresolved` split, and purity / determinism (deep-equality on repeated calls, input not mutated, undefined-vs-null parity).
  - `__tests__/gallerySectionCopy.test.ts` ŌĆö 29 new tests covering completeness (10 entries, one per union member, order matches SECTION_ORDER), length budgets, doctrine ban-list (verdict / popularity / person-attribution tokens forbidden; word-boundary scanning avoids false positives on routine English; `right` / `wrong` intentionally not banned because they are plain-language English with no verdict semantics in this catalogue), plain-language guard (no snake_case / no raw lane id leaks), heat-as-activity doctrine, accessibility metadata sanity, frozen-structure invariants.
  - `__tests__/galleryLaneFilter.test.tsx` ŌĆö 56 new source-scan + contract tests following the existing `argumentReplySidecar.test.tsx` pattern. Asserts: lane chip row present with `lane-chip-` testID prefix; bucket chip row removed (no `bucket-chip-` testIDs, no `BUCKET_DEFINITIONS` reference, no `activeBucket` state); single-select state with chip toggle-back behaviour; accessibility metadata complete (role / state / hint / hitSlop); lane section rendering uses `groupGalleryCardsBySection` in all-lanes mode and `classifyCardToSection` in single-lane mode; observer-default entry preserved (GAL-002 / Stage 6.4 contract intact); no AI / Supabase / network imports; plain-language guard ban-list clean.
- **Behaviour change (documented):** the Stage 6.4 `hot_unresolved` lane is **retired**. Cards previously routed there now split: `hot_now` bucket and `overheated` heatLevel route to `jump_in`; `unresolved_deep_chain` bucket routes to `logic_traps`. The Stage 6.4 `easy_first_move` lane is **renamed** to `quiet_beginner_rooms`; classification rule unchanged. No production runtime code reads the retired strings ŌĆö only tests + docs, all migrated.
- **Resolved design questions (operator-confirmed):**
  1. Bucket chip row vs lane chip row ŌĆö the bucket-only chip filter is REMOVED. Lanes replace it. Buckets stay as internal classification on `ConversationGalleryCard.bucket` and feed lane derivation but are not user-selectable on the gallery UI.
  2. `SECTION_ORDER` placement of `my_rooms` ŌĆö `my_rooms` is FIRST.
  3. `hot_unresolved` removal ŌĆö ACCEPTED. Cards split between `jump_in` and `logic_traps` per the priority chain.
  4. Lane derivation file split ŌĆö left in `conversationGalleryModel.ts` (file size ~1500 lines, well under any practical threshold and the lane logic is small + tightly coupled to the existing dedupe + sort helpers).
- **Doctrine encoded:** No verdict / popularity / person-attribution tokens in any authored string (verified by `gallerySectionCopy.test.ts` ban-list scan). Heat framed as activity / friction (`jump_in` helper: "Active back-and-forth ŌĆö a fresh move lands cleanly."), never popularity / correctness. `logic_traps` describes move structure ("Same-axis pressure has repeated without new information."), not a verdict. `almost_synthesis` describes structural convergence, not correctness. Lane derivation reads only structural / activity / lifecycle descriptors ŌĆö never popularity / engagement / virality / view counts / follower counts (doctrine ┬¦3).
- **Boundary enforcement:** `conversationGalleryModel.ts` lane derivation is pure / total / deterministic ŌĆö no `Date.now` / `Math.random` / `fetch` / `anthropic` / `xai`. `ConversationGalleryScreen.tsx` source-scan refuses Supabase client, Anthropic SDK, xAI, raw fetch, XMLHttpRequest, `Date.now`, `Math.random`, `console.log`, `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`, `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` literals.
- **No xAI, Anthropic, or X API calls; no Supabase writes; no service-role; no migration; no Edge Function change; no new dependency; no `.env*` touched; no hosting file touched; no `pointLifecycleModel.ts` / `moveMetadataLedger.ts` / `lifecycleUxMap.ts` / `timelineNodeActionDockModel.ts` / `TimelineNodeActionDock.tsx` / `ArgumentReplySidecar*` / `ArgumentComposer.tsx` / `suggestedMovesModel.ts` / `heatModel.ts` / `src/lib/constitution/*` touched. `GalleryEntryHint` / `deriveGalleryEntryHint` (GAL-002) untouched.**
- **+151 tests / +3 suites** (3762 ŌåÆ 3913 passing baseline). The 19 pre-existing xAI / Anthropic / engagement-intel suite failures remain unrelated to this card and operator-gated. Typecheck + lint clean. `skills:validate` clean.
- **No operator follow-up** ŌĆö pure local change. No deploy step. The gallery loader does not yet populate `rootClusterLifecycleState` / `entryOpportunity` on every card; the lifecycle priorities fall through cleanly to the bucket path until a future loader card plumbs those fields (no regression vs. Stage 6.4 behaviour).

## SW-002 ŌĆö Heat, momentum, trend without truth claims (Release 6.6 / Wave 2)

**Status:** Pure-TS deriver + 79 doctrine-anchored tests landed. Activity-model layer that future Gallery + mini-map cards (GAL-001 / GAL-002 / IX-002) consume read-only. No UI in this card.

- **Why this card exists:** Downstream UI cards needed a doctrine-clean activity model ŌĆö `HeatLevel` / `MomentumState` / `TrendDirection` ŌĆö that describes "what is going on" in a room without sliding into engagement, popularity, or truth claims. Doctrine ┬¦2: heat = activity / friction, never correctness. The card delivers the typed unions + the deriver + the helper-line lookup + the ban-list helper. Issue #19.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/strengthWeakness/heatModel.ts` ŌĆö pure TS. No React, no Supabase, no network, no AI, no `Date.now()`, no `Math.random()`. Exports the three locked 3-valued unions (`HeatLevel = 'quiet' | 'active' | 'hot'`, `MomentumState = 'cooling' | 'steady' | 'building'`, `TrendDirection = 'unresolved_open' | 'narrowing_toward_synthesis' | 'branch_proliferating'`), the 8-value `ActivityChip['kind']` set (`recent_post` / `open_source_request` / `repeated_axis_pressure` / `no_rebuttal` / `synthesis_ready` / `branch_tangent` / `evidence_debt_open` / `cool_room_easy_entry`), `EntryOpportunity` (3 values), `RoomActivityProfile`, `HeatInputBundle`, `ActivityThresholds`, the LOCKED `DEFAULT_ACTIVITY_THRESHOLDS` (1 / 6 / 3 / 1.5 / 0.5 / 4), the `ACTIVITY_HELPER_LINES` lookup (5 of 8 entries read RULE-003 helper lines verbatim; 2 NEW lines pass the ban-list), `deriveRoomActivityProfile(input)`, `deriveRoomActivityChips(input)`, and `_forbiddenActivityTokens()`. Caller injects `clockMs`; the deriver never reads the system clock.
  - `src/features/strengthWeakness/index.ts` ŌĆö public-surface barrel re-export.
  - `__tests__/heatModel.test.ts` ŌĆö 79 tests covering vocabulary reach (5), cool-room default + null handling (5), determinism + idempotency (3), heat / momentum / trend reach (9), the 8 chip kinds (8), entry opportunity reach (4), hot + no_rebuttal coexistence (1), threshold normalization + defensive swap (5), single-root + sparse-tree cases (2), doctrine ban-list scan with the `hot` carve-out pinned inline to cdiscourse-doctrine ┬¦2 + COPY-001 ┬¦5.1 + ┬¦8 (8), RULE-003 read-through invariants (5), locked v1 thresholds + freeze (3), profile freeze + JSON round-trip (3), forbidden-imports source scan (14), and cross-module type-only import scan (4). Two clock values exercise the recent-window slicing path.
- **Doctrine encoded:** `hot` is an activity descriptor; the carve-out is documented in three places (`HeatLevel` JSDoc, `_forbiddenActivityTokens` JSDoc, explicit test with inline doctrine pin). All verdict-adjacent tokens (`winning / losing / dominant / losing ground / gaining ground / proven / disproven / verdict / validated / correct / incorrect / right / wrong / true / false`) ban-listed. Person-attribution tokens (`you / your / they / their / the user / the author / the poster / the participant`) ban-listed. Amplification tokens (`likes / shares / followers / trending / popular / viral / engagement / amplification / virality / views / verified / retweets`) ban-listed. Side-stratified heat is OUT OF SCOPE for v1 (no per-side scores). No scoring read (`standingBand` never consumed). The model is room-level only. The deriver is total ŌĆö null inputs ŌåÆ cool-room default; never throws.
- **Boundary enforcement:** cross-module imports of LIFE-001 / META-001 / `argumentGameSurfaceModel` are `import type` only (4 source-scan tests pin this). The single runtime-value import is RULE-003's `lifecycleUxMap` for helper-line text ŌĆö documented in the file header. Forbidden-imports scan refuses `buildPointLifecycleMap` / `buildMoveMetadataLedger` / `deriveAutoMetadataForMessage` / `gradeChallenge` / `gradeRepair` / `applyAntiAmplification` / `Date.now` / `Math.random` / `supabase` / `fetch` / `anthropic` / `xai` / `console.log` / `XMLHttpRequest` / secret literals in executable code (comments + string literals stripped before scan).

## ST-002 ŌĆö Suggested reply flags per bubble card (Release 6.6 / Wave 2)

**Status:** Pure-TS deriver + SC-003 stub widening + 74 tests landed. The sidecar's `SuggestedNextMove` slot is now structurally population-ready; SC-003's builder behaviour is unchanged (still emits `suggestion: null` + `reason: 'st_002_not_yet_implemented'`). The render-side chip + integrator wiring are future cards.

- **Why this card exists:** SC-003 reserved a typed `SuggestedMoveStub = never` slot on the sidecar view-model so a future card could widen it to a real `SuggestedNextMove` union. ST-002 fills that slot with a pure-TS deriver that turns lifecycle (LIFE-001) + manual tag + auto-metadata (META-001) + evidence source-chain (EV-001) state into a small, ordered list of advisory suggested moves. Each suggestion carries a plain-language rationale assembled from RULE-003 helper lines (never freshly authored), an existing `QuickActionLabel` preset key, an optional SC-004 dock action, and a structural `sourceSignals[]` record for AN-003 diagnostics. Issue #13.
- **Deliverables (all in this card):**
  - `src/features/arguments/suggestedMovesModel.ts` ŌĆö pure TS. No React, no Supabase, no network, no AI. Exports `SuggestedMoveCode` (9-value union: `ask_source` / `ask_quote` / `narrow` / `concede` / `confirm` / `challenge_mechanism` / `challenge_scope` / `branch_tangent` / `synthesize`), `SuggestionSignal` (discriminated union covering source-chain / lifecycle / manual-tag / auto-metadata / 4 narrow signal kinds / `preset_gap`), `SuggestedMove` (`code` + `label` Ōēż 24 chars + `rationale` Ōēż 80 chars + `presetKey` + `dockAction` + `sourceSignals`), `SuggestionDerivationInput` (lifecycle / metadata / move-linkage / source-chain status / standing / depth / branch / tangent / `maxSuggestions`), `SuggestedNextMove = SuggestedMove`, plus `deriveSuggestedMoves(input)` (pure, total, deterministic; default `maxSuggestions = 3`), `buildRationale(signals)`, `_forbiddenSuggestionTokens()`. The three documented gap codes (`challenge_mechanism` ŌåÆ `challenge`, `challenge_scope` ŌåÆ `narrow`, `branch_tangent` ŌåÆ `branch`) route to existing presets and emit a `preset_gap` signal so AN-003 / PRESET-001 can track them.
  - `src/features/arguments/argumentReplySidecarModel.ts` ŌĆö type-level widening only: `SuggestedMoveStub` changes from `never` to `SuggestedMove` (one new `import type`, one type alias change). No behaviour change in `buildSidecarViewModel(...)`. The SC-003 happy-path tests that pin `suggestion === null` continue to pass; the runtime tautology test that pins `SuggestedMoveStub | null` accepting `null` also continues to pass because the widening is purely additive.
  - `__tests__/suggestedMovesModel.test.ts` ŌĆö 66 tests covering empty / null inputs (5), parameterized lifecycle-state primary coverage across all 19 `PointLifecycleState` values, parameterized manual-tag override across all 9 promotable tags + 1 deferred (`definition_issue`), parameterized auto-metadata refinement (6 promotions), parameterized source-chain override (4 statuses that fire + 2 that do not), preset mapping invariant (every `presetKey` is a member of `QuickActionLabel`), dock-action mapping invariant, exhaustive rationale ban-list scan (every signal kind ├Ś every code) against `_forbiddenSuggestionTokens()`, person-attribution scan against the COPY-001 token list (`you / your / they / their / the user / the author / the poster / the speaker / the participant / this person / this user`), snake_case scan on rationale + label, cap enforcement (rationale Ōēż 80 / label Ōēż 24 / array length Ōēż `maxSuggestions`), gap-code routing (`challenge_mechanism` / `challenge_scope` / `branch_tangent` each pin their preset + dock + `preset_gap` signal), no-forced-gate contract (empty array is a valid output; no `onPress|onAction|dispatch|callback|handler` field name), determinism (deep-equality + stable signal order), standing-band ignored doctrine check, source-scan for engagement / amplification identifier reads (comment-stripped), forbidden-imports scan (`buildPointLifecycleMap` / `deriveAutoMetadataForMessage` / `gradeChallenge` / `gradeRepair` / `applyAntiAmplification` / `supabase` / `fetch` / `anthropic` / `xai` / `ArgumentComposer` / `react` / `react-native`), `ALL_SUGGESTED_MOVE_CODES` reachability coverage, and `SuggestedNextMove` type re-export round-trip.

- **Doctrine encoded:** Suggestions describe move shape ŌĆö never the author (zero `you / your / they / their / the user / the author / the poster / the speaker / the participant / this person / this user` token in any rationale). Score never blocks posting ŌĆö empty suggestion array is a valid output. No popularity / engagement / heat / virality input is consumed (source-scan enforces no identifier read of `engagement / amplification / likes / shares / followers / trending / viral`). No new presets ŌĆö every `presetKey` is a pre-existing `QuickActionLabel`. No live AI ŌĆö pure deterministic TS, same inputs ŌåÆ same outputs. The dock owns execution; ST-002 produces data only (no `onPress` / `onAction` / `dispatch` / `callback` / `handler` field). Rationale text comes from the RULE-003 helper-line vocabulary or is derived from existing plain-language phrases; nothing is freshly authored per call. `definition_issue` manual tag is documented as deferred (no `clarify`-shaped `SuggestedMoveCode` in v1).

Audit ┬¦5.1 + ┬¦8 record the carve-out.

Audit found zero drifts; the hardening is purely additive ŌĆö it catches future drift without forcing any current label rewrite or snapshot update. The 5 render-rules (R1 scope-strict positioning, R2 same-label dedup, R3 provenance suffix on cross-level reuse, R4 runner-status suppression in normal-user surfaces, R5 axis-vs-manual-tag dedup) are owned by consumer cards (SC-004 already implements R1+R2; ST-002 and RULE-003 are pending consumers).

## HOST-005 ŌĆö Secret Manager migration + Cloud Run secret binding (Release 6.8 / hosting prep)

**Status:** Implementation complete on `feat/HOST-005-secret-manager-migration-and-cloud-run-s`. **No GCP mutation has been executed by the agent.** Operator runs every `gcloud secrets create` / `versions add` / `add-iam-policy-binding` command themselves per the new runbook.

**Headline:** Two-secret manifest + JSON Schema + two operator helper scripts (`print-secret-commands` and `preflight-secrets`) + 9-step runbook + a HOST-001 runbook step-13 patch. **+106 new tests across 3 new files. Typecheck + lint clean.**

**Files (high level):**

- `infra/secrets/cdiscourse-dev-manifest.json` ŌĆö names-only manifest. Two entries: `cdiscourse-dev-supabase-url` -> `EXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL`; `cdiscourse-dev-supabase-publishable-key` -> `EXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY`. Cross-checks against `infra/cloud-run/cdiscourse-dev.template.yaml` `secretKeyRef.name` entries and against `infra/iam/cdiscourse-dev-runner.iam.yaml` resource-scoped bindings ŌĆö a test fails if either drifts.
- `infra/secrets/manifest.schema.json` ŌĆö draft-07 JSON Schema. Enforces `^EXPO_PUBLIC_[A-Z0-9_]+$` on every `cloudRunEnvVar` and `^cdiscourse-(dev|prod)-[a-z0-9-]+$` on every `name`. Schema permits prod manifests but HOST-005 ships only the dev one.
- `scripts/deploy/print-secret-commands.{mjs,ps1,sh}` ŌĆö emits operator-runnable `gcloud secrets create` / `versions add --data-file=-` / `add-iam-policy-binding` shapes from the manifest. **Never accepts a value as input, never reads `.env*`, never runs `gcloud`.** Refuses forbidden names (service-role / Anthropic / xAI / X bearer / Resend / `*-api-key` / `*-secret-key`) with exit 3 and value-shaped literals (JWT, `sk-ant-`, `xai-`, `sb_secret_`, `sb_publishable_`, Bearer prefix, `.supabase.co` URL) with exit 4. Stdout only.
- `scripts/deploy/preflight-secrets.{mjs,ps1,sh}` ŌĆö verifies every manifest secret exists with state=ENABLED + has the runtime SA's `secretAccessor` binding. **Only invokes `gcloud --version`, `gcloud config get-value project`, `gcloud secrets describe`, `gcloud secrets versions list`, `gcloud secrets get-iam-policy`.** **NEVER calls `gcloud secrets versions access`.** Source-scan test enforces this absence. `--strict-project` flag (default off for humans, on for HOST-004) refuses if `gcloud config get-value project` mismatches `manifest.project`.
- `docs/deployment/host-005-secrets-runbook.md` ŌĆö 9 numbered operator-runnable steps (authenticate, project + region, enable API, generate command list, create each secret, add the first version via stdin + clear history/clipboard, bind runtime SA, run preflight, hand off back to HOST-001 Phase 4). Every section carries an explicit "Agent does NOT run" marker; rollback guidance per step.
- `__tests__/fixtures/host-005-gcloud-stub.mjs` ŌĆö gcloud stub that the preflight test suite spawns via `--gcloud-bin=<path>` (test-only injection; preflight detects `.mjs`/`.js` suffix and invokes via `process.execPath`). Driven by `HOST_005_STUB_PROJECT` / `_MISSING` / `_NO_ENABLED` / `_NO_IAM` / `_VERSION_EXIT` env vars.
- **HOST-001 patch:** `docs/deployment/host-001-operator-runbook.md` Phase 3 step 13 ŌĆö body updated to link to `host-005-secrets-runbook.md` + both helper scripts. The previous `printf %s "<VALUE>" | gcloud ...` shape is replaced with the `--data-file=-` stdin path so the value is never argv-literal.

**Locked decisions held (subset of HOST-001's D1-D11):**

- D1 project `cdiscourse-host`, D2 region `us-central1`.
- D8 operator runs every `gcloud secrets create` / `gcloud secrets versions add` themselves; agent never executes any `gcloud` command (helpers print or verify, never apply).
- D10 reuse existing dev Supabase project; manifest names target the existing project. Two secrets at v0.
- D11 `.env*` history audit skipped; ┬¦7.5 rotation criteria are the going-forward policy. The runbook restates ┬¦7.5 verbatim under "Rotation procedure (┬¦7.5 reminder)".

**Cross-card contract:**

- HOST-004 (deploy scripts) will read `infra/secrets/cdiscourse-dev-manifest.json` to assemble `--set-secrets=EXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL=cdiscourse-dev-supabase-url:latest,EXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY=cdiscourse-dev-supabase-publishable-key:latest`. HOST-004 must run `node scripts/deploy/preflight-secrets.mjs --manifest=infra/secrets/cdiscourse-dev-manifest.json --strict-project` before every `gcloud run deploy ...`.
- HOST-008 (prod) inherits the manifest shape under `cdiscourse-prod-manifest.json`. The schema already permits `environment: "prod"` and `name` pattern `cdiscourse-prod-*`. Helpers are environment-agnostic ŌĆö they read whatever manifest is passed via `--manifest=`.

**Doctrine self-check (re-walked):**

1. Score is gameplay analysis, never truth ŌĆö no scoring copy added. PASS.
2. Heat != truth ŌĆö no heat copy. PASS.
3. Popularity is not evidence ŌĆö no engagement copy. PASS.
4. AI moderator hard limits ŌĆö no AI surface touched. PASS.

10. v1 scope guards ŌĆö no voting, no collaborative editing, no OAuth, no public API, no push, no search. PASS.

**Operator action items (when ready to deploy):**

**Detailed file-by-file (for reviewer):**

- New `Dockerfile` at repo root: Node 22 alpine builder ŌåÆ `gcr.io/distroless/nodejs22-debian12:nonroot` runtime stage, `EXPOSE 8080`, `USER nonroot`, `CMD ["server.mjs"]`. Locked build args: `BUILD_COMMIT_SHA`, `BUILD_VERSION`, `BUILD_TIMESTAMP`, `EXPO_PUBLIC_DEPLOY_ENV`, `EXPO_PUBLIC_APP_URL`, `EXPO_PUBLIC_REPORT_ISSUE_URL`. The bundle's dev-banner identity (`EXPO_PUBLIC_COMMIT_HASH` etc.) IS baked. The Supabase URL + publishable key are NOT baked ŌĆö they arrive at container start via Cloud Run `--set-secrets=` and the runtime entrypoint writes them into `dist/runtime-env.js` for the SPA bootstrap. This is what makes HOST-008's digest-only promotion correct.
- New `.dockerignore` excludes `node_modules`, `.git`, `.env*` (except the three committed `*.example` files), `logs/`, `.expo`, `__tests__`, `docs/`, `.claude/`, `coverage/`, `artifacts/`, `data/engagement-intelligence/`, native build outputs, and any `*.json` matching the GCP service-account-key path patterns (defence in depth ŌĆö no key file should ever exist in the repo).
- New `scripts/build/build-web.{mjs,ps1,sh}` triplet wraps `expo export --platform web`. Defaults output to `dist/`; refuses paths that escape the repo root; supports `--dry` plan-only mode; never reads `.env*` files; never calls Anthropic / xAI / X / Supabase.
- New `scripts/build/inject-runtime-env.{mjs,ps1,sh}` triplet writes `dist/runtime-env.js`. Reads `EXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL` + `EXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY` from `process.env` only (Cloud Run injects them from Secret Manager) OR from explicit `--url=` / `--publishable-key=` flags. Refuses on (a) missing values (exit 4), (b) forbidden secret shapes ŌĆö `sk` + `-ant-` Anthropic, `xai` + `-` xAI, `sb` + `_secret` + `_` Supabase service-role, `Bearer` token shape, literal `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` / `service_role` strings (exit 5), (c) URL not https-shaped (exit 6), (d) publishable key not in `sb_publishable_` or JWT (`eyJ...`) shape (exit 7), (e) `dist/` missing (exit 8). Values are never echoed; logs report only `loaded N/2 (url=present|missing, publishable-key=present|missing)`.
- New `scripts/runtime/server.mjs` is the Cloud Run container entrypoint. Single-process Node script that (1) runs the same env preflight as the inject script (refuses on the same forbidden shapes), (2) writes `dist/runtime-env.js`, (3) spawns the vendored `serve@14.2.6` CLI with `-s` SPA fallback on `$PORT` (default 8080), `--no-clipboard --no-port-switching` for deterministic boot, (4) forwards `SIGTERM`/`SIGINT` to the child for graceful Cloud Run shutdown.
- New `infra/cloud-run/cdiscourse-dev.template.yaml` Cloud Run service spec template. Locked flags: name `cdiscourse-dev`, namespace `cdiscourse-host`, region `us-central1` (in the deploy command), ingress `all`, runtime service account is the `cdiscourse-dev-runner` identity in project `cdiscourse-host`, `gen2` execution environment, `minScale=0` / `maxScale=4`, `cpu=1` / `memory=512Mi` / `containerConcurrency=80` / `timeoutSeconds=60`, image at `us-central1-docker.pkg.dev/cdiscourse-host/cdiscourse-web/cdiscourse-web:dev-<COMMIT_SHA_7>`. Binds exactly the two allowed Secret Manager secrets (`cdiscourse-dev-supabase-url:latest`, `cdiscourse-dev-supabase-publishable-key:latest`). Startup probe is TCP on 8080 (no `/healthz` route inside `serve`; HOST-003a follow-up will add one). Operator substitutes `<COMMIT_SHA_7>` and `<REVISION_SUFFIX>` and applies via `gcloud run services replace`.
- New `infra/iam/cdiscourse-dev-runner.iam.yaml` runtime SA template. Minimum project-wide roles: `roles/logging.logWriter`, `roles/monitoring.metricWriter`. Resource-scoped roles only: `roles/secretmanager.secretAccessor` per-secret (not project-wide), `roles/artifactregistry.reader` on the `cdiscourse-web` repo. Forbidden roles enumerated: owner, editor, `iam.security/serviceAccountAdmin`, `iam.serviceAccountKeyAdmin`, `iam.serviceAccountTokenCreator`, `secretmanager.admin`, `run.admin`, `artifactregistry.admin`, `artifactregistry.writer`. The file includes the operator-runnable `gcloud` commands at the bottom ŌĆö agent never runs them.
- New `infra/iam/cdiscourse-deployer.iam.yaml` deployer SA template. Project-wide roles: `roles/run.admin`, `roles/logging.viewer`. Resource-scoped: `roles/iam.serviceAccountUser` on the runtime SA (the deployer can pass the runtime SA on deploys), `roles/artifactregistry.writer` on the `cdiscourse-web` repo. Operator impersonation grant uses the `<OPERATOR_EMAIL>` placeholder. Forbidden roles: owner, editor, admin chains, any `secretmanager.*` role.
- New `docs/deployment/host-001-operator-runbook.md` ŌĆö 23 numbered operator-runnable steps across project setup ŌåÆ identity ŌåÆ Artifact Registry ŌåÆ Secret Manager handoff (HOST-005) ŌåÆ image build + push ŌåÆ deploy ŌåÆ H1+H2 smoke ŌåÆ handoff. Every command operator-runnable; explicit "Agent does NOT run" markers; references master plan ┬¦11 and `infra/iam/*.iam.yaml` + `infra/cloud-run/cdiscourse-dev.template.yaml`.
- **HOST-001b folded in.** `src/lib/supabase.ts` now exports `readRuntimeEnv()` and resolves `EXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL` + `EXPO_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY` from `window.__CDISCOURSE_RUNTIME_ENV__` first (web Cloud Run path) and falls back to `process.env` (native + local dev). Guards `typeof window === 'undefined'` so native + SSR + Jest stay safe. No behaviour change in any code path that already passed env vars via process.env. Issue #92 closes when this PR merges.
- **New dependency:** `serve@14.2.6` pinned to exact version (no `^` or `~`) under `dependencies` in `package.json`. The operator pre-approved this in the spawn-card decision lock. `package-lock.json` updated via `npm install --save-exact --legacy-peer-deps`. The image vendors `node_modules/serve` from the builder stage ŌĆö `npx serve` is NEVER used at container start.
- **New npm scripts:** `web:build` (runs `expo export --platform web --output-dir dist`), `web:build:dry` (delegates to `scripts/build/build-web.mjs --dry`).

## HOST ŌĆö Google Cloud Run hosting plan for cdiscourse.com (Release 6.8 / hosting prep)

**Status:** Plan written. Operator decisions LOCKED. No deploy executed.

- New doc [`docs/deployment/google-cloud-run-hosting-plan.md`](deployment/google-cloud-run-hosting-plan.md) is the master architecture plan for moving CDiscourse onto a real public dev / sandbox environment on Google Cloud Run, using the existing `cdiscourse.com` domain (GoDaddy) and the existing Supabase backend. 18 sections covering goal, current app assumptions, environment topology (local / dev / prod), recommended GCP architecture (Cloud Run + Artifact Registry + Secret Manager + service accounts), domain strategy (`dev.cdiscourse.com` recommended over `cdiscourse.com/dev` because Cloud Run domain mapping maps a domain to `/`, not a path), DNS strategy (Option A keep GoDaddy / Option B migrate to Cloud DNS ŌĆö recommendation A for v0), secret migration (inventory names only, history-leak audit, `gcloud secrets versions add --data-file=-` from stdin, never agent-run), Supabase integration (no schema change, redirect URLs + site URL config only), dev access control (Option A IAM + IAP / Option B Cloud Armor IP allowlist via HTTPS LB + serverless NEG ŌĆö recommendation A), deploy script plan (`scripts/deploy/gcloud-preflight.*` / `deploy-cloud-run-dev.*` / `promote-cloud-run-prod.*` stub; all dry-run default, refuse on dirty git, never echo secret values), manual operator steps, smoke plan (existing HOST-003 checklist + 2 new hosting checks H1 TLS / H2 revision-match), rollback (one `gcloud run services update-traffic` command), cost watchpoints, risks/decisions table, do-not-implement-in-this-card boundary, proposed issue changes, and next implementation sequence.
- Companion doc [`docs/deployment/claude-code-vertex-ai-note.md`](deployment/claude-code-vertex-ai-note.md) keeps the Claude Code Vertex AI routing setup explicitly separate from app hosting ŌĆö Vertex AI is the operator's local model-routing convenience, **not** part of `cdiscourse.com` infrastructure.
- HOST-001 (#27) is refreshed to point at the plan doc; HOST-002 (#28) and HOST-003 (#29) remain closed (banner + smoke checklist already shipped). Plan proposes splitting hosting work into HOST-001 (architecture design + first Cloud Run revision) plus new cards HOST-004 (deploy scripts + Artifact Registry), HOST-005 (Secret Manager migration + Cloud Run binding), HOST-006 (DNS strategy + GoDaddy record set), HOST-007 (dev access control ŌĆö IAM+IAP or Cloud Armor), HOST-008 (prod promotion pipeline stub). Each card has a distinct manual-operator gate and rollback surface.
- Hard rules held in writing:
  1. **No `.env*` value is ever read or printed by the agent.** Operator runs ┬¦7.1 inventory locally and shares only key names.
